import { useState, useRef, useEffect, useCallback, Fragment } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  Search,
  X,
  Hash,
  MessageSquare,
  User,
  ArrowUp,
  ArrowDown,
  CornerDownLeft,
  FileText,
  Lock,
  Megaphone,
  Loader2,
  Image as ImageIcon,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { useAuthUser } from '@/app/selectors';
import { setCurrentChannelId } from '@/features/channelSlice';
import { mockApi } from '@/lib/mockApi';
import type {
  Message,
  Channel,
  User as UserType,
  Attachment,
} from '@/data/mockData';
import { useGetWorkspaceUsers } from '@/hooks/users/useGetUsers';

// ─── Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

type FilterType = 'all' | 'messages' | 'channels' | 'people' | 'files';

interface SearchResult {
  type: 'message' | 'channel' | 'person' | 'file';
  id: string;
  message?: Message & { channelName?: string };
  channel?: Channel;
  person?: UserType;
  file?: { attachment: Attachment; message: Message; channelName?: string };
}

// ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
  online: 'bg-online',
  away: 'bg-away',
  dnd: 'bg-dnd',
  offline: 'bg-muted-foreground',
};

const formatTime = (ts: string) => {
  const d = new Date(ts);
  const now = new Date();
  const yesterday = new Date(now);
  yesterday.setDate(now.getDate() - 1);
  if (d.toDateString() === now.toDateString())
    return d.toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
      hour: 'numeric',
      minute: '2-digit',
    });
  if (d.toDateString() === yesterday.toDateString()) return 'Yesterday';
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' });
};

// ─── HighlightedText ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const HighlightedText = ({ text, query }: { text: string; query: string }) => {
  if (!query.trim()) return <>{text}</>;
  const parts = text.split(
    new RegExp(`(${query.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&')})`, 'gi'),
  );
  return (
    <>
      {parts.map((part, i) =>
        part.toLowerCase() === query.toLowerCase() ? (
          <mark
            key={i}
            className='bg-away/30 text-foreground rounded-sm px-0.5'
          >
            {part}
          </mark>
        ) : (
          part
        ),
      )}
    </>
  );
};

// ─── Filter config ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const FILTERS: { label: string; value: FilterType; icon: React.ElementType }[] =
  [
    { label: 'All', value: 'all', icon: Search },
    { label: 'Messages', value: 'messages', icon: MessageSquare },
    { label: 'Channels', value: 'channels', icon: Hash },
    { label: 'People', value: 'people', icon: User },
    { label: 'Files', value: 'files', icon: FileText },
  ];

// ─── SearchModal ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export const SearchModal = () => {
  // ── UI context ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const { searchOpen, setSearchOpen } = useUI();

  // ── Auth + Redux ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const authUser = useAuthUser();

  // ── Users cache (replaces getUser from WorkspaceContext) ──────────────────
  const { data: users = [] } = useGetWorkspaceUsers();
  const getUser = (id: string) => users.find((u) => u.id === id);

  // ── Search state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [query, setQuery] = useState('');
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState<FilterType>('all');
  const [selectedIdx, setSelectedIdx] = useState(0);
  const [recentSearches, setRecentSearches] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(false);
  const [results, setResults] = useState<SearchResult[]>([]);
  const [totalCount, setTotalCount] = useState(0);

  // ── Advanced filter state ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [channelFilter, setChannelFilter] = useState('');
  const [authorFilter, setAuthorFilter] = useState('');
  const [hasFiles, setHasFiles] = useState(false);
  const [hasLinks, setHasLinks] = useState(false);
  const [hasReactions, setHasReactions] = useState(false);

  // ── Refs ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const inputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
  const debounceRef = useRef<NodeJS.Timeout>();

  // ── Reset + focus on open ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!searchOpen) return;
    setQuery('');
    setSelectedIdx(0);
    setResults([]);
    setFilter('all');
    setChannelFilter('');
    setAuthorFilter('');
    setHasFiles(false);
    setHasLinks(false);
    setHasReactions(false);
    setTimeout(() => inputRef.current?.focus(), 50);
    if (authUser) {
      mockApi.search.getHistory(authUser.id).then(setRecentSearches);
    }
  }, [searchOpen, authUser]);

  // ── Search fn ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const doSearch = useCallback(
    async (q: string) => {
      if (!q.trim()) {
        setResults([]);
        setTotalCount(0);
        setLoading(false);
        return;
      }
      setLoading(true);
      try {
        const res = await mockApi.search.global(q, {
          type: filter === 'all' ? undefined : filter,
          channelId: channelFilter || undefined,
          authorId: authorFilter || undefined,
          hasFiles,
          hasLinks,
          hasReactions,
        });

        const items: SearchResult[] = [];
        if (filter === 'all' || filter === 'messages')
          res.messages.forEach((m) =>
            items.push({ type: 'message', id: m.id, message: m }),
          );
        if (filter === 'all' || filter === 'channels')
          res.channels.forEach((c) =>
            items.push({ type: 'channel', id: c.id, channel: c }),
          );
        if (filter === 'all' || filter === 'people')
          res.people.forEach((p) =>
            items.push({ type: 'person', id: p.id, person: p }),
          );
        if (filter === 'all' || filter === 'files')
          res.files.forEach((f) =>
            items.push({ type: 'file', id: f.attachment.id, file: f }),
          );

        setResults(items.slice(0, 30));
        setTotalCount(res.total);
        setSelectedIdx(0);

        if (authUser) mockApi.search.addToHistory(authUser.id, q);
      } catch {
        // silently fail — search errors shouldn't crash the modal
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    },
    [
      filter,
      channelFilter,
      authorFilter,
      hasFiles,
      hasLinks,
      hasReactions,
      authUser,
    ],
  );

  // ── Debounced search trigger ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    clearTimeout(debounceRef.current);
    if (!query.trim()) {
      setResults([]);
      setLoading(false);
      return;
    }
    setLoading(true);
    debounceRef.current = setTimeout(() => doSearch(query), 250);
    return () => clearTimeout(debounceRef.current);
  }, [query, doSearch]);

  // ── Select result ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleSelect = (item: SearchResult) => {
    if (item.type === 'channel' && item.channel) {
      dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(item.channel.id));
    }
    if (item.type === 'message' && item.message?.channelId) {
      dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(item.message.channelId));
      setTimeout(() => {
        const el = document.querySelector(
          `[data-message-id="${item.message!.id}"]`,
        );
        if (el) {
          el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
          el.classList.add('animate-highlight');
          setTimeout(() => el.classList.remove('animate-highlight'), 2500);
        }
      }, 200);
    }
    setRecentSearches((prev) =>
      [query, ...prev.filter((s) => s !== query)].slice(0, 10),
    );
    setSearchOpen(false);
  };

  // ── Keyboard navigation ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    switch (e.key) {
      case 'ArrowDown':
        e.preventDefault();
        setSelectedIdx((i) => Math.min(i + 1, results.length - 1));
        break;
      case 'ArrowUp':
        e.preventDefault();
        setSelectedIdx((i) => Math.max(i - 1, 0));
        break;
      case 'Enter':
        if (results[selectedIdx]) handleSelect(results[selectedIdx]);
        break;
      case 'Escape':
        setSearchOpen(false);
        break;
      case 'Tab': {
        e.preventDefault();
        const tabs: FilterType[] = [
          'all',
          'messages',
          'channels',
          'people',
          'files',
        ];
        setFilter(tabs[(tabs.indexOf(filter) + 1) % tabs.length]);
        break;
      }
    }
  };

  const removeRecent = (s: string) => {
    setRecentSearches((prev) => prev.filter((x) => x !== s));
    if (authUser) mockApi.search.clearHistoryItem(authUser.id, s);
  };

  if (!searchOpen) return null;

  // ── Render ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
        exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
        className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50 flex items-start justify-center pt-[10vh]'
        onClick={() => setSearchOpen(false)}
      >
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -20, scale: 0.95 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0, scale: 1 }}
          exit={{ opacity: 0, y: -20 }}
          onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          className='w-full max-w-2xl bg-card border border-border rounded-xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden'
        >
          {/* ── Search input ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className='flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3 border-b border-border'>
            <Search className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0' />
            <input
              ref={inputRef}
              value={query}
              onChange={(e) => setQuery(e.target.value)}
              onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
              placeholder='Search Linkly...'
              className='flex-1 bg-transparent text-foreground text-sm focus:outline-none placeholder:text-muted-foreground'
            />
            {loading && (
              <Loader2 className='w-4 h-4 animate-spin text-muted-foreground' />
            )}
            <kbd className='text-xs text-muted-foreground bg-muted px-2 py-0.5 rounded'>
              ESC
            </kbd>
          </div>

          {/* ── Filter tabs ──────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className='flex items-center gap-1 px-4 py-2 border-b border-border overflow-x-auto'>
            {FILTERS.map(({ label, value, icon: Icon }) => (
              <button
                key={value}
                onClick={() => setFilter(value)}
                className={`flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium transition-colors whitespace-nowrap ${
                  filter === value
                    ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                    : 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
                }`}
              >
                <Icon className='w-3 h-3' /> {label}
              </button>
            ))}
            <div className='h-4 w-px bg-border mx-1' />
            {[
              {
                label: '📎 Files',
                active: hasFiles,
                toggle: () => setHasFiles((v) => !v),
              },
              {
                label: '🔗 Links',
                active: hasLinks,
                toggle: () => setHasLinks((v) => !v),
              },
              {
                label: '😄 Reactions',
                active: hasReactions,
                toggle: () => setHasReactions((v) => !v),
              },
            ].map((pill) => (
              <button
                key={pill.label}
                onClick={pill.toggle}
                className={`px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium transition-colors whitespace-nowrap ${
                  pill.active
                    ? 'bg-primary/20 text-primary border border-primary/30'
                    : 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
                }`}
              >
                {pill.label}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* ── Results ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className='max-h-[60vh] overflow-y-auto'>
            {/* Empty query — show recent searches */}
            {query.trim() === '' && (
              <div className='p-4'>
                {recentSearches.length > 0 ? (
                  <>
                    <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-2'>
                      Recent searches
                    </p>
                    {recentSearches.map((s, i) => (
                      <div key={i} className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                        <button
                          onClick={() => setQuery(s)}
                          className='flex-1 text-left px-3 py-2 rounded-md text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
                        >
                          <Search className='w-3.5 h-3.5 inline mr-2' />
                          {s}
                        </button>
                        <button
                          onClick={() => removeRecent(s)}
                          className='p-1 rounded hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
                        >
                          <X className='w-3 h-3' />
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </>
                ) : (
                  <div className='text-center py-8'>
                    <Search className='w-10 h-10 text-muted-foreground/30 mx-auto mb-3' />
                    <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                      Search messages, channels, people, and files
                    </p>
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1'>
                      Try searching for a person's name or a channel
                    </p>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Loading skeleton */}
            {query.trim() !== '' && loading && results.length === 0 && (
              <div className='p-4 space-y-3'>
                {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => (
                  <div
                    key={i}
                    className='flex gap-3 animate-shimmer rounded-md p-3'
                  >
                    <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-muted shrink-0' />
                    <div className='flex-1 space-y-2'>
                      <div className='h-3 bg-muted rounded w-32' />
                      <div className='h-3 bg-muted rounded w-3/4' />
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}

            {/* No results */}
            {query.trim() !== '' && !loading && results.length === 0 && (
              <div className='p-8 text-center'>
                <Search className='w-10 h-10 text-muted-foreground/30 mx-auto mb-3' />
                <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                  No results for "{query}"
                </p>
                <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1'>
                  Try a different search term or filter
                </p>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Results list */}
            {results.length > 0 && (
              <div className='py-1'>
                {totalCount > 0 && (
                  <p className='px-4 py-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                    {totalCount} result{totalCount !== 1 ? 's' : ''} for "
                    {query}"
                  </p>
                )}
                {results.map((item, idx) => (
                  <button
                    key={`${item.type}-${item.id}`}
                    onClick={() => handleSelect(item)}
                    className={`w-full text-left px-4 py-2.5 transition-colors ${
                      idx === selectedIdx
                        ? 'bg-primary/10 ring-1 ring-primary/20'
                        : 'hover:bg-accent/50'
                    }`}
                  >
                    {/* Message */}
                    {item.type === 'message' &&
                      item.message &&
                      (() => {
                        const author = getUser(item.message.authorId);
                        return (
                          <div className='flex gap-3'>
                            <img
                              src={author?.avatar}
                              alt=''
                              className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-muted shrink-0 mt-0.5'
                            />
                            <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                              <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                                <span className='text-sm font-medium'>
                                  {author?.displayName}
                                </span>
                                <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                  in #{item.message.channelName}
                                </span>
                                <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground ml-auto'>
                                  {formatTime(item.message.timestamp)}
                                </span>
                              </div>
                              <p className='text-sm text-foreground/80 truncate mt-0.5'>
                                <HighlightedText
                                  text={item.message.content.slice(0, 120)}
                                  query={query}
                                />
                              </p>
                              <div className='flex items-center gap-3 mt-1'>
                                {item.message.thread.length > 0 && (
                                  <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                    💬 {item.message.thread.length} replies
                                  </span>
                                )}
                                {item.message.reactions.length > 0 && (
                                  <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                    {item.message.reactions
                                      .map((r) => r.emoji)
                                      .join(' ')}
                                  </span>
                                )}
                              </div>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        );
                      })()}

                    {/* Channel */}
                    {item.type === 'channel' && item.channel && (
                      <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                        <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-md bg-muted flex items-center justify-center shrink-0'>
                          {item.channel.isPrivate ? (
                            <Lock className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                          ) : item.channel.type === 'announcement' ? (
                            <Megaphone className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                          ) : (
                            <Hash className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                          )}
                        </div>
                        <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                          <p className='text-sm font-medium'>
                            <HighlightedText
                              text={item.channel.name}
                              query={query}
                            />
                            {item.channel.isPrivate && (
                              <span className='ml-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                                🔒 Private
                              </span>
                            )}
                          </p>
                          <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate'>
                            {item.channel.description}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                        <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                          {item.channel.members.length} members
                        </span>
                      </div>
                    )}

                    {/* Person */}
                    {item.type === 'person' && item.person && (
                      <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                        <div className='relative'>
                          <img
                            src={item.person.avatar}
                            alt=''
                            className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-muted'
                          />
                          <span
                            className={`absolute bottom-0 right-0 w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full border-2 border-card ${statusColors[item.person.status]}`}
                          />
                        </div>
                        <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                          <p className='text-sm font-medium'>
                            <HighlightedText
                              text={item.person.displayName}
                              query={query}
                            />
                          </p>
                          <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                            @{item.person.username} · {item.person.title}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}

                    {/* File */}
                    {item.type === 'file' && item.file && (
                      <div className='flex items-center gap-3'>
                        <div className='w-8 h-8 rounded-md bg-muted flex items-center justify-center shrink-0'>
                          {item.file.attachment.type === 'image' ? (
                            <ImageIcon className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                          ) : (
                            <FileText className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                          )}
                        </div>
                        <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                          <p className='text-sm font-medium'>
                            <HighlightedText
                              text={item.file.attachment.name}
                              query={query}
                            />
                          </p>
                          <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                            Shared in #{item.file.channelName} ·{' '}
                            {item.file.attachment.size}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* ── Footer ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div className='flex items-center gap-4 px-4 py-2 border-t border-border text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
            <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
              <ArrowUp className='w-3 h-3' />
              <ArrowDown className='w-3 h-3' /> Navigate
            </span>
            <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
              <CornerDownLeft className='w-3 h-3' /> Open
            </span>
            <span>Tab — Switch filters</span>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      </motion.div>
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
};

import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  X,
  User,

  { id: 'appearance', label: 'Appearance', icon: Palette },
  { id: 'language', label: 'Language', icon: Languages },
  { id: 'emoji', label: 'Custom Emoji', icon: Smile },
  { id: 'shortcuts', label: 'Shortcuts', icon: Keyboard },
];

const shortcuts = [

interface SettingsModalProps {
  open: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  /** Pass true to open directly on the Shortcuts tab (from keyboard shortcut) */
  shortcutsOpen?: boolean;
  onShortcutsClose?: () => void;
  // UI preferences — owned by your UI slice / context
  theme: 'dark' | 'light';
  onThemeChange: (theme: 'dark' | 'light') => void;
  locale: Locale;
  onLocaleChange: (locale: Locale) => void;
}

// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Component
// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

export const SettingsModal = ({
  open,
  onClose,
  shortcutsOpen = false,
  onShortcutsClose,
  theme,
  onThemeChange,
  locale,
  onLocaleChange,
}: SettingsModalProps) => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const user = useAppSelector((s) => s.auth.user);

  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('profile');
  const [notifToggles, setNotifToggles] = useState<Record<string, boolean>>({
    desktop: true,
    mobile: true,
    email: false,
    sound: true,
  });
  const [statusEmoji, setStatusEmoji] = useState('');
  const [statusText, setStatusText] = useState('');
  const [statusDuration, setStatusDuration] = useState(0);
  const [savingStatus, setSavingStatus] = useState(false);
  const [savingProfile, setSavingProfile] = useState(false);

  // Sync status fields from Redux user
  useEffect(() => {
    if (user) {
      setStatusEmoji(user.statusEmoji ?? '');
      setStatusText(user.statusText ?? '');
    }
  }, [user?.statusEmoji, user?.statusText]);

  // Load notification prefs
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!user) return;
    mockApi.users
      .getPrefs(user.id)
      .then((prefs) => {
        if (prefs?.notifications) setNotifToggles(prefs.notifications);
      })
      .catch(() => {});
  }, [user?.id]);

  const isOpen = open || shortcutsOpen;
  if (!isOpen || !user) return null;

  const currentTab = shortcutsOpen ? 'shortcuts' : activeTab;

  const handleClose = () => {
    onClose();
    onShortcutsClose?.();
  };

  // Patch user in Redux and propagate to mockApi
  const updateProfile = (patch: Partial<typeof user>) => {
    dispatch(setCredentials({ ...user, ...patch }));
  };

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Handlers
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  const handleSetStatus = async (emoji: string, text: string) => {
    setSavingStatus(true);
    setStatusEmoji(emoji);
    setStatusText(text);
    updateProfile({ statusEmoji: emoji, statusText: text });
    await mockApi.users.updateStatus(user.id, {
      emoji,
      text,
      duration: statusDuration,
    });
    setSavingStatus(false);
    toast.success(text ? `Status set to ${emoji} ${text}` : 'Status cleared');
  };

  const handleClearStatus = () => handleSetStatus('', '');

  const handleSaveCustomStatus = () => {
    if (statusEmoji || statusText) handleSetStatus(statusEmoji, statusText);
  };

  const handleToggleNotif = async (key: string) => {
    const updated = { ...notifToggles, [key]: !notifToggles[key] };
    setNotifToggles(updated);
    await mockApi.users.savePrefs(user.id, { notifications: updated });
  };

  const handleProfileBlur = async (key: string, value: string) => {
    setSavingProfile(true);
    updateProfile({ [key]: value } as any);
    setSavingProfile(false);
  };

  const handleTabChange = (id: string) => {
    setActiveTab(id);
    // If we were driven here by shortcutsOpen and user clicks another tab,
    // notify parent so it can clear its shortcutsOpen flag
    if (shortcutsOpen && id !== 'shortcuts') {
      onShortcutsClose?.();
    }
  };

  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  // Render
  // ---------------------------------------------------------------------------

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
      className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4'
      onClick={handleClose}
    >
      <motion.div
        initial={{ scale: 0.95, opacity: 0 }}
        animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1 }}
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        className='w-full max-w-2xl bg-card border border-border rounded-xl shadow-2xl overflow-hidden max-h-[85vh] flex'
      >
        {/* Sidebar */}
        <div className='w-48 border-r border-border py-4 shrink-0'>
          <div className='px-4 mb-4'>
            <h2 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>Settings</h2>
          </div>
          {tabs.map((tab) => {
            const Icon = tab.icon;
            const isActive = currentTab === tab.id;
            return (
              <button
                key={tab.id}
                onClick={() => handleTabChange(tab.id)}
                className={`w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 text-sm transition-colors ${
                  isActive
                    ? 'bg-primary/10 text-primary'
                    : 'text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-foreground'
                }`}
              >
                <Icon className='w-4 h-4' /> {tab.label}
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        {/* Content */}
        <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 relative'>
          <button
            onClick={handleClose}
            className='absolute top-4 right-4 p-1 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
          >
            <X className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>

          {/* Shortcuts */}
          {currentTab === 'shortcuts' && (
            <div>
              <h3 className='font-heading font-bold mb-4'>
                Keyboard Shortcuts
              </h3>
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                {shortcuts.map((s) => (
                  <div
                    key={s.desc}
                    className='flex items-center justify-between py-2 border-b border-border'
                  >
                    <span className='text-sm text-foreground'>{s.desc}</span>
                    <div className='flex gap-1'>
                      {s.keys.map((k) => (
                        <kbd
                          key={k}
                          className='bg-muted text-muted-foreground text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded border border-border font-mono'
                        >
                          {k}
                        </kbd>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Profile */}
          {currentTab === 'profile' && (
            <div className='space-y-4'>
              <h3 className='font-heading font-bold mb-4'>Profile</h3>
              <div className='flex items-center gap-4 mb-4'>
                <img
                  src={user.avatar}
                  alt=''
                  className='w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-muted'
                />
                <button className='text-sm text-primary hover:underline'>
                  Change avatar
                </button>
                {savingProfile && (
                  <Loader2 className='w-4 h-4 animate-spin text-muted-foreground' />
                )}
              </div>
              {[
                {
                  label: 'Display Name',
                  value: user.displayName,
                  key: 'displayName',
                },
                { label: 'Username', value: user.username, key: 'username' },
                { label: 'Title', value: user.title, key: 'title' },
              ].map((field) => (
                <div key={field.key}>
                  <label className='text-sm font-medium block mb-1'>
                    {field.label}
                  </label>
                  <input
                    defaultValue={field.value}
                    onBlur={(e) => handleProfileBlur(field.key, e.target.value)}
                    className='w-full bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
                  />
                </div>
              ))}
              <div>
                <label className='text-sm font-medium block mb-1'>Bio</label>
                <textarea
                  defaultValue={user.bio}
                  onBlur={(e) => handleProfileBlur('bio', e.target.value)}
                  rows={3}
                  className='w-full bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm resize-none focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
                />
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Status */}
          {currentTab === 'status' && (
            <div className='space-y-4'>
              <h3 className='font-heading font-bold mb-4'>Status</h3>
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                <div className='flex gap-2'>
                  <input
                    value={statusEmoji}
                    onChange={(e) => setStatusEmoji(e.target.value)}
                    placeholder='😀'
                    className='w-12 bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-2 py-2 text-center text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
                  />
                  <input
                    value={statusText}
                    onChange={(e) => setStatusText(e.target.value)}
                    placeholder="What's your status?"
                    className='flex-1 bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
                  />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-1.5'>
                    Clear after
                  </p>
                  <div className='flex flex-wrap gap-1.5'>
                    {durationPresets.map((d) => (
                      <button
                        key={d.label}
                        onClick={() => setStatusDuration(d.value)}
                        className={`text-xs px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border transition-colors ${
                          statusDuration === d.value
                            ? 'border-primary bg-primary/10 text-primary'
                            : 'border-border hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
                        }`}
                      >
                        {d.label}
                      </button>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                </div>
                <button
                  onClick={handleSaveCustomStatus}
                  disabled={savingStatus || (!statusEmoji && !statusText)}
                  className='w-full py-2 rounded-md bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-sm font-medium hover:bg-primary/90 disabled:opacity-50 flex items-center justify-center gap-2'
                >
                  {savingStatus && (
                    <Loader2 className='w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin' />
                  )}
                  Set Status
                </button>
              </div>

              <div className='border-t border-border pt-3'>
                <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-2'>
                  Quick presets
                </p>
                <div className='space-y-1.5'>
                  {statusPresets.map((preset) => (
                    <button
                      key={preset.text}
                      onClick={() => handleSetStatus(preset.emoji, preset.text)}
                      className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-2.5 rounded-lg border border-border hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-left ${
                        user.statusEmoji === preset.emoji &&
                        user.statusText === preset.text
                          ? 'bg-primary/10 border-primary/30'
                          : ''
                      }`}
                    >
                      <span className='text-lg'>{preset.emoji}</span>
                      <span className='text-sm'>{preset.text}</span>
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              {(user.statusEmoji || user.statusText) && (
                <button
                  onClick={handleClearStatus}
                  disabled={savingStatus}
                  className='text-sm text-destructive hover:underline flex items-center gap-1.5'
                >
                  {savingStatus && <Loader2 className='w-3 h-3 animate-spin' />}
                  Clear status
                </button>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Notifications */}
          {currentTab === 'notifications' && (
            <div className='space-y-4'>
              <h3 className='font-heading font-bold mb-4'>Notifications</h3>
              {[
                { label: 'Desktop notifications', key: 'desktop' },
                { label: 'Mobile push notifications', key: 'mobile' },
                { label: 'Email notifications', key: 'email' },
                { label: 'Sound for messages', key: 'sound' },
              ].map(({ label, key }) => (
                <div
                  key={key}
                  className='flex items-center justify-between py-3 border-b border-border'
                >
                  <span className='text-sm'>{label}</span>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => handleToggleNotif(key)}
                    className={`w-10 h-6 rounded-full relative transition-colors ${
                      notifToggles[key] ? 'bg-primary' : 'bg-muted'
                    }`}
                  >
                    <span
                      className={`absolute top-1 w-4 h-4 rounded-full bg-foreground transition-all ${
                        notifToggles[key] ? 'left-5' : 'left-1'
                      }`}
                    />
                  </button>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Appearance */}
          {currentTab === 'appearance' && (
            <div className='space-y-4'>
              <h3 className='font-heading font-bold mb-4'>Appearance</h3>
              <div className='flex gap-3'>
                {(['dark', 'light'] as const).map((t) => (
                  <button
                    key={t}
                    onClick={() => onThemeChange(t)}
                    className={`flex-1 py-6 rounded-xl border-2 transition-colors flex flex-col items-center gap-2 ${
                      theme === t
                        ? 'border-primary bg-primary/10'
                        : 'border-border hover:border-muted-foreground'
                    }`}
                  >
                    {t === 'dark' ? (
                      <Moon className='w-6 h-6' />
                    ) : (
                      <Sun className='w-6 h-6' />
                    )}
                    <p className='font-medium text-sm capitalize'>{t}</p>
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Language */}
          {currentTab === 'language' && (
            <div className='space-y-4'>
              <h3 className='font-heading font-bold mb-4'>Language</h3>
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                {(Object.entries(LOCALE_LABELS) as [Locale, string][]).map(
                  ([code, label]) => (
                    <button
                      key={code}
                      onClick={() => onLocaleChange(code)}
                      className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-3 rounded-lg border transition-colors text-left ${
                        locale === code
                          ? 'border-primary bg-primary/10'
                          : 'border-border hover:bg-accent'
                      }`}
                    >
                      <span className='text-sm font-medium'>{label}</span>
                      <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground ml-auto'>
                        {code.toUpperCase()}
                      </span>
                    </button>
                  ),
                )}
              </div>
              <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                UI language preference. Content will remain in its original
                language.
              </p>
            </div>
          )}

          {/* Custom Emoji */}
          {currentTab === 'emoji' && <CustomEmojiManager />}
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\modals\WorkspaceSwitcher.tsx

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { X, Check } from 'lucide-react';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { setCurrentWorkspaceId } from '@/features/workspaceSlice';
import { resetChannelState } from '@/features/channelSlice';
import { useGetWorkspaces } from '@/hooks/workspace/useGetWorkspaces';
import { useJoinWorkspace } from '@/hooks/workspace/useJoinWorkspace';


interface WorkspaceSwitcherProps {
  open: boolean;
  onClose: () => void;
  onCreateWorkspace: () => void;
}

export const WorkspaceSwitcher = ({
  open,
  onClose,
  onCreateWorkspace,
}: WorkspaceSwitcherProps) => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const currentWorkspaceId = useAppSelector(
    (s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId,
  );

  const { data: workspaces = [] } = useGetWorkspaces();
  const { mutate: joinWorkspace, isPending } = useJoinWorkspace();

  const [joinMode, setJoinMode] = useState(false);
  const [joinCode, setJoinCode] = useState('');
  const [previewWs, setPreviewWs] = useState<(typeof workspaces)[0] | null>(
    null,
  );

  if (!open) return null;

  const handleClose = () => {
    setJoinMode(false);
    setJoinCode('');
    setPreviewWs(null);
    onClose();
  };

  const handleSwitchWorkspace = (id: string) => {
    if (id === currentWorkspaceId) {
      onClose();
      return;
    }
    dispatch(resetChannelState());
    dispatch(setCurrentWorkspaceId(id));
    onClose();
  };

  const handleCodeChange = (code: string) => {
    const upper = code.toUpperCase();
    setJoinCode(upper);
    const ws = workspaces.find(
      (w) => w.joinCode?.toLowerCase() === code.toLowerCase(),
    );
    setPreviewWs(ws ?? null);
  };

  const handleJoin = () => {
    if (joinCode.length < 3) return;
    joinWorkspace(joinCode, {
      onSuccess: () => {
        setTimeout(handleClose, 800);
      },
    });
  };

  const resetJoin = () => {
    setJoinMode(false);
    setJoinCode('');
    setPreviewWs(null);
  };

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
      className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/80 backdrop-blur-sm z-50 flex items-center justify-center p-4'
      onClick={handleClose}
    >
      <motion.div
        initial={{ scale: 0.95, opacity: 0 }}
        animate={{ scale: 1, opacity: 1 }}
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        className='w-full max-w-sm bg-card border border-border rounded-xl shadow-2xl p-6 space-y-4'
      >
        {/* Header */}
        <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
          <h2 className='font-heading font-bold text-lg'>Workspaces</h2>
          <button
            onClick={handleClose}
            className='p-1 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
          >
            <X className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
        </div>

        {!joinMode ? (
          <>
            {/* Workspace list */}
            <div className='space-y-1'>
              {workspaces.map((ws) => (
                <button
                  key={ws.id}
                  onClick={() => handleSwitchWorkspace(ws.id)}
                  className={`w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-lg text-left transition-colors ${
                    ws.id === currentWorkspaceId
                      ? 'bg-primary/10'
                      : 'hover:bg-accent'
                  }`}
                >
                  <span className='w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-secondary flex items-center justify-center text-lg'>
                    {ws.icon}
                  </span>
                  <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                    <p className='font-medium text-sm truncate'>{ws.name}</p>
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                      {ws.members.length} members
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  {ws.id === currentWorkspaceId && (
                    <Check className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
                  )}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>

            {/* Actions */}
            <div className='border-t border-border pt-3 space-y-2'>
              <button
                onClick={() => {
                  onClose();
                  onCreateWorkspace();
                }}
                className='w-full py-2 rounded-md border border-border text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
              >
                Create a Workspace
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={() => setJoinMode(true)}
                className='w-full py-2 rounded-md border border-border text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
              >
                Join a Workspace
              </button>
            </div>
          </>
        ) : (
          /* Join mode */
          <div className='space-y-3'>
            <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
              Enter a workspace invite code to join
            </p>

            <input
              value={joinCode}
              onChange={(e) => handleCodeChange(e.target.value)}
              placeholder='e.g. LNK-2026'
              maxLength={10}
              className='w-full bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm font-mono text-center tracking-widest focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
              autoFocus
            />

            {/* Workspace preview */}
            {previewWs && (
              <motion.div
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 4 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                className='flex items-center gap-3 p-3 bg-muted/50 rounded-lg border border-border'
              >
                <span className='w-10 h-10 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-secondary flex items-center justify-center text-xl'>
                  {previewWs.icon}
                </span>
                <div>
                  <p className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>
                    {previewWs.name}
                  </p>
                  <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                    {previewWs.members.length} members ·{' '}
                    {previewWs.channels?.length ?? 0} channels
                  </p>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            )}

            <div className='flex gap-2'>
              <button
                onClick={resetJoin}
                disabled={isPending}
                className='flex-1 py-2 rounded-md border border-border text-sm hover:bg-accent disabled:opacity-50'
              >
                Back
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={handleJoin}
                disabled={joinCode.length < 3 || isPending}
                className='flex-1 py-2 rounded-md bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-sm hover:bg-primary/90 disabled:opacity-50'
              >
                {isPending ? 'Joining…' : 'Join'}
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </motion.div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

import { NavLink as RouterNavLink, NavLinkProps } from 'react-router-dom';
import { forwardRef } from 'react';
import { cn } from '@/lib/utils';

interface NavLinkCompatProps extends Omit<NavLinkProps, 'className'> {
  className?: string;
  activeClassName?: string;
  pendingClassName?: string;
}

const NavLink = forwardRef<HTMLAnchorElement, NavLinkCompatProps>(
  ({ className, activeClassName, pendingClassName, to, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <RouterNavLink
        ref={ref}
        to={to}
        className={({ isActive, isPending }) =>
          cn(
            className,
            isActive && activeClassName,
            isPending && pendingClassName,
          )
        }
        {...props}
      />
    );
  },
);

NavLink.displayName = 'NavLink';

export { NavLink };

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\profile\ProfilePage.tsx

import React, { useState, useMemo, useEffect } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  ArrowLeft,
  Edit3,
  MessageSquare,
  Save,
  X,
  Hash,
  Clock,
  MapPin,
  FileText,
  Image as ImageIcon,
  Link2,
  Github,
  Twitter,
  Linkedin,
  Globe,
  Loader2,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';
import { mockApi } from '@/lib/mockApi';
import { type User, type Attachment } from '@/data/mockData';

const statusPresets = [
  { emoji: '🎯', text: 'Focusing' },
  { emoji: '🏖️', text: 'Vacationing' },
  { emoji: '🤒', text: 'Out sick' },
  { emoji: '🚂', text: 'Commuting' },
  { emoji: '📞', text: 'On a call' },
  { emoji: '🍽️', text: 'Lunch break' },
  { emoji: '💤', text: 'Away' },
];

type ProfileTab = 'about' | 'files' | 'channels';

interface ProfilePageProps {
  userId: string;
  onBack: () => void;
}

interface UserFile {
  attachment: Attachment;
  channelName: string;
  date: string;
}

export const ProfilePage = ({ userId, onBack }: ProfilePageProps) => {
  const { getUser, currentWorkspace, setCurrentDMId, setCurrentChannelId } =
    useWorkspace();
  const { auth, updateProfile } = useAuth();
  const { triggerConfetti } = useUI();

  const user = getUser(userId);
  const isOwnProfile = userId === auth.user?.id;
  const displayUser = isOwnProfile ? auth.user : user;

  const [tab, setTab] = useState<ProfileTab>('about');
  const [editing, setEditing] = useState(false);
  const [editForm, setEditForm] = useState<Partial<User>>({});
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const [statusEmoji, setStatusEmoji] = useState(
    displayUser?.statusEmoji || '',
  );
  const [statusText, setStatusText] = useState(displayUser?.statusText || '');
  const [userFiles, setUserFiles] = useState<UserFile[]>([]);
  const [filesLoading, setFilesLoading] = useState(false);
  const [fileFilter, setFileFilter] = useState<'all' | 'image' | 'document'>(
    'all',
  );

  // Load files when Files tab is selected
  useEffect(() => {
    if (tab === 'files' && displayUser) {
      setFilesLoading(true);
      mockApi.files.getUserFiles(displayUser.id).then((files) => {
        setUserFiles(files);
        setFilesLoading(false);
      });
    }
  }, [tab, displayUser?.id]);

  // Channels this user is in (that viewer can also see)
  const userChannels = useMemo(() => {
    if (!displayUser || !currentWorkspace) return [];
    return currentWorkspace.channels.filter(
      (ch) =>
        ch.members.includes(displayUser.id) &&
        ch.members.includes(auth.user?.id || ''),
    );
  }, [displayUser, currentWorkspace, auth.user]);

  const filteredFiles = useMemo(() => {
    if (fileFilter === 'all') return userFiles;
    if (fileFilter === 'image')
      return userFiles.filter((f) => f.attachment.type === 'image');
    return userFiles.filter((f) => f.attachment.type !== 'image');
  }, [userFiles, fileFilter]);

  if (!displayUser) return null;

  const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
    online: 'bg-online',
    away: 'bg-away',
    dnd: 'bg-dnd',
    offline: 'bg-muted-foreground',
  };
  const statusLabels: Record<string, string> = {
    online: 'Active',
    away: 'Away',
    dnd: 'Do Not Disturb',
    offline: 'Offline',
  };

  const localTime = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
    hour: 'numeric',
    minute: '2-digit',
    timeZone: displayUser.timezone,
  });

  const startEditing = () => {
    setEditForm({
      displayName: displayUser.displayName,
      bio: displayUser.bio,
      title: displayUser.title,
      timezone: displayUser.timezone,
    });
    setStatusEmoji(displayUser.statusEmoji || '');
    setStatusText(displayUser.statusText || '');
    setEditing(true);
  };

  const handleSave = async () => {
    setSaving(true);
    updateProfile(editForm);
    if (
      statusEmoji !== displayUser.statusEmoji ||
      statusText !== displayUser.statusText
    ) {
      updateProfile({ statusEmoji, statusText });
    }
    await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 300));
    setSaving(false);
    setEditing(false);
  };

  const handleMessage = () => {
    const dm = currentWorkspace?.dms.find(
      (d) =>
        d.participantIds.includes(displayUser.id) &&
        d.participantIds.includes(auth.user?.id || ''),
    );
    if (dm) setCurrentDMId(dm.id);
    onBack();
  };

  const tabItems: { id: ProfileTab; label: string; icon: typeof FileText }[] = [
    { id: 'about', label: 'About', icon: FileText },
    { id: 'files', label: 'Files', icon: ImageIcon },
    { id: 'channels', label: 'Channels', icon: Hash },
  ];

  // Social links (mock data for demo)
  const socialLinks = isOwnProfile
    ? [
        { icon: Github, label: 'GitHub', url: 'https://github.com' },
        { icon: Twitter, label: 'Twitter', url: 'https://twitter.com' },
        { icon: Globe, label: 'Website', url: 'https://example.com' },
      ]
    : [];

  return (
    <div className='flex flex-col h-full bg-background'>
      {/* Header */}
      <div className='shrink-0 px-4 py-3 border-b border-border flex items-center justify-between'>
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className='flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors'
        >
          <ArrowLeft className='w-4 h-4' /> Back
        </button>
        {isOwnProfile && !editing && (
          <button
            onClick={startEditing}
            className='flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-primary hover:text-primary/80 transition-colors'
          >
            <Edit3 className='w-4 h-4' /> Edit Profile
          </button>
        )}
        {editing && (
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
            <button
              onClick={() => setEditing(false)}
              className='px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
            >
              Cancel
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={handleSave}
              disabled={saving}
              className='px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-sm font-medium hover:bg-primary/90 disabled:opacity-50 flex items-center gap-1.5'
            >
              {saving ? (
                <Loader2 className='w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin' />
              ) : (
                <Save className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
              )}
              {saving ? 'Saving...' : 'Save'}
            </button>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Profile Hero */}
      <div className='px-6 py-6 border-b border-border'>
        <div className='flex items-start gap-5'>
          <div className='relative shrink-0'>
            <img
              src={displayUser.avatar}
              alt=''
              className='w-[100px] h-[100px] rounded-full bg-muted'
            />
            <span
              className={`absolute bottom-1 right-1 w-5 h-5 rounded-full border-[3px] border-background ${statusColors[displayUser.status]}`}
            />
          </div>
          <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
            {editing ? (
              <input
                value={editForm.displayName || ''}
                onChange={(e) =>
                  setEditForm((p) => ({ ...p, displayName: e.target.value }))
                }
                className='font-heading font-bold text-xl bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-2 py-1 w-full focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
              />
            ) : (
              <h1 className='font-heading font-bold text-xl'>
                {displayUser.displayName}
              </h1>
            )}
            <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
              @{displayUser.username}
            </p>
            {editing ? (
              <input
                value={editForm.title || ''}
                onChange={(e) =>
                  setEditForm((p) => ({ ...p, title: e.target.value }))
                }
                placeholder='Your title'
                className='text-sm bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-2 py-1 mt-1 w-full focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
              />
            ) : (
              displayUser.title && (
                <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1'>
                  {displayUser.title}
                </p>
              )
            )}
            <div className='flex items-center gap-3 mt-2 text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
              <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
                <Clock className='w-3.5 h-3.5' /> {localTime} local time
              </span>
              <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
                <MapPin className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />{' '}
                {displayUser.timezone.split('/').pop()?.replace('_', ' ')}
              </span>
            </div>
            <div className='flex items-center gap-2 mt-3'>
              <span className='inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border border-border'>
                <span
                  className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${statusColors[displayUser.status]}`}
                />
                {statusLabels[displayUser.status]}
              </span>
              {displayUser.statusEmoji && (
                <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                  {displayUser.statusEmoji} {displayUser.statusText}
                </span>
              )}
            </div>
            {!isOwnProfile && (
              <div className='flex gap-2 mt-3'>
                <button
                  onClick={handleMessage}
                  className='flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-sm font-medium hover:bg-primary/90'
                >
                  <MessageSquare className='w-3.5 h-3.5' /> Message
                </button>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Status Editor (own profile, editing mode) */}
      {isOwnProfile && editing && (
        <div className='px-6 py-4 border-b border-border space-y-3'>
          <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider'>
            Status
          </p>
          <div className='flex gap-2'>
            <input
              value={statusEmoji}
              onChange={(e) => setStatusEmoji(e.target.value)}
              placeholder='😀'
              className='w-12 bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-2 py-1.5 text-center text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
            />
            <input
              value={statusText}
              onChange={(e) => setStatusText(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="What's your status?"
              className='flex-1 bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-1.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
            />
          </div>
          <div className='flex flex-wrap gap-1.5'>
            {statusPresets.map((s) => (
              <button
                key={s.text}
                onClick={() => {
                  setStatusEmoji(s.emoji);
                  setStatusText(s.text);
                }}
                className='text-xs px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full border border-border hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
              >
                {s.emoji} {s.text}
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Tabs */}
      <div className='flex border-b border-border px-6'>
        {tabItems.map((t) => (
          <button
            key={t.id}
            onClick={() => setTab(t.id)}
            className={`flex items-center gap-1.5 px-4 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium border-b-2 transition-colors ${tab === t.id ? 'border-primary text-foreground' : 'border-transparent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'}`}
          >
            <t.icon className='w-3.5 h-3.5' /> {t.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Tab Content */}
      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-6 py-4'>
        <AnimatePresence mode='wait'>
          {tab === 'about' && (
            <motion.div
              key='about'
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
              className='space-y-4'
            >
              <div>
                <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-1'>
                  Bio
                </p>
                {editing ? (
                  <div>
                    <textarea
                      value={editForm.bio || ''}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setEditForm((p) => ({
                          ...p,
                          bio: e.target.value.slice(0, 200),
                        }))
                      }
                      rows={3}
                      className='w-full bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring resize-none'
                    />
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground text-right'>
                      {(editForm.bio || '').length}/200
                    </p>
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <p className='text-sm text-foreground/80'>
                    {displayUser.bio || 'No bio set'}
                  </p>
                )}
              </div>

              <div>
                <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-1'>
                  Email
                </p>
                <p className='text-sm text-foreground/80'>
                  {displayUser.email}
                </p>
              </div>

              <div>
                <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-1'>
                  Timezone
                </p>
                {editing ? (
                  <input
                    value={editForm.timezone || ''}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setEditForm((p) => ({ ...p, timezone: e.target.value }))
                    }
                    className='w-full bg-muted border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-2 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
                  />
                ) : (
                  <p className='text-sm text-foreground/80'>
                    {displayUser.timezone}
                  </p>
                )}
              </div>

              <div>
                <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-1'>
                  Member since
                </p>
                <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                  {new Date(displayUser.memberSince).toLocaleDateString(
                    'en-US',
                    { month: 'long', year: 'numeric' },
                  )}
                </p>
              </div>

              {/* Social Links */}
              {socialLinks.length > 0 && (
                <div>
                  <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-2'>
                    Links
                  </p>
                  <div className='space-y-1.5'>
                    {socialLinks.map((link) => (
                      <a
                        key={link.label}
                        href={link.url}
                        target='_blank'
                        rel='noopener noreferrer'
                        className='flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-primary hover:underline'
                      >
                        <link.icon className='w-4 h-4' /> {link.label}
                      </a>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </motion.div>
          )}

          {tab === 'files' && (
            <motion.div
              key='files'
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
            >
              {/* Filter bar */}
              <div className='flex gap-2 mb-4'>
                {(['all', 'image', 'document'] as const).map((f) => (
                  <button
                    key={f}
                    onClick={() => setFileFilter(f)}
                    className={`text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full border transition-colors capitalize ${fileFilter === f ? 'border-primary bg-primary/10 text-primary' : 'border-border text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent'}`}
                  >
                    {f === 'all'
                      ? 'All'
                      : f === 'image'
                        ? 'Images'
                        : 'Documents'}
                  </button>
                ))}
              </div>

              {filesLoading ? (
                <div className='flex items-center justify-center py-12'>
                  <Loader2 className='w-6 h-6 animate-spin text-muted-foreground' />
                </div>
              ) : filteredFiles.length === 0 ? (
                <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-8'>
                  No files shared yet
                </p>
              ) : (
                <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-3'>
                  {filteredFiles.map((f, i) => (
                    <motion.div
                      key={i}
                      initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
                      animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
                      transition={{ delay: i * 0.05 }}
                      className='border border-border rounded-lg p-3 hover:bg-accent/30 transition-colors'
                    >
                      {f.attachment.type === 'image' ? (
                        <div className='aspect-video rounded-md bg-muted mb-2 flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden'>
                          <img
                            src={f.attachment.url}
                            alt={f.attachment.name}
                            className='w-full h-full object-cover'
                          />
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <div className='aspect-video rounded-md bg-muted/50 mb-2 flex items-center justify-center'>
                          <FileText className='w-8 h-8 text-muted-foreground' />
                        </div>
                      )}
                      <p className='text-xs font-medium truncate'>
                        {f.attachment.name}
                      </p>
                      <p className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                        #{f.channelName} ·{' '}
                        {new Date(f.date).toLocaleDateString()}
                      </p>
                    </motion.div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </motion.div>
          )}

          {tab === 'channels' && (
            <motion.div
              key='channels'
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
              className='space-y-1'
            >
              {userChannels.length === 0 ? (
                <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground text-center py-8'>
                  No shared channels
                </p>
              ) : (
                userChannels.map((ch) => (
                  <button
                    key={ch.id}
                    onClick={() => {
                      setCurrentChannelId(ch.id);
                      onBack();
                    }}
                    className='w-full flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent/50 transition-colors text-left'
                  >
                    <Hash className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0' />
                    <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                      <p className='text-sm font-medium truncate'>{ch.name}</p>
                      <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate'>
                        {ch.description}
                      </p>
                    </div>
                    <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                      {ch.members.length} members
                    </span>
                  </button>
                ))
              )}
            </motion.div>
          )}
        </AnimatePresence>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\ActivityPanel.tsx

import React, { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  X,
  MessageSquare,
  AtSign,
  Heart,
  Reply,
  Filter,
  Bell,
  BellOff,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';

const typeIcons: Record<string, typeof MessageSquare> = {
  mention: AtSign,
  reaction: Heart,
  thread_reply: Reply,
  dm: MessageSquare,
};

const typeLabels: Record<string, string> = {
  mention: 'mentioned you',
  reaction: 'reacted to your message',
  thread_reply: 'replied in a thread',
  dm: 'sent you a message',
};

const typeBadgeColors: Record<string, string> = {
  mention: 'bg-blue-500/10 text-blue-500',
  reaction: 'bg-pink-500/10 text-pink-500',
  thread_reply: 'bg-emerald-500/10 text-emerald-500',
  dm: 'bg-violet-500/10 text-violet-500',
};

type FilterType = 'all' | 'mention' | 'reaction' | 'thread_reply' | 'dm';

export const ActivityPanel = () => {
  const {
    notifications,
    markNotificationRead,
    markAllNotificationsRead,
    getUser,
  } = useWorkspace();
  const { setRightPanel, openThread } = useUI();
  const [filter, setFilter] = useState<FilterType>('all');

  const unreadCount = notifications.filter((n) => !n.read).length;
  const filtered =
    filter === 'all'
      ? notifications
      : notifications.filter((n) => n.type === filter);

  const filters: {
    key: FilterType;
    label: string;
    icon: typeof MessageSquare;
  }[] = [
    { key: 'all', label: 'All', icon: Bell },
    { key: 'mention', label: 'Mentions', icon: AtSign },
    { key: 'reaction', label: 'Reactions', icon: Heart },
    { key: 'thread_reply', label: 'Threads', icon: Reply },
    { key: 'dm', label: 'DMs', icon: MessageSquare },
  ];

  const formatTime = (ts: string) => {
    const d = new Date(ts);
    const now = new Date();
    const diff = now.getTime() - d.getTime();
    const mins = Math.floor(diff / 60000);
    if (mins < 1) return 'just now';
    if (mins < 60) return `${mins}m ago`;
    const hours = Math.floor(mins / 60);
    if (hours < 24) return `${hours}h ago`;
    const days = Math.floor(hours / 24);
    if (days < 7) return `${days}d ago`;
    return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' });
  };

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ x: '100%' }}
      animate={{ x: 0 }}
      exit={{ x: '100%' }}
      transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
      className='h-full flex flex-col bg-card border-l border-border'
    >
      {/* Header */}
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border shrink-0'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
          <Bell className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
          <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>Activity</h3>
          {unreadCount > 0 && (
            <span className='bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground text-[10px] font-bold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full min-w-[18px] text-center'>
              {unreadCount}
            </span>
          )}
        </div>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-1'>
          {unreadCount > 0 && (
            <button
              onClick={markAllNotificationsRead}
              className='text-[10px] text-primary hover:text-primary/80 px-2 py-1 rounded-md hover:bg-primary/10 transition-colors'
            >
              Mark all read
            </button>
          )}
          <button
            onClick={() => setRightPanel(null)}
            className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
          >
            <X className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Filter tabs */}
      <div className='flex items-center gap-1 px-3 py-2 border-b border-border overflow-x-auto'>
        {filters.map((f) => {
          const count =
            f.key === 'all'
              ? notifications.filter((n) => !n.read).length
              : notifications.filter((n) => n.type === f.key && !n.read).length;
          return (
            <button
              key={f.key}
              onClick={() => setFilter(f.key)}
              className={`flex items-center gap-1 px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full text-[11px] font-medium transition-colors whitespace-nowrap ${
                filter === f.key
                  ? 'bg-primary/10 text-primary'
                  : 'text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-foreground'
              }`}
            >
              <f.icon className='w-3 h-3' />
              {f.label}
              {count > 0 && (
                <span className='bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground text-[9px] px-1 rounded-full min-w-[14px] text-center'>
                  {count}
                </span>
              )}
            </button>
          );
        })}
      </div>

      {/* Notification list */}
      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto'>
        {filtered.length === 0 ? (
          <div className='flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center px-4'>
            <div className='w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-muted/50 flex items-center justify-center mb-3'>
              <BellOff className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground' />
            </div>
            <p className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground mb-1'>
              All caught up!
            </p>
            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
              {filter === 'all'
                ? 'No notifications yet'
                : `No ${filter.replace('_', ' ')} notifications`}
            </p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <AnimatePresence>
            {filtered.map((n, idx) => {
              const user = getUser(n.fromUserId);
              const Icon = typeIcons[n.type] || MessageSquare;
              return (
                <motion.button
                  key={n.id}
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, x: 10 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                  transition={{ delay: idx * 0.03 }}
                  onClick={() => markNotificationRead(n.id)}
                  className={`w-full flex items-start gap-3 px-4 py-3 hover:bg-accent/50 transition-colors text-left group ${
                    !n.read ? 'bg-primary/5' : ''
                  }`}
                >
                  <div className='relative shrink-0 mt-0.5'>
                    <img
                      src={user?.avatar || ''}
                      className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-muted'
                      alt=''
                    />
                    <span
                      className={`absolute -bottom-0.5 -right-0.5 w-4 h-4 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center ${typeBadgeColors[n.type] || 'bg-muted'}`}
                    >
                      <Icon className='w-2.5 h-2.5' />
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                    <div className='flex items-baseline gap-1.5 flex-wrap'>
                      <span className='text-sm font-semibold text-foreground'>
                        {user?.displayName}
                      </span>
                      <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                        {typeLabels[n.type]}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5 line-clamp-2'>
                      {n.messagePreview}
                    </p>
                    <p className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground/60 mt-1'>
                      {formatTime(n.timestamp)}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  {!n.read && (
                    <span className='w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-primary shrink-0 mt-2 group-hover:scale-125 transition-transform' />
                  )}
                </motion.button>
              );
            })}
          </AnimatePresence>
        )}
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\AnalyticsDashboard.tsx
