import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  BarChart3,
  TrendingUp,
  TrendingDown,
  MessageSquare,
  Users,
  Hash,
  Smile,
  FileText,
  ArrowLeft,
} from 'lucide-react';
import {
  BarChart,
  Bar,
  XAxis,
  YAxis,
  CartesianGrid,
  Tooltip,
  ResponsiveContainer,
  LineChart,
  Line,
  PieChart,
  Pie,
  Cell,
} from 'recharts';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';

const generateDailyMessages = () => {
  const data = [];
  for (let i = 13; i >= 0; i--) {
    const d = new Date();
    d.setDate(d.getDate() - i);
    data.push({
      day: d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric' }),
      messages: Math.floor(Math.random() * 80) + 20,
    });
  }
  return data;
};

const CHART_COLORS = [
  'hsl(239, 84%, 67%)',
  'hsl(258, 90%, 66%)',
  'hsl(172, 50%, 40%)',
  'hsl(38, 92%, 50%)',
  'hsl(0, 72%, 51%)',
];

export const AnalyticsDashboard = ({ onBack }: { onBack: () => void }) => {
  const { currentWorkspace, getUser } = useWorkspace();
  const [messagesData] = useState(generateDailyMessages);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    const t = setTimeout(() => setLoading(false), 800);
    return () => clearTimeout(t);
  }, []);

  if (!currentWorkspace) return null;

  const channelActivity = currentWorkspace.channels.slice(0, 5).map((ch) => ({
    name: `#${ch.name}`,
    messages: Math.floor(Math.random() * 200) + 30,
  }));

  const topContributors = currentWorkspace.members
    .slice(0, 5)
    .map((id) => {
      const user = getUser(id);
      return {
        name: user?.displayName || 'Unknown',
        avatar: user?.avatar || '',
        messages: Math.floor(Math.random() * 150) + 20,
      };
    })
    .sort((a, b) => b.messages - a.messages);

  const emojiUsage = [
    { emoji: '👍', count: 45 },
    { emoji: '🎉', count: 38 },
    { emoji: '❤️', count: 32 },
    { emoji: '🔥', count: 28 },
    { emoji: '😂', count: 24 },
    { emoji: '🚀', count: 21 },
  ];

  const stats = [
    {
      label: 'Messages Today',
      value: '127',
      change: '+12%',
      up: true,
      icon: MessageSquare,
    },
    {
      label: 'Active Members',
      value: `${currentWorkspace.members.length}`,
      change: '+2',
      up: true,
      icon: Users,
    },
    {
      label: 'Channels',
      value: `${currentWorkspace.channels.length}`,
      change: '0',
      up: true,
      icon: Hash,
    },
    {
      label: 'Files Shared',
      value: '34',
      change: '+8%',
      up: true,
      icon: FileText,
    },
  ];

  return (
    <div className='flex flex-col h-full overflow-hidden'>
      <div className='shrink-0 px-6 py-4 border-b border-border flex items-center gap-3'>
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
        >
          <ArrowLeft className='w-4 h-4' />
        </button>
        <BarChart3 className='w-5 h-5 text-primary' />
        <h2 className='font-heading font-bold text-lg'>Workspace Analytics</h2>
      </div>

      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-6 space-y-6'>
        {loading ? (
          <div className='grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4'>
            {[1, 2, 3, 4].map((i) => (
              <div
                key={i}
                className='h-24 rounded-xl bg-muted animate-shimmer'
                style={{ animationDelay: `${i * 0.1}s` }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        ) : (
          <>
            {/* Stats cards */}
            <div className='grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-4'>
              {stats.map((stat, i) => {
                const Icon = stat.icon;
                return (
                  <motion.div
                    key={stat.label}
                    initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                    animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                    transition={{ delay: i * 0.1 }}
                    className='rounded-xl border border-border bg-card p-4 space-y-2'
                  >
                    <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
                      <Icon className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground' />
                      <span
                        className={`flex items-center gap-0.5 text-[10px] font-medium ${stat.up ? 'text-green-500' : 'text-red-500'}`}
                      >
                        {stat.up ? (
                          <TrendingUp className='w-3 h-3' />
                        ) : (
                          <TrendingDown className='w-3 h-3' />
                        )}
                        {stat.change}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <p className='text-2xl font-bold font-heading'>
                      {stat.value}
                    </p>
                    <p className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                      {stat.label}
                    </p>
                  </motion.div>
                );
              })}
            </div>

            {/* Messages per day chart */}
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              transition={{ delay: 0.3 }}
              className='rounded-xl border border-border bg-card p-4'
            >
              <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm mb-4'>
                Messages per Day
              </h3>
              <div className='h-[200px]'>
                <ResponsiveContainer width='100%' height='100%'>
                  <BarChart data={messagesData}>
                    <CartesianGrid
                      strokeDasharray='3 3'
                      stroke='hsl(var(--border))'
                    />
                    <XAxis
                      dataKey='day'
                      tick={{
                        fontSize: 10,
                        fill: 'hsl(var(--muted-foreground))',
                      }}
                    />
                    <YAxis
                      tick={{
                        fontSize: 10,
                        fill: 'hsl(var(--muted-foreground))',
                      }}
                    />
                    <Tooltip
                      contentStyle={{
                        backgroundColor: 'hsl(var(--card))',
                        border: '1px solid hsl(var(--border))',
                        borderRadius: 8,
                        fontSize: 12,
                      }}
                    />
                    <Bar
                      dataKey='messages'
                      fill='hsl(var(--primary))'
                      radius={[4, 4, 0, 0]}
                    />
                  </BarChart>
                </ResponsiveContainer>
              </div>
            </motion.div>

            <div className='grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-4'>
              {/* Most active channels */}
              <motion.div
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                transition={{ delay: 0.4 }}
                className='rounded-xl border border-border bg-card p-4'
              >
                <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm mb-3'>
                  Most Active Channels
                </h3>
                <div className='space-y-2'>
                  {channelActivity.map((ch, i) => (
                    <div key={ch.name} className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                      <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground w-4'>
                        {i + 1}
                      </span>
                      <span className='text-sm flex-1 truncate'>{ch.name}</span>
                      <div className='w-24 h-2 rounded-full bg-muted overflow-hidden'>
                        <motion.div
                          initial={{ width: 0 }}
                          animate={{ width: `${(ch.messages / 230) * 100}%` }}
                          transition={{ delay: 0.5 + i * 0.1, duration: 0.8 }}
                          className='h-full rounded-full'
                          style={{
                            backgroundColor:
                              CHART_COLORS[i % CHART_COLORS.length],
                          }}
                        />
                      </div>
                      <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground w-8 text-right'>
                        {ch.messages}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </motion.div>

              {/* Top contributors */}
              <motion.div
                initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                transition={{ delay: 0.5 }}
                className='rounded-xl border border-border bg-card p-4'
              >
                <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm mb-3'>
                  Top Contributors
                </h3>
                <div className='space-y-2'>
                  {topContributors.map((user, i) => (
                    <div key={user.name} className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                      <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground w-4'>
                        {i + 1}
                      </span>
                      <img
                        src={user.avatar}
                        alt=''
                        className='w-5 h-5 rounded-full'
                      />
                      <span className='text-sm flex-1 truncate'>
                        {user.name}
                      </span>
                      <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                        {user.messages} msgs
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            </div>

            {/* Emoji usage */}
            <motion.div
              initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
              animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
              transition={{ delay: 0.6 }}
              className='rounded-xl border border-border bg-card p-4'
            >
              <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm mb-3'>
                Popular Reactions
              </h3>
              <div className='flex gap-3 flex-wrap'>
                {emojiUsage.map((e) => (
                  <div
                    key={e.emoji}
                    className='flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full border border-border bg-muted/30'
                  >
                    <span className='text-lg'>{e.emoji}</span>
                    <span className='text-xs font-medium'>{e.count}</span>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            </motion.div>
          </>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\CalendarPanel.tsx

import React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  X,
  Calendar as CalendarIcon,
  Plus,
  ChevronLeft,
  ChevronRight,
  Clock,
  MapPin,
  Users,
  Check,
  HelpCircle,
  X as XMark,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface CalendarEvent {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  description: string;
  date: string; // YYYY-MM-DD
  time: string;
  channelId: string;
  creatorId: string;
  rsvp: Record<string, 'yes' | 'no' | 'maybe'>;
}

const genId = () =>
  `evt_${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6)}`;

const loadEvents = (channelId: string): CalendarEvent[] => {
  try {
    return JSON.parse(
      localStorage.getItem(`linkly_events_${channelId}`) || '[]',
    );
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
};
const saveEvents = (channelId: string, events: CalendarEvent[]) => {
  localStorage.setItem(`linkly_events_${channelId}`, JSON.stringify(events));
};

const MONTHS = [
  'January',
  'February',
  'March',
  'April',
  'May',
  'June',
  'July',
  'August',
  'September',
  'October',
  'November',
  'December',
];
const DAYS = ['Sun', 'Mon', 'Tue', 'Wed', 'Thu', 'Fri', 'Sat'];

export const CalendarPanel = ({ onClose }: { onClose: () => void }) => {
  const { currentChannel, getUser } = useWorkspace();
  const { auth } = useAuth();
  const channelId = currentChannel?.id || '';
  const userId = auth.user?.id || 'u1';

  const [events, setEvents] = useState<CalendarEvent[]>(loadEvents(channelId));
  const [viewMode, setViewMode] = useState<'month' | 'week'>('month');
  const [currentDate, setCurrentDate] = useState(new Date());
  const [selectedDate, setSelectedDate] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showCreateForm, setShowCreateForm] = useState(false);
  const [newEvent, setNewEvent] = useState({
    title: '',
    description: '',
    time: '10:00',
  });

  const year = currentDate.getFullYear();
  const month = currentDate.getMonth();

  const daysInMonth = new Date(year, month + 1, 0).getDate();
  const firstDayOfMonth = new Date(year, month, 1).getDay();

  const calendarDays = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < firstDayOfMonth; i++) calendarDays.push(null);
  for (let i = 1; i <= daysInMonth; i++) calendarDays.push(i);

  const prev = () => setCurrentDate(new Date(year, month - 1, 1));
  const next = () => setCurrentDate(new Date(year, month + 1, 1));

  const dateStr = (day: number) =>
    `${year}-${String(month + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(day).padStart(2, '0')}`;
  const eventsOnDay = (day: number) =>
    events.filter((e) => e.date === dateStr(day));

  const handleCreateEvent = () => {
    if (!newEvent.title || !selectedDate) return;
    const event: CalendarEvent = {
      id: genId(),
      title: newEvent.title,
      description: newEvent.description,
      date: selectedDate,
      time: newEvent.time,
      channelId,
      creatorId: userId,
      rsvp: { [userId]: 'yes' },
    };
    const updated = [...events, event];
    setEvents(updated);
    saveEvents(channelId, updated);
    setShowCreateForm(false);
    setNewEvent({ title: '', description: '', time: '10:00' });
    toast.success('Event created!');
  };

  const handleRSVP = (eventId: string, response: 'yes' | 'no' | 'maybe') => {
    const updated = events.map((e) =>
      e.id === eventId ? { ...e, rsvp: { ...e.rsvp, [userId]: response } } : e,
    );
    setEvents(updated);
    saveEvents(channelId, updated);
  };

  const selectedEvents = selectedDate
    ? events.filter((e) => e.date === selectedDate)
    : [];
  const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ x: '100%' }}
      animate={{ x: 0 }}
      exit={{ x: '100%' }}
      transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
      className='h-full flex flex-col bg-card border-l border-border'
    >
      {/* Header */}
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
          <CalendarIcon className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
          <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>Calendar</h3>
        </div>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-1'>
          <div className='flex rounded-md border border-border overflow-hidden text-xs'>
            <button
              onClick={() => setViewMode('month')}
              className={`px-2 py-1 ${viewMode === 'month' ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground' : 'hover:bg-accent'}`}
            >
              Month
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={() => setViewMode('week')}
              className={`px-2 py-1 ${viewMode === 'week' ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground' : 'hover:bg-accent'}`}
            >
              Week
            </button>
          </div>
          <button
            onClick={onClose}
            className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
          >
            <X className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Month navigation */}
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2'>
        <button onClick={prev} className='p-1 rounded hover:bg-accent'>
          <ChevronLeft className='w-4 h-4' />
        </button>
        <span className='text-sm font-heading font-bold'>
          {MONTHS[month]} {year}
        </span>
        <button onClick={next} className='p-1 rounded hover:bg-accent'>
          <ChevronRight className='w-4 h-4' />
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Calendar grid */}
      <div className='px-4 pb-2'>
        <div className='grid grid-cols-7 gap-px'>
          {DAYS.map((d) => (
            <div
              key={d}
              className='text-center text-[10px] font-medium text-muted-foreground py-1'
            >
              {d}
            </div>
          ))}
          {calendarDays.map((day, i) => {
            if (day === null) return <div key={`empty-${i}`} />;
            const ds = dateStr(day);
            const dayEvents = eventsOnDay(day);
            const isToday = ds === today;
            const isSelected = ds === selectedDate;
            return (
              <button
                key={i}
                onClick={() => setSelectedDate(ds)}
                className={`relative p-1 text-xs rounded-md transition-colors min-h-[32px] ${
                  isSelected
                    ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground'
                    : isToday
                      ? 'bg-primary/10 text-primary font-bold'
                      : 'hover:bg-accent text-foreground'
                }`}
              >
                {day}
                {dayEvents.length > 0 && (
                  <div className='absolute bottom-0.5 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 flex gap-0.5'>
                    {dayEvents.slice(0, 3).map((_, j) => (
                      <span
                        key={j}
                        className={`w-1 h-1 rounded-full ${isSelected ? 'bg-primary-foreground' : 'bg-primary'}`}
                      />
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
              </button>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Selected day events */}
      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto border-t border-border'>
        {selectedDate ? (
          <div className='p-4 space-y-3'>
            <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
              <span className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground'>
                {new Date(selectedDate + 'T12:00:00').toLocaleDateString(
                  'en-US',
                  { weekday: 'long', month: 'short', day: 'numeric' },
                )}
              </span>
              <button
                onClick={() => setShowCreateForm(true)}
                className='flex items-center gap-1 text-xs text-primary hover:underline'
              >
                <Plus className='w-3 h-3' /> Add event
              </button>
            </div>

            {/* Create form */}
            <AnimatePresence>
              {showCreateForm && (
                <motion.div
                  initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                  animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
                  exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                  className='overflow-hidden'
                >
                  <div className='space-y-2 p-3 rounded-lg border border-border bg-muted/30'>
                    <input
                      value={newEvent.title}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setNewEvent({ ...newEvent, title: e.target.value })
                      }
                      placeholder='Event title'
                      className='w-full bg-background border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-1.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
                    />
                    <div className='flex gap-2'>
                      <input
                        type='time'
                        value={newEvent.time}
                        onChange={(e) =>
                          setNewEvent({ ...newEvent, time: e.target.value })
                        }
                        className='bg-background border border-border rounded-md px-2 py-1 text-xs focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
                      />
                    </div>
                    <textarea
                      value={newEvent.description}
                      onChange={(e) =>
                        setNewEvent({
                          ...newEvent,
                          description: e.target.value,
                        })
                      }
                      placeholder='Description (optional)'
                      rows={2}
                      className='w-full bg-background border border-border rounded-md px-3 py-1.5 text-sm resize-none focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring'
                    />
                    <div className='flex gap-2'>
                      <button
                        onClick={handleCreateEvent}
                        className='px-3 py-1 rounded-md bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-xs hover:bg-primary/90'
                      >
                        Create
                      </button>
                      <button
                        onClick={() => setShowCreateForm(false)}
                        className='text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground'
                      >
                        Cancel
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </motion.div>
              )}
            </AnimatePresence>

            {selectedEvents.length === 0 && !showCreateForm && (
              <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center py-4'>
                No events on this day
              </p>
            )}

            {selectedEvents.map((event) => {
              const creator = getUser(event.creatorId);
              const myRsvp = event.rsvp[userId];
              const yesCnt = Object.values(event.rsvp).filter(
                (v) => v === 'yes',
              ).length;
              return (
                <motion.div
                  key={event.id}
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 4 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                  className='rounded-lg border border-border bg-card/50 p-3 space-y-2'
                >
                  <div className='flex items-start gap-2'>
                    <div className='w-1 h-8 rounded-full bg-primary shrink-0 mt-0.5' />
                    <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                      <p className='text-sm font-medium'>{event.title}</p>
                      <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5'>
                        <span className='flex items-center gap-0.5'>
                          <Clock className='w-2.5 h-2.5' />
                          {event.time}
                        </span>
                        <span className='flex items-center gap-0.5'>
                          <Users className='w-2.5 h-2.5' />
                          {yesCnt} going
                        </span>
                      </div>
                      {event.description && (
                        <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1'>
                          {event.description}
                        </p>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div className='flex gap-1 ml-3'>
                    {(['yes', 'maybe', 'no'] as const).map((r) => {
                      const Icon =
                        r === 'yes'
                          ? Check
                          : r === 'maybe'
                            ? HelpCircle
                            : XMark;
                      return (
                        <button
                          key={r}
                          onClick={() => handleRSVP(event.id, r)}
                          className={`flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-md text-[10px] border transition-colors ${
                            myRsvp === r
                              ? 'border-primary bg-primary/10 text-primary'
                              : 'border-border hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
                          }`}
                        >
                          <Icon className='w-2.5 h-2.5' />
                          {r === 'yes'
                            ? 'Going'
                            : r === 'maybe'
                              ? 'Maybe'
                              : "Can't go"}
                        </button>
                      );
                    })}
                  </div>
                </motion.div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div className='flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center px-4'>
            <CalendarIcon className='w-8 h-8 text-muted-foreground/30 mb-2' />
            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
              Select a day to view events
            </p>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\CanvasPanel.tsx

import React, { useState, useRef, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  X,
  Pencil,
  Square,
  Circle,
  Minus,
  Type,
  Eraser,
  Download,
  Send,
  Palette,
  StickyNote,
  ArrowRight,
  Undo,
  Trash2,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

type Tool =
  | 'pen'
  | 'eraser'
  | 'rect'
  | 'circle'
  | 'line'
  | 'arrow'
  | 'sticky'
  | 'text';
type DrawElement = {
  id: string;
  type: Tool;
  points?: { x: number; y: number }[];
  x?: number;
  y?: number;
  w?: number;
  h?: number;
  color: string;
  lineWidth: number;
  text?: string;
};

const COLORS = [
  '#7c3aed',
  '#ef4444',
  '#f59e0b',
  '#10b981',
  '#3b82f6',
  '#ec4899',
  '#f97316',
  '#ffffff',
  '#6b7280',
];

export const CanvasPanel = ({
  onClose,
  onShareToChannel,
}: {
  onClose: () => void;
  onShareToChannel: (imageData: string) => void;
}) => {
  const canvasRef = useRef<HTMLCanvasElement>(null);
  const [tool, setTool] = useState<Tool>('pen');
  const [color, setColor] = useState('#7c3aed');
  const [lineWidth, setLineWidth] = useState(3);
  const [elements, setElements] = useState<DrawElement[]>([]);
  const [isDrawing, setIsDrawing] = useState(false);
  const [showColorPicker, setShowColorPicker] = useState(false);
  const currentElement = useRef<DrawElement | null>(null);

  const redraw = useCallback(() => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d')!;
    ctx.clearRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    // Background
    ctx.fillStyle = '#1a1a2e';
    ctx.fillRect(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);

    // Grid
    ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.03)';
    ctx.lineWidth = 1;
    for (let x = 0; x < canvas.width; x += 20) {
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(x, 0);
      ctx.lineTo(x, canvas.height);
      ctx.stroke();
    }
    for (let y = 0; y < canvas.height; y += 20) {
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(0, y);
      ctx.lineTo(canvas.width, y);
      ctx.stroke();
    }

    elements.forEach((el) => drawElement(ctx, el));
    if (currentElement.current) drawElement(ctx, currentElement.current);
  }, [elements]);

  useEffect(() => {
    redraw();
  }, [redraw]);

  const drawElement = (ctx: CanvasRenderingContext2D, el: DrawElement) => {
    ctx.strokeStyle = el.type === 'eraser' ? '#1a1a2e' : el.color;
    ctx.fillStyle = el.color;
    ctx.lineWidth = el.type === 'eraser' ? 20 : el.lineWidth;
    ctx.lineCap = 'round';
    ctx.lineJoin = 'round';

    switch (el.type) {
      case 'pen':
      case 'eraser':
        if (el.points && el.points.length > 1) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(el.points[0].x, el.points[0].y);
          for (let i = 1; i < el.points.length; i++)
            ctx.lineTo(el.points[i].x, el.points[i].y);
          ctx.stroke();
        }
        break;
      case 'rect':
        if (el.x != null && el.y != null && el.w != null && el.h != null) {
          ctx.strokeRect(el.x, el.y, el.w, el.h);
        }
        break;
      case 'circle':
        if (el.x != null && el.y != null && el.w != null && el.h != null) {
          const rx = Math.abs(el.w) / 2,
            ry = Math.abs(el.h) / 2;
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.ellipse(
            el.x + el.w / 2,
            el.y + el.h / 2,
            rx,
            ry,
            0,
            0,
            Math.PI * 2,
          );
          ctx.stroke();
        }
        break;
      case 'line':
      case 'arrow':
        if (el.x != null && el.y != null && el.w != null && el.h != null) {
          ctx.beginPath();
          ctx.moveTo(el.x, el.y);
          ctx.lineTo(el.x + el.w, el.y + el.h);
          ctx.stroke();
          if (el.type === 'arrow') {
            const angle = Math.atan2(el.h, el.w);
            const headLen = 12;
            ctx.beginPath();
            ctx.moveTo(el.x + el.w, el.y + el.h);
            ctx.lineTo(
              el.x + el.w - headLen * Math.cos(angle - 0.5),
              el.y + el.h - headLen * Math.sin(angle - 0.5),
            );
            ctx.moveTo(el.x + el.w, el.y + el.h);
            ctx.lineTo(
              el.x + el.w - headLen * Math.cos(angle + 0.5),
              el.y + el.h - headLen * Math.sin(angle + 0.5),
            );
            ctx.stroke();
          }
        }
        break;
      case 'sticky':
        if (el.x != null && el.y != null) {
          const w = 120,
            h = 100;
          ctx.fillStyle = '#fde68a';
          ctx.shadowColor = 'rgba(0,0,0,0.2)';
          ctx.shadowBlur = 8;
          ctx.fillRect(el.x, el.y, w, h);
          ctx.shadowBlur = 0;
          ctx.fillStyle = '#92400e';
          ctx.font = '12px DM Sans, sans-serif';
          const lines = (el.text || 'Note').split('\n');
          lines.forEach((line, i) =>
            ctx.fillText(line, el.x! + 8, el.y! + 20 + i * 16),
          );
        }
        break;
      case 'text':
        if (el.x != null && el.y != null) {
          ctx.fillStyle = el.color;
          ctx.font = `${el.lineWidth * 6}px DM Sans, sans-serif`;
          ctx.fillText(el.text || 'Text', el.x, el.y);
        }
        break;
    }
  };

  const getPos = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    const rect = canvasRef.current!.getBoundingClientRect();
    return { x: e.clientX - rect.left, y: e.clientY - rect.top };
  };

  const handleMouseDown = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    const pos = getPos(e);
    if (tool === 'sticky') {
      const text = prompt('Sticky note text:', 'Note') || 'Note';
      setElements((prev) => [
        ...prev,
        {
          id: `el_${Date.now()}`,
          type: 'sticky',
          x: pos.x,
          y: pos.y,
          color,
          lineWidth,
          text,
        },
      ]);
      return;
    }
    if (tool === 'text') {
      const text = prompt('Enter text:', 'Hello') || 'Hello';
      setElements((prev) => [
        ...prev,
        {
          id: `el_${Date.now()}`,
          type: 'text',
          x: pos.x,
          y: pos.y,
          color,
          lineWidth,
          text,
        },
      ]);
      return;
    }
    setIsDrawing(true);
    if (tool === 'pen' || tool === 'eraser') {
      currentElement.current = {
        id: `el_${Date.now()}`,
        type: tool,
        points: [pos],
        color,
        lineWidth,
      };
    } else {
      currentElement.current = {
        id: `el_${Date.now()}`,
        type: tool,
        x: pos.x,
        y: pos.y,
        w: 0,
        h: 0,
        color,
        lineWidth,
      };
    }
  };

  const handleMouseMove = (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    if (!isDrawing || !currentElement.current) return;
    const pos = getPos(e);
    if (
      currentElement.current.type === 'pen' ||
      currentElement.current.type === 'eraser'
    ) {
      currentElement.current.points!.push(pos);
    } else {
      currentElement.current.w = pos.x - (currentElement.current.x || 0);
      currentElement.current.h = pos.y - (currentElement.current.y || 0);
    }
    redraw();
  };

  const handleMouseUp = () => {
    if (!isDrawing || !currentElement.current) return;
    setElements((prev) => [...prev, currentElement.current!]);
    currentElement.current = null;
    setIsDrawing(false);
    redraw();
  };

  const handleUndo = () => setElements((prev) => prev.slice(0, -1));
  const handleClear = () => setElements([]);

  const handleShare = () => {
    const canvas = canvasRef.current;
    if (!canvas) return;
    const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png');
    onShareToChannel(dataUrl);
    toast.success('Canvas shared to channel!');
  };

  const tools: { tool: Tool; icon: typeof Pencil; label: string }[] = [
    { tool: 'pen', icon: Pencil, label: 'Pen' },
    { tool: 'eraser', icon: Eraser, label: 'Eraser' },
    { tool: 'rect', icon: Square, label: 'Rectangle' },
    { tool: 'circle', icon: Circle, label: 'Circle' },
    { tool: 'line', icon: Minus, label: 'Line' },
    { tool: 'arrow', icon: ArrowRight, label: 'Arrow' },
    { tool: 'sticky', icon: StickyNote, label: 'Sticky Note' },
    { tool: 'text', icon: Type, label: 'Text' },
  ];

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      exit={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
      className='fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-background/95 backdrop-blur-sm flex flex-col'
    >
      {/* Toolbar */}
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b border-border bg-card'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-1'>
          {tools.map(({ tool: t, icon: Icon, label }) => (
            <button
              key={t}
              onClick={() => setTool(t)}
              title={label}
              className={`p-2 rounded-lg transition-colors ${tool === t ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground' : 'text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent'}`}
            >
              <Icon className='w-4 h-4' />
            </button>
          ))}
          <div className='w-px h-6 bg-border mx-1' />
          <div className='relative'>
            <button
              onClick={() => setShowColorPicker(!showColorPicker)}
              className='p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent'
            >
              <div
                className='w-4 h-4 rounded-full border-2 border-foreground/20'
                style={{ backgroundColor: color }}
              />
            </button>
            {showColorPicker && (
              <div className='absolute top-full mt-1 left-0 bg-card border border-border rounded-lg p-2 flex gap-1 z-10 shadow-lg'>
                {COLORS.map((c) => (
                  <button
                    key={c}
                    onClick={() => {
                      setColor(c);
                      setShowColorPicker(false);
                    }}
                    className={`w-6 h-6 rounded-full border-2 transition-transform hover:scale-110 ${color === c ? 'border-foreground scale-110' : 'border-transparent'}`}
                    style={{ backgroundColor: c }}
                  />
                ))}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <input
            type='range'
            min={1}
            max={8}
            value={lineWidth}
            onChange={(e) => setLineWidth(+e.target.value)}
            className='w-20 h-1 accent-primary'
            title='Brush size'
          />
        </div>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-1'>
          <button
            onClick={handleUndo}
            className='p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
            title='Undo'
          >
            <Undo className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={handleClear}
            className='p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
            title='Clear'
          >
            <Trash2 className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={handleShare}
            className='flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-sm hover:bg-primary/90'
          >
            <Send className='w-3.5 h-3.5' /> Share
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={onClose}
            className='p-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
          >
            <X className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Canvas */}
      <div className='flex-1 overflow-hidden'>
        <canvas
          ref={canvasRef}
          width={1200}
          height={800}
          onMouseDown={handleMouseDown}
          onMouseMove={handleMouseMove}
          onMouseUp={handleMouseUp}
          onMouseLeave={handleMouseUp}
          className='w-full h-full cursor-crosshair'
          style={{ touchAction: 'none' }}
        />
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

import { useState, useRef, useEffect, useCallback, Fragment } from 'react';
import { AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  Hash,
  Lock,
  Users,
  Pin,
  Search,
  Video,
  Megaphone,
  Loader2,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { useAuthUser } from '@/app/selectors';
import { useGetChannels } from '@/hooks/channel/useGetChannels';
import { useGetMessages } from '@/hooks/messages/useGetMessages';
import { useSendMessage } from '@/hooks/messages/useSendMessage';
import { MessageItem } from './MessageItem';
import { MessageInput } from './MessageInput';
import { HuddleOverlay } from './HuddleOverlay';
import { TypingIndicator } from './TypingIndicator';
import type { Message } from '@/data/mockData';

// ─── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const formatDateDivider = (dateStr: string) => {
  const d = new Date(dateStr);
  const today = new Date();
  const yesterday = new Date(today);
  yesterday.setDate(yesterday.getDate() - 1);
  if (d.toDateString() === today.toDateString()) return 'Today';
  if (d.toDateString() === yesterday.toDateString()) return 'Yesterday';
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
    weekday: 'long',
    month: 'short',
    day: 'numeric',
  });
};

const groupByDate = (messages: Message[]) => {
  const groups: { date: string; messages: Message[] }[] = [];
  messages.forEach((msg) => {
    const date = new Date(msg.timestamp).toDateString();
    const last = groups[groups.length - 1];
    if (last && last.date === date) last.messages.push(msg);
    else groups.push({ date, messages: [msg] });
  });
  return groups;
};

// ─── ChannelView ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export const ChannelView = () => {
  // ── UI context ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const { setRightPanel, setSearchOpen } = useUI();

  // ── Auth ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const authUser = useAuthUser();

  // ── Redux state ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const currentChannelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);

  // ── Server data ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const { data: channels = [] } = useGetChannels();
  const currentChannel =
    channels.find((c) => c.id === currentChannelId) ?? null;

  const { data: messages = [], isLoading: loadingMessages } = useGetMessages();

  const { mutate: sendMessageMutate } = useSendMessage();

  // ── Local state ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [editingId, setEditingId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [newMsgIds, setNewMsgIds] = useState<Set<string>>(new Set());
  const [huddleOpen, setHuddleOpen] = useState(false);

  // ── Refs ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const messagesEndRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const scrollContainerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const shouldScrollRef = useRef(true);

  // ── Auto-scroll on new messages ───────────────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (shouldScrollRef.current) {
      messagesEndRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
    }
  }, [messages.length]);

  // ── Infinite scroll handler ───────────────────────────────────────────────
  // Note: loadEarlierMessages will be wired to a TanStack Query cursor-based
  // query when the backend pagination endpoint is ready. For now it's a no-op
  // placeholder that matches the original contract.
  const handleScroll = useCallback(() => {
    const el = scrollContainerRef.current;
    if (!el) return;
    const nearBottom = el.scrollHeight - el.scrollTop - el.clientHeight < 100;
    shouldScrollRef.current = nearBottom;
    // TODO: trigger loadEarlierMessages when el.scrollTop < 50
  }, []);

  // ── Send handler ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleSend = useCallback(
    (content: string) => {
      shouldScrollRef.current = true;
      const tempId = `temp_${Date.now()}`;
      sendMessageMutate({ content });
      setNewMsgIds((prev) => new Set(prev).add(tempId));
      setTimeout(() => {
        setNewMsgIds((prev) => {
          const n = new Set(prev);
          n.delete(tempId);
          return n;
        });
      }, 500);
    },
    [sendMessageMutate],
  );

  // ── Edit last own message on ArrowUp ─────────────────────────────────────
  const handleEditLast = useCallback(() => {
    const ownMessages = messages.filter(
      (m) => m.authorId === authUser?.id && !m.isSystem,
    );
    if (ownMessages.length > 0) {
      setEditingId(ownMessages[ownMessages.length - 1].id);
    }
  }, [messages, authUser?.id]);

  // ── Empty state ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  if (!currentChannel) {
    return (
      <div className='flex-1 flex items-center justify-center'>
        <div className='text-center text-muted-foreground'>
          <Hash className='w-12 h-12 mx-auto mb-3 opacity-30' />
          <p className='text-lg font-heading'>Select a channel</p>
          <p className='text-sm'>
            Choose a channel from the sidebar to start chatting
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const groupedMessages = groupByDate(messages);

  // ── Render ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  return (
    <div className='flex flex-col h-full'>
      {/* ── Channel header ──────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      <div className='shrink-0 px-4 py-3 border-b border-border flex items-center gap-3'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2 flex-1 min-w-0'>
          {currentChannel.type === 'announcement' ? (
            <Megaphone className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0' />
          ) : currentChannel.isPrivate ? (
            <Lock className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0' />
          ) : (
            <Hash className='w-5 h-5 text-muted-foreground shrink-0' />
          )}
          <h2 className='font-heading font-bold text-foreground truncate'>
            {currentChannel.name}
          </h2>
          {currentChannel.description && (
            <>
              <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground hidden sm:inline'>
                |
              </span>
              <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate hidden sm:inline'>
                {currentChannel.description}
              </span>
            </>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className='flex items-center gap-1 shrink-0'>
          <button
            onClick={() => setRightPanel('members')}
            className='p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
            title='Members'
          >
            <Users className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => setRightPanel('pinned')}
            className='p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors flex items-center gap-1'
            title={`${currentChannel.pinnedMessages.length} pinned`}
          >
            <Pin className='w-4 h-4' />
            {currentChannel.pinnedMessages.length > 0 && (
              <span className='text-xs'>
                {currentChannel.pinnedMessages.length}
              </span>
            )}
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => setSearchOpen(true)}
            className='p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
            title='Search'
          >
            <Search className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => setHuddleOpen(true)}
            className='p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
            title='Start huddle'
          >
            <Video className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* ── Messages ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      <div
        ref={scrollContainerRef}
        onScroll={handleScroll}
        className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-2'
      >
        {loadingMessages && (
          <div className='flex items-center justify-center py-3'>
            <Loader2 className='w-4 h-4 animate-spin text-muted-foreground mr-2' />
            <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
              Loading earlier messages…
            </span>
          </div>
        )}

        <AnimatePresence mode='popLayout'>
          {groupedMessages.map((group) => (
            <div key={group.date}>
              {/* Date divider */}
              <div className='flex items-center gap-3 my-4'>
                <div className='flex-1 h-px bg-border' />
                <span className='text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground px-2 py-1 rounded-full border border-border bg-card'>
                  {formatDateDivider(group.messages[0].timestamp)}
                </span>
                <div className='flex-1 h-px bg-border' />
              </div>

              {group.messages.map((msg, idx) => {
                const prevMsg = idx > 0 ? group.messages[idx - 1] : null;
                const sameAuthor =
                  prevMsg &&
                  prevMsg.authorId === msg.authorId &&
                  !msg.isSystem &&
                  !prevMsg.isSystem;
                const timeDiff = prevMsg
                  ? (new Date(msg.timestamp).getTime() -
                      new Date(prevMsg.timestamp).getTime()) /
                    60000
                  : Infinity;
                const collapsed = !!(sameAuthor && timeDiff < 5);

                return (
                  <Fragment key={msg.id}>
                    <MessageItem
                      message={msg}
                      collapsed={collapsed}
                      isOwn={msg.authorId === authUser?.id}
                      editing={editingId === msg.id}
                      onStartEdit={() => setEditingId(msg.id)}
                      onCancelEdit={() => setEditingId(null)}
                      isNew={newMsgIds.has(msg.id)}
                    />
                  </Fragment>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          ))}
        </AnimatePresence>

        <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
      </div>

      {/* ── Typing indicator ────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      <TypingIndicator channelId={currentChannel.id} />

      {/* ── Message input ───────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
      <MessageInput
        placeholder={`Message #${currentChannel.name}`}
        onSend={handleSend}
        onEditLast={handleEditLast}
      />

      <HuddleOverlay
        open={huddleOpen}
        onClose={() => setHuddleOpen(false)}
        channelName={currentChannel.name}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Hash, Video } from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';
import { MessageItem } from './MessageItem';
import { MessageInput } from './MessageInput';

const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
  online: 'bg-online',
  away: 'bg-away',
  dnd: 'bg-dnd',
  offline: 'bg-muted-foreground',
};

const formatDateDivider = (dateStr: string) => {
  const d = new Date(dateStr);
  const today = new Date();
  const yesterday = new Date(today);
  yesterday.setDate(yesterday.getDate() - 1);
  if (d.toDateString() === today.toDateString()) return 'Today';
  if (d.toDateString() === yesterday.toDateString()) return 'Yesterday';
  return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
    weekday: 'long',
    month: 'short',
    day: 'numeric',
  });
};

export const DMView = () => {
  const { currentDM, dmMessages, sendDMMessage, getUser, currentWorkspace } =
    useWorkspace();
  const { openProfile } = useUI();
  const { auth } = useAuth();
  const endRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [editingId, setEditingId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    endRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  }, [dmMessages.length]);

  if (!currentDM) {
    return (
      <div className='flex-1 flex items-center justify-center'>
        <div className='text-center text-muted-foreground'>
          <svg
            className='w-16 h-16 mx-auto mb-4 opacity-20'
            viewBox='0 0 64 64'
            fill='none'
          >
            <rect
              x='8'
              y='16'
              width='48'
              height='32'
              rx='4'
              stroke='currentColor'
              strokeWidth='2'
            />
            <path d='M8 20l24 16 24-16' stroke='currentColor' strokeWidth='2' />
          </svg>
          <p className='text-lg font-heading'>No conversation selected</p>
          <p className='text-sm'>
            Choose a DM from the sidebar or start a new one
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const otherId = currentDM.participantIds.find((id) => id !== auth.user?.id);
  const other = otherId ? getUser(otherId) : null;
  if (!other) return null;

  const sharedChannels =
    currentWorkspace?.channels.filter(
      (ch) =>
        ch.members.includes(other.id) &&
        ch.members.includes(auth.user?.id || ''),
    ) || [];

  // Group DM messages by date
  const grouped: { date: string; messages: typeof dmMessages }[] = [];
  dmMessages.forEach((msg) => {
    const date = new Date(msg.timestamp).toDateString();
    const last = grouped[grouped.length - 1];
    if (last && last.date === date) {
      last.messages.push(msg);
    } else {
      grouped.push({ date, messages: [msg] });
    }
  });

  return (
    <div className='flex flex-col h-full'>
      {/* Header */}
      <div className='shrink-0 px-4 py-3 border-b border-border flex items-center gap-3'>
        <div className='relative'>
          <img
            src={other.avatar}
            alt=''
            className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-muted'
          />
          <span
            className={`absolute -bottom-0.5 -right-0.5 w-3 h-3 rounded-full border-2 border-background ${statusColors[other.status]} ${other.status === 'online' ? 'animate-pulse-dot' : ''}`}
          />
        </div>
        <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
          <h2 className='font-heading font-bold text-foreground truncate text-sm'>
            {other.displayName}
          </h2>
          {sharedChannels.length > 0 && (
            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate'>
              Also in{' '}
              {sharedChannels
                .slice(0, 3)
                .map((c) => `#${c.name}`)
                .join(', ')}
            </p>
          )}
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => openProfile(other.id)}
          className='text-xs text-primary hover:underline'
        >
          View Profile
        </button>
        <button className='p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'>
          <Video className='w-4 h-4' />
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Messages with date dividers and grouping */}
      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-2'>
        {grouped.length === 0 ? (
          <div className='flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center'>
            <div className='w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-muted/50 flex items-center justify-center mb-3'>
              <img
                src={other.avatar}
                alt=''
                className='w-12 h-12 rounded-full'
              />
            </div>
            <p className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>
              {other.displayName}
            </p>
            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1'>
              This is the very beginning of your DM with {other.displayName}
            </p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          grouped.map((group) => (
            <div key={group.date}>
              <div className='flex items-center gap-3 my-4'>
                <div className='flex-1 h-px bg-border' />
                <span className='text-xs font-medium text-muted-foreground px-2 py-1 rounded-full border border-border bg-card'>
                  {formatDateDivider(group.messages[0].timestamp)}
                </span>
                <div className='flex-1 h-px bg-border' />
              </div>
              {group.messages.map((msg, idx) => {
                const prevMsg = idx > 0 ? group.messages[idx - 1] : null;
                const sameAuthor = prevMsg && prevMsg.authorId === msg.authorId;
                const timeDiff = prevMsg
                  ? (new Date(msg.timestamp).getTime() -
                      new Date(prevMsg.timestamp).getTime()) /
                    60000
                  : Infinity;
                const collapsed = !!(sameAuthor && timeDiff < 5);

                return (
                  <MessageItem
                    key={msg.id}
                    message={msg}
                    collapsed={collapsed}
                    isOwn={msg.authorId === auth.user?.id}
                    editing={editingId === msg.id}
                    onStartEdit={() => setEditingId(msg.id)}
                    onCancelEdit={() => setEditingId(null)}
                  />
                );
              })}
            </div>
          ))
        )}
        <div ref={endRef} />
      </div>

      <MessageInput
        placeholder={`Message ${other.displayName}`}
        onSend={sendDMMessage}
      />
    </div>
  );
};


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\DocsPanel.tsx
==============================

import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  FileText,
  Plus,
  X,
  Save,
  Share,
  Trash2,
  Heading1,
  Heading2,
  List,
  Code,
  Minus as Divider,
  Type,
  Image,
  ChevronLeft,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

type BlockType =
  | 'paragraph'
  | 'heading1'
  | 'heading2'
  | 'bullet'
  | 'code'
  | 'divider'
  | 'image';
interface Block {
  id: string;
  type: BlockType;
  content: string;
}
interface Doc {
  id: string;
  title: string;
  channelId: string;
  blocks: Block[];
  updatedAt: string;
}

const genId = () => `${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6)}`;

const loadDocs = (channelId: string): Doc[] => {
  try {
    return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(`linkly_docs_${channelId}`) || '[]');
  } catch {
    return [];
  }
};
const saveDocs = (channelId: string, docs: Doc[]) => {
  localStorage.setItem(`linkly_docs_${channelId}`, JSON.stringify(docs));
};

export const DocsPanel = ({
  onClose,
  onShareToChannel,
}: {
  onClose: () => void;
  onShareToChannel: (title: string) => void;
}) => {
  const { currentChannel } = useWorkspace();
  const channelId = currentChannel?.id || '';
  const [docs, setDocs] = useState<Doc[]>([]);
  const [activeDocId, setActiveDocId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    setDocs(loadDocs(channelId));
    setActiveDocId(null);
  }, [channelId]);

  const activeDoc = docs.find((d) => d.id === activeDocId);

  const createDoc = () => {
    const doc: Doc = {
      id: genId(),
      title: 'Untitled',
      channelId,
      blocks: [{ id: genId(), type: 'paragraph', content: '' }],
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };
    const updated = [...docs, doc];
    setDocs(updated);
    saveDocs(channelId, updated);
    setActiveDocId(doc.id);
  };

  const updateDoc = useCallback(
    (docId: string, changes: Partial<Doc>) => {
      setDocs((prev) => {
        const updated = prev.map((d) =>
          d.id === docId
            ? { ...d, ...changes, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() }
            : d,
        );
        saveDocs(channelId, updated);
        return updated;
      });
    },
    [channelId],
  );

  const deleteDoc = (docId: string) => {
    setDocs((prev) => {
      const updated = prev.filter((d) => d.id !== docId);
      saveDocs(channelId, updated);
      return updated;
    });
    if (activeDocId === docId) setActiveDocId(null);
    toast.success('Document deleted');
  };

  const updateBlock = (blockId: string, changes: Partial<Block>) => {
    if (!activeDoc) return;
    updateDoc(activeDoc.id, {
      blocks: activeDoc.blocks.map((b) =>
        b.id === blockId ? { ...b, ...changes } : b,
      ),
    });
  };

  const addBlock = (afterId: string, type: BlockType = 'paragraph') => {
    if (!activeDoc) return;
    const idx = activeDoc.blocks.findIndex((b) => b.id === afterId);
    const newBlock: Block = { id: genId(), type, content: '' };
    const blocks = [...activeDoc.blocks];
    blocks.splice(idx + 1, 0, newBlock);
    updateDoc(activeDoc.id, { blocks });
    setTimeout(
      () => document.getElementById(`block-${newBlock.id}`)?.focus(),
      50,
    );
  };

  const removeBlock = (blockId: string) => {
    if (!activeDoc || activeDoc.blocks.length <= 1) return;
    updateDoc(activeDoc.id, {
      blocks: activeDoc.blocks.filter((b) => b.id !== blockId),
    });
  };

  const handleBlockKeyDown = (e: React.KeyboardEvent, block: Block) => {
    if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey && block.type !== 'code') {
      e.preventDefault();
      addBlock(block.id);
    }
    if (
      e.key === 'Backspace' &&
      block.content === '' &&
      activeDoc &&
      activeDoc.blocks.length > 1
    ) {
      e.preventDefault();
      removeBlock(block.id);
    }
  };

  const handleShare = () => {
    if (!activeDoc) return;
    onShareToChannel(`📄 **${activeDoc.title}** — [Open Document]`);
    toast.success('Document link shared!');
  };

  const blockTools: { type: BlockType; icon: typeof Type; label: string }[] = [
    { type: 'heading1', icon: Heading1, label: 'H1' },
    { type: 'heading2', icon: Heading2, label: 'H2' },
    { type: 'paragraph', icon: Type, label: 'Text' },
    { type: 'bullet', icon: List, label: 'Bullet' },
    { type: 'code', icon: Code, label: 'Code' },
    { type: 'divider', icon: Divider, label: 'Divider' },
  ];

  // Doc list view
  if (!activeDoc) {
    return (
      <motion.div
        initial={{ x: '100%' }}
        animate={{ x: 0 }}
        exit={{ x: '100%' }}
        transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
        className='h-full flex flex-col bg-card border-l border-border'
      >
        <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border'>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
            <FileText className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
            <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>Documents</h3>
          </div>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-1'>
            <button
              onClick={createDoc}
              className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-primary transition-colors'
              title='New doc'
            >
              <Plus className='w-4 h-4' />
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={onClose}
              className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
            >
              <X className='w-4 h-4' />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4'>
          {docs.length === 0 ? (
            <div className='flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center'>
              <div className='w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center mb-3'>
                <FileText className='w-6 h-6 text-primary' />
              </div>
              <p className='text-sm font-medium mb-1'>No documents yet</p>
              <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mb-3'>
                Create a document to collaborate with your team
              </p>
              <button
                onClick={createDoc}
                className='text-sm px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90'
              >
                Create Document
              </button>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div className='space-y-2'>
              {docs.map((doc) => (
                <motion.div
                  key={doc.id}
                  initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
                  className='group flex items-center gap-3 px-3 py-2.5 rounded-lg border border-border hover:bg-accent/30 cursor-pointer transition-colors'
                  onClick={() => setActiveDocId(doc.id)}
                >
                  <FileText className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0' />
                  <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
                    <p className='text-sm font-medium truncate'>{doc.title}</p>
                    <p className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                      {new Date(doc.updatedAt).toLocaleDateString()}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <button
                    onClick={(e) => {
                      e.stopPropagation();
                      deleteDoc(doc.id);
                    }}
                    className='p-1 rounded hover:bg-destructive/10 text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all'
                  >
                    <Trash2 className='w-3 h-3' />
                  </button>
                </motion.div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    );
  }

  // Editor view
  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ x: '100%' }}
      animate={{ x: 0 }}
      exit={{ x: '100%' }}
      transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
      className='h-full flex flex-col bg-card border-l border-border'
    >
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
          <button
            onClick={() => setActiveDocId(null)}
            className='p-1 rounded hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
          >
            <ChevronLeft className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
          <FileText className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
          <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>Auto-saved</span>
        </div>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-1'>
          <button
            onClick={handleShare}
            className='flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-1 rounded-md text-xs bg-primary text-primary-foreground hover:bg-primary/90'
          >
            <Share className='w-3 h-3' /> Share
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={onClose}
            className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground'
          >
            <X className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Title */}
      <div className='px-4 pt-4'>
        <input
          value={activeDoc.title}
          onChange={(e) => updateDoc(activeDoc.id, { title: e.target.value })}
          className='w-full text-xl font-heading font-bold bg-transparent border-none focus:outline-none placeholder:text-muted-foreground'
          placeholder='Untitled'
        />
      </div>

      {/* Block type toolbar */}
      <div className='flex items-center gap-0.5 px-4 py-2 border-b border-border'>
        {blockTools.map(({ type, icon: Icon, label }) => (
          <button
            key={type}
            onClick={() => {
              if (activeDoc.blocks.length > 0) {
                const last = activeDoc.blocks[activeDoc.blocks.length - 1];
                addBlock(last.id, type);
              }
            }}
            title={label}
            className='p-1.5 rounded hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors'
          >
            <Icon className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Blocks */}
      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-3 space-y-1'>
        {activeDoc.blocks.map((block) => {
          if (block.type === 'divider') {
            return (
              <div key={block.id} className='py-2'>
                <hr className='border-border' />
              </div>
            );
          }
          const className =
            {
              heading1: 'text-2xl font-heading font-bold',
              heading2: 'text-lg font-heading font-semibold',
              paragraph: 'text-sm',
              bullet:
                "text-sm pl-4 before:content-['•'] before:absolute before:left-0 before:text-muted-foreground relative",
              code: 'text-sm font-mono bg-muted rounded-md px-3 py-2',
              image: 'text-sm',
            }[block.type] || 'text-sm';

          return (
            <div key={block.id} className='group relative'>
              {block.type === 'code' ? (
                <textarea
                  id={`block-${block.id}`}
                  value={block.content}
                  onChange={(e) =>
                    updateBlock(block.id, { content: e.target.value })
                  }
                  onKeyDown={(e) => {
                    if (e.key === 'Backspace' && block.content === '') {
                      e.preventDefault();
                      removeBlock(block.id);
                    }
                  }}
                  className={`w-full bg-muted border-none resize-none focus:outline-none focus:ring-1 focus:ring-ring ${className}`}
                  rows={3}
                  placeholder='Code...'
                />
              ) : (
                <div
                  id={`block-${block.id}`}
                  contentEditable
                  suppressContentEditableWarning
                  onInput={(e) =>
                    updateBlock(block.id, {
                      content: (e.target as HTMLElement).textContent || '',
                    })
                  }
                  onKeyDown={(e) => handleBlockKeyDown(e, block)}
                  className={`w-full focus:outline-none empty:before:content-[attr(data-placeholder)] empty:before:text-muted-foreground ${className}`}
                  data-placeholder={
                    block.type === 'heading1'
                      ? 'Heading 1'
                      : block.type === 'heading2'
                        ? 'Heading 2'
                        : 'Type something...'
                  }
                  dangerouslySetInnerHTML={{ __html: block.content }}
                />
              )}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\GoalsPanel.tsx
