import React from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { X, Pin } from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';
import { MessageItem } from './MessageItem';

export const PinnedMessagesPanel = () => {
  const { currentChannel, messages } = useWorkspace();
  const { setRightPanel } = useUI();
  const { auth } = useAuth();

  if (!currentChannel) return null;

  const pinnedMessages = messages.filter((m) =>
    currentChannel.pinnedMessages.includes(m.id),
  );

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ x: '100%' }}
      animate={{ x: 0 }}
      exit={{ x: '100%' }}
      transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
      className='h-full flex flex-col bg-card border-l border-border'
    >
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border shrink-0'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
          <Pin className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
          <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>Pinned Messages</h3>
          <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
            ({pinnedMessages.length})
          </span>
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={() => setRightPanel(null)}
          className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
        >
          <X className='w-4 h-4' />
        </button>
      </div>

      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-2 py-2'>
        {pinnedMessages.length === 0 ? (
          <div className='flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center p-4'>
            <Pin className='w-8 h-8 text-muted-foreground/30 mb-2' />
            <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>No pinned messages</p>
            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground/60 mt-1'>
              Pin important messages to find them later
            </p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          pinnedMessages.map((msg) => (
            <div
              key={msg.id}
              className='border-b border-border pb-2 mb-2 last:border-0'
            >
              <MessageItem
                message={msg}
                collapsed={false}
                isOwn={msg.authorId === auth.user?.id}
                editing={false}
                onStartEdit={() => {}}
                onCancelEdit={() => {}}
                compact
              />
            </div>
          ))
        )}
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\PollCard.tsx
==============================

import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { BarChart3, Clock, Users, Eye, EyeOff, Check } from 'lucide-react';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { mockApi } from '@/lib/mockApi';
import type { Poll } from '@/data/mockData';

interface PollCardProps {
  pollId: string;
}

export const PollCard = ({ pollId }: PollCardProps) => {
  const { auth } = useAuth();
  const { getUser } = useWorkspace();
  const [poll, setPoll] = useState<Poll | null>(null);
  const [hoveredOption, setHoveredOption] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [showVoters, setShowVoters] = useState<string | null>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    mockApi.polls.get(pollId).then(setPoll);
  }, [pollId]);

  if (!poll) return null;

  const userId = auth.user?.id || 'u1';
  const totalVotes = poll.options.reduce((sum, o) => sum + o.votes.length, 0);
  const userVoted = poll.options.some((o) => o.votes.includes(userId));
  const isExpired = poll.endDate ? new Date(poll.endDate) < new Date() : false;

  const handleVote = async (optionId: string) => {
    if (isExpired) return;
    const updated = await mockApi.polls.vote(pollId, optionId, userId);
    setPoll(updated);
  };

  const formatEndDate = (date: string) => {
    const d = new Date(date);
    const diff = d.getTime() - Date.now();
    if (diff <= 0) return 'Ended';
    const hours = Math.floor(diff / (1000 * 60 * 60));
    if (hours < 24) return `${hours}h remaining`;
    return `${Math.floor(hours / 24)}d remaining`;
  };

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
      animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
      className='mt-2 rounded-xl border border-border bg-card/80 backdrop-blur-sm overflow-hidden max-w-[420px]'
    >
      {/* Header */}
      <div className='px-4 pt-3 pb-2 flex items-start gap-2'>
        <div className='p-1.5 rounded-lg bg-primary/10 text-primary shrink-0'>
          <BarChart3 className='w-4 h-4' />
        </div>
        <div className='flex-1 min-w-0'>
          <h4 className='font-semibold text-sm text-foreground'>
            {poll.question}
          </h4>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-3 mt-1 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
            <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
              <Users className='w-3 h-3' />
              {totalVotes} vote{totalVotes !== 1 ? 's' : ''}
            </span>
            {poll.anonymous && (
              <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
                <EyeOff className='w-3 h-3' />
                Anonymous
              </span>
            )}
            {poll.endDate && (
              <span className='flex items-center gap-1'>
                <Clock className='w-3 h-3' />
                {formatEndDate(poll.endDate)}
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Options */}
      <div className='px-4 pb-3 space-y-1.5'>
        {poll.options.map((option) => {
          const pct =
            totalVotes > 0 ? (option.votes.length / totalVotes) * 100 : 0;
          const hasVoted = option.votes.includes(userId);

          return (
            <div key={option.id}>
              <button
                onClick={() => handleVote(option.id)}
                onMouseEnter={() => setHoveredOption(option.id)}
                onMouseLeave={() => setHoveredOption(null)}
                disabled={isExpired}
                className={`relative w-full text-left rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm transition-all overflow-hidden ${
                  hasVoted
                    ? 'border border-primary/40 bg-primary/5'
                    : 'border border-border hover:border-primary/30 hover:bg-accent/30'
                } ${isExpired ? 'opacity-60 cursor-default' : 'cursor-pointer'}`}
              >
                {/* Progress bar background */}
                {(userVoted || isExpired) && (
                  <motion.div
                    initial={{ width: 0 }}
                    animate={{ width: `${pct}%` }}
                    transition={{ duration: 0.8, ease: 'easeOut', delay: 0.1 }}
                    className={`absolute inset-y-0 left-0 ${hasVoted ? 'bg-primary/15' : 'bg-muted/50'} rounded-lg`}
                  />
                )}
                <div className='relative flex items-center gap-2'>
                  {hasVoted && (
                    <Check className='w-3.5 h-3.5 text-primary shrink-0' />
                  )}
                  <span
                    className={`flex-1 ${hasVoted ? 'text-primary font-medium' : 'text-foreground'}`}
                  >
                    {option.text}
                  </span>
                  {(userVoted || isExpired) && (
                    <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground font-mono shrink-0'>
                      {Math.round(pct)}%
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
              </button>

              {/* Voter avatars on hover */}
              {!poll.anonymous &&
                hoveredOption === option.id &&
                option.votes.length > 0 && (
                  <motion.div
                    initial={{ opacity: 0, height: 0 }}
                    animate={{ opacity: 1, height: 'auto' }}
                    className='flex items-center gap-1 mt-1 ml-2'
                  >
                    {option.votes.slice(0, 5).map((vId) => {
                      const voter = getUser(vId);
                      return (
                        <img
                          key={vId}
                          src={voter?.avatar || ''}
                          title={voter?.displayName}
                          className='w-5 h-5 rounded-full border border-background'
                          alt=''
                        />
                      );
                    })}
                    {option.votes.length > 5 && (
                      <span className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                        +{option.votes.length - 5}
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </motion.div>
                )}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

import React from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { X, MessageSquare, Clock, Hash, MapPin } from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';

const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
  online: 'bg-online',
  away: 'bg-away',
  dnd: 'bg-dnd',
  offline: 'bg-muted-foreground',
};
const statusLabels: Record<string, string> = {
  online: 'Active',
  away: 'Away',
  dnd: 'Do Not Disturb',
  offline: 'Offline',
};

export const ProfilePanel = ({
  onViewFullProfile,
}: {
  onViewFullProfile?: (id: string) => void;
}) => {
  const { getUser, currentWorkspace, setCurrentDMId } = useWorkspace();
  const { profileUserId, closeProfile } = useUI();
  const { auth } = useAuth();

  const user = profileUserId ? getUser(profileUserId) : null;
  if (!user) return null;

  const sharedChannels =
    currentWorkspace?.channels.filter(
      (ch) =>
        ch.members.includes(user.id) &&
        ch.members.includes(auth.user?.id || ''),
    ) || [];

  const handleMessage = () => {
    const dm = currentWorkspace?.dms.find(
      (d) =>
        d.participantIds.includes(user.id) &&
        d.participantIds.includes(auth.user?.id || ''),
    );
    if (dm) setCurrentDMId(dm.id);
    closeProfile();
  };

  const localTime = new Date().toLocaleTimeString('en-US', {
    hour: 'numeric',
    minute: '2-digit',
    timeZone: user.timezone,
  });

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ x: '100%' }}
      animate={{ x: 0 }}
      exit={{ x: '100%' }}
      transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
      className='h-full flex flex-col bg-card border-l border-border'
    >
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border shrink-0'>
        <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>Profile</h3>
        <button
          onClick={closeProfile}
          className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
        >
          <X className='w-4 h-4' />
        </button>
      </div>

      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto p-4 space-y-4'>
        {/* Avatar */}
        <div className='flex flex-col items-center text-center'>
          <div className='relative'>
            <img
              src={user.avatar}
              alt=''
              className='w-20 h-20 rounded-full bg-muted'
            />
            <span
              className={`absolute bottom-1 right-1 w-4 h-4 rounded-full border-2 border-card ${statusColors[user.status]}`}
            />
          </div>
          <h2 className='font-heading font-bold text-lg mt-3'>
            {user.displayName}
          </h2>
          <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>@{user.username}</p>
          {user.statusEmoji && (
            <p className='text-sm mt-1'>
              <span>{user.statusEmoji}</span>{' '}
              <span className='text-muted-foreground'>{user.statusText}</span>
            </p>
          )}
          <span
            className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs mt-2 px-2 py-1 rounded-full ${statusColors[user.status]}/10 text-foreground`}
          >
            <span
              className={`w-2 h-2 rounded-full ${statusColors[user.status]}`}
            />
            {statusLabels[user.status]}
          </span>
        </div>

        {/* View Full Profile + Message */}
        {onViewFullProfile && (
          <button
            onClick={() => onViewFullProfile(user.id)}
            className='w-full flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-2 rounded-md border border-border text-sm font-medium hover:bg-accent transition-colors text-muted-foreground'
          >
            View Full Profile
          </button>
        )}
        {user.id !== auth.user?.id && (
          <button
            onClick={handleMessage}
            className='w-full flex items-center justify-center gap-2 py-2 rounded-md bg-primary text-primary-foreground text-sm font-medium hover:bg-primary/90 transition-colors'
          >
            <MessageSquare className='w-4 h-4' /> Message
          </button>
        )}

        {/* Info */}
        <div className='space-y-3 text-sm'>
          <div>
            <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-1'>
              Title
            </p>
            <p className='text-foreground'>{user.title}</p>
          </div>
          <div>
            <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-1'>
              Bio
            </p>
            <p className='text-foreground/80'>{user.bio}</p>
          </div>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
            <MapPin className='w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground' />
            <span className='text-muted-foreground'>{user.timezone}</span>
          </div>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
            <Clock className='w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground' />
            <span className='text-muted-foreground'>
              Local time: {localTime}
            </span>
          </div>
          <div>
            <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-1'>
              Member since
            </p>
            <p className='text-muted-foreground'>
              {new Date(user.memberSince).toLocaleDateString('en-US', {
                month: 'long',
                year: 'numeric',
              })}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Shared channels */}
        {sharedChannels.length > 0 && (
          <div>
            <p className='text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider mb-2'>
              Shared Channels
            </p>
            <div className='space-y-1'>
              {sharedChannels.map((ch) => (
                <div
                  key={ch.id}
                  className='flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1 rounded-md text-sm text-muted-foreground'
                >
                  <Hash className='w-3.5 h-3.5' /> {ch.name}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\SavedItemsPanel.tsx
==============================

import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { Bookmark, X, Hash, Search, Tag, Download, Trash2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';
import { mockApi } from '@/lib/mockApi';
import type { Message } from '@/data/mockData';

interface SavedItem {
  messageId: string;
  channelId: string;
  channelName: string;
  savedAt: string;
  tags: string[];
}

export const SavedItemsPanel = () => {
  const { setRightPanel } = useUI();
  const {
    getUser,
    messages: currentMessages,
    setCurrentChannelId,
  } = useWorkspace();
  const { auth } = useAuth();
  const [savedItems, setSavedItems] = useState<SavedItem[]>([]);
  const [messageCache, setMessageCache] = useState<Record<string, Message>>({});
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const userId = auth.user?.id || 'u1';

  useEffect(() => {
    setLoading(true);
    mockApi.bookmarks.list(userId).then(async (items) => {
      setSavedItems(items);
      // Fetch messages for each saved item
      const cache: Record<string, Message> = {};
      for (const item of items) {
        const msgs = await mockApi.messages.getAll(item.channelId);
        const msg = msgs.find((m) => m.id === item.messageId);
        if (msg) cache[item.messageId] = msg;
      }
      setMessageCache(cache);
      setLoading(false);
    });
  }, [userId]);

  const handleRemove = async (messageId: string) => {
    await mockApi.bookmarks.toggle(userId, messageId, '', '');
    setSavedItems((prev) => prev.filter((s) => s.messageId !== messageId));
  };

  const handleGoToMessage = (item: SavedItem) => {
    setCurrentChannelId(item.channelId);
    setRightPanel(null);
    // Highlight the message
    setTimeout(() => {
      const el = document.querySelector(
        `[data-message-id="${item.messageId}"]`,
      );
      if (el) {
        el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' });
        el.classList.add('animate-highlight');
        setTimeout(() => el.classList.remove('animate-highlight'), 2500);
      }
    }, 300);
  };

  const handleExportMarkdown = () => {
    const lines = savedItems.map((item) => {
      const msg = messageCache[item.messageId];
      const author = msg
        ? getUser(msg.authorId)?.displayName || 'Unknown'
        : 'Unknown';
      const content = msg?.content || '';
      return `## #${item.channelName}\n**${author}** — ${new Date(item.savedAt).toLocaleDateString()}\n\n${content}\n`;
    });
    const blob = new Blob([`# Saved Items\n\n${lines.join('\n---\n\n')}`], {
      type: 'text/markdown',
    });
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url;
    a.download = 'saved-items.md';
    a.click();
    URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  };

  const filtered = savedItems.filter((item) => {
    if (!searchQuery) return true;
    const msg = messageCache[item.messageId];
    return (
      msg?.content.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase()) ||
      item.channelName.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase())
    );
  });

  // Group by channel
  const grouped = filtered.reduce<Record<string, SavedItem[]>>((acc, item) => {
    if (!acc[item.channelName]) acc[item.channelName] = [];
    acc[item.channelName].push(item);
    return acc;
  }, {});

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ x: '100%' }}
      animate={{ x: 0 }}
      exit={{ x: '100%' }}
      transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
      className='h-full flex flex-col bg-card border-l border-border'
    >
      {/* Header */}
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border shrink-0'>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
          <Bookmark className='w-4 h-4 text-primary' />
          <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>Saved Items</h3>
          <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
            ({savedItems.length})
          </span>
        </div>
        <div className='flex items-center gap-1'>
          {savedItems.length > 0 && (
            <button
              onClick={handleExportMarkdown}
              className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
              title='Export as Markdown'
            >
              <Download className='w-4 h-4' />
            </button>
          )}
          <button
            onClick={() => setRightPanel(null)}
            className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
          >
            <X className='w-4 h-4' />
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Search */}
      {savedItems.length > 0 && (
        <div className='px-4 py-2 border-b border-border'>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md bg-muted/50 border border-border'>
            <Search className='w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground' />
            <input
              value={searchQuery}
              onChange={(e) => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
              placeholder='Search saved items...'
              className='flex-1 bg-transparent text-sm focus:outline-none placeholder:text-muted-foreground'
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Content */}
      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-4 py-3'>
        {loading ? (
          <div className='space-y-3'>
            {[1, 2, 3].map((i) => (
              <div
                key={i}
                className='h-16 rounded-lg bg-muted animate-shimmer'
                style={{ animationDelay: `${i * 0.1}s` }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        ) : savedItems.length === 0 ? (
          <div className='flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center'>
            <div className='w-14 h-14 rounded-2xl bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center mb-3'>
              <Bookmark className='w-6 h-6 text-primary' />
            </div>
            <p className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground mb-1'>
              No saved items yet
            </p>
            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground max-w-[200px]'>
              Bookmark messages to save them here for quick reference
            </p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <AnimatePresence>
            {Object.entries(grouped).map(([channelName, items]) => (
              <div key={channelName} className='mb-4'>
                <div className='flex items-center gap-1.5 mb-2 text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground uppercase tracking-wider'>
                  <Hash className='w-3 h-3' />
                  {channelName}
                </div>
                <div className='space-y-1.5'>
                  {items.map((item) => {
                    const msg = messageCache[item.messageId];
                    const author = msg ? getUser(msg.authorId) : null;
                    return (
                      <motion.div
                        key={item.messageId}
                        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 4 }}
                        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                        exit={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
                        className='group relative rounded-lg border border-border bg-card/50 hover:bg-accent/30 transition-colors cursor-pointer'
                        onClick={() => handleGoToMessage(item)}
                      >
                        <div className='px-3 py-2'>
                          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 mb-1'>
                            {author && (
                              <img
                                src={author.avatar}
                                alt=''
                                className='w-4 h-4 rounded-full'
                              />
                            )}
                            <span className='text-xs font-medium text-foreground'>
                              {author?.displayName || 'Unknown'}
                            </span>
                            <span className='text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
                              {new Date(item.savedAt).toLocaleDateString()}
                            </span>
                          </div>
                          <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground line-clamp-2'>
                            {msg?.content || 'Message not found'}
                          </p>
                        </div>
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => {
                            e.stopPropagation();
                            handleRemove(item.messageId);
                          }}
                          className='absolute top-2 right-2 p-1 rounded hover:bg-destructive/10 text-muted-foreground hover:text-destructive opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all'
                          title='Remove'
                        >
                          <Trash2 className='w-3 h-3' />
                        </button>
                      </motion.div>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </AnimatePresence>
        )}
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\components\workspace\ThreadPanel.tsx
==============================

import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { X, Hash, ChevronDown, Sparkles, Copy, Check } from 'lucide-react';
import { useWorkspace } from '@/context/WorkspaceContext';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';
import { MessageItem } from './MessageItem';
import { MessageInput } from './MessageInput';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

export const ThreadPanel = () => {
  const { messages, addThreadReply, currentChannel, getUser } = useWorkspace();
  const { threadParentId, closeThread } = useUI();
  const { auth } = useAuth();
  const endRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const [collapsed, setCollapsed] = useState(false);
  const [showSummary, setShowSummary] = useState(false);
  const [summaryLoading, setSummaryLoading] = useState(false);
  const [summary, setSummary] = useState('');
  const [summaryCopied, setSummaryCopied] = useState(false);

  const parentMsg = messages.find((m) => m.id === threadParentId);

  useEffect(() => {
    endRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  }, [parentMsg?.thread.length]);

  if (!parentMsg) return null;

  const handleReply = (content: string) => {
    addThreadReply(parentMsg.id, content, auth.user?.id || 'u1');
  };

  const handleSummarize = async () => {
    setSummaryLoading(true);
    setShowSummary(true);
    // Simulate AI thinking
    await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 1500));
    const authorNames = [
      ...new Set(
        parentMsg.thread.map(
          (t) => getUser(t.authorId)?.displayName || 'Someone',
        ),
      ),
    ];
    const topics = parentMsg.thread
      .slice(0, 3)
      .map((t) => t.content.slice(0, 40))
      .join('; ');
    const summaryText = `**TLDR:** ${authorNames.join(', ')} discussed: ${topics.replace(/\n/g, ' ')}... The consensus was to move forward with the proposed approach. Key action items were identified and assigned.`;
    setSummary(summaryText);
    setSummaryLoading(false);
  };

  const handleCopySummary = () => {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(summary.replace(/\*\*/g, ''));
    setSummaryCopied(true);
    toast.success('Summary copied!');
    setTimeout(() => setSummaryCopied(false), 2000);
  };

  const participants = [
    ...new Set([
      parentMsg.authorId,
      ...parentMsg.thread.map((t) => t.authorId),
    ]),
  ];
  const replyCount = parentMsg.thread.length;

  return (
    <motion.div
      initial={{ x: '100%' }}
      animate={{ x: 0 }}
      exit={{ x: '100%' }}
      transition={{ type: 'spring', damping: 25, stiffness: 300 }}
      className='h-full flex flex-col bg-card border-l border-border'
    >
      {/* Header */}
      <div className='flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-border shrink-0'>
        <div>
          <h3 className='font-heading font-bold text-sm'>Thread</h3>
          {currentChannel && (
            <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground flex items-center gap-1'>
              <Hash className='w-3 h-3' />
              {currentChannel.name}
            </span>
          )}
        </div>
        <button
          onClick={closeThread}
          className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
        >
          <X className='w-4 h-4' />
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Parent message (collapsible) */}
      <div className='border-b border-border'>
        <button
          onClick={() => setCollapsed(!collapsed)}
          className='w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent/50 transition-colors'
        >
          <ChevronDown
            className={`w-3 h-3 transition-transform ${collapsed ? '-rotate-90' : ''}`}
          />
          {collapsed ? 'Show original message' : 'Original message'}
        </button>
        <AnimatePresence initial={false}>
          {!collapsed && (
            <motion.div
              initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
              animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
              exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
              className='overflow-hidden px-2 pb-2'
            >
              <MessageItem
                message={parentMsg}
                collapsed={false}
                isOwn={parentMsg.authorId === auth.user?.id}
                editing={false}
                onStartEdit={() => {}}
                onCancelEdit={() => {}}
              />
            </motion.div>
          )}
        </AnimatePresence>
      </div>

      {/* Participants bar */}
      <div className='flex items-center gap-3 px-4 py-2.5 border-b border-border bg-muted/30'>
        <div className='flex -space-x-2'>
          {participants.slice(0, 6).map((id) => {
            const user = getUser(id);
            return (
              <img
                key={id}
                src={user?.avatar || ''}
                title={user?.displayName}
                className='w-6 h-6 rounded-full border-2 border-card hover:scale-110 transition-transform cursor-pointer'
                alt={user?.displayName}
              />
            );
          })}
          {participants.length > 6 && (
            <div className='w-6 h-6 rounded-full border-2 border-card bg-muted flex items-center justify-center text-[10px] font-medium text-muted-foreground'>
              +{participants.length - 6}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
        <div className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
          <span className='font-medium text-foreground'>{replyCount}</span>{' '}
          {replyCount === 1 ? 'reply' : 'replies'} from{' '}
          <span className='font-medium text-foreground'>
            {participants.length}
          </span>{' '}
          {participants.length === 1 ? 'person' : 'people'}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Summary banner */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {showSummary && (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
            exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
            className='border-b border-border overflow-hidden'
          >
            <div className='px-4 py-3 bg-primary/5 border-l-4 border-primary'>
              {summaryLoading ? (
                <div className='flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
                  <Sparkles className='w-4 h-4 animate-pulse text-primary' />
                  <span>Generating summary...</span>
                  <div className='flex gap-0.5 ml-1'>
                    <span className='w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-primary typing-dot-1' />
                    <span className='w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-primary typing-dot-2' />
                    <span className='w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-primary typing-dot-3' />
                  </div>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div>
                  <div className='flex items-center gap-2 mb-1'>
                    <Sparkles className='w-3.5 h-3.5 text-primary' />
                    <span className='text-xs font-semibold text-primary'>
                      AI Summary
                    </span>
                    <div className='ml-auto flex items-center gap-1'>
                      <button
                        onClick={handleCopySummary}
                        className='p-1 rounded hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
                        title='Copy'
                      >
                        {summaryCopied ? (
                          <Check className='w-3 h-3 text-online' />
                        ) : (
                          <Copy className='w-3 h-3' />
                        )}
                      </button>
                      <button
                        onClick={() => setShowSummary(false)}
                        className='p-1 rounded hover:bg-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
                      >
                        <X className='w-3 h-3' />
                      </button>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <p className='text-xs text-foreground/80 leading-relaxed'>
                    {summary}
                  </p>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </motion.div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>

      {/* Summarize button for threads with 5+ replies */}
      {replyCount >= 5 && !showSummary && (
        <div className='px-4 py-2 border-b border-border'>
          <button
            onClick={handleSummarize}
            className='flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs text-primary hover:text-primary/80 transition-colors'
          >
            <Sparkles className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
            Summarize thread
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Thread replies */}
      <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-2 py-2'>
        {replyCount === 0 ? (
          <div className='flex flex-col items-center justify-center h-full text-center px-4'>
            <div className='w-12 h-12 rounded-full bg-primary/10 flex items-center justify-center mb-3'>
              <Hash className='w-5 h-5 text-primary' />
            </div>
            <p className='text-sm font-medium text-foreground mb-1'>
              No replies yet
            </p>
            <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
              Be the first to reply to this thread
            </p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          <AnimatePresence>
            {parentMsg.thread.map((reply, idx) => {
              const prevReply = idx > 0 ? parentMsg.thread[idx - 1] : null;
              const sameAuthor =
                prevReply && prevReply.authorId === reply.authorId;
              const timeDiff = prevReply
                ? (new Date(reply.timestamp).getTime() -
                    new Date(prevReply.timestamp).getTime()) /
                  60000
                : Infinity;
              const isCollapsed = !!(sameAuthor && timeDiff < 5);

              return (
                <motion.div
                  key={reply.id}
                  initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
                  animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                  transition={{ delay: idx * 0.03 }}
                >
                  <MessageItem
                    message={reply}
                    collapsed={isCollapsed}
                    isOwn={reply.authorId === auth.user?.id}
                    editing={false}
                    onStartEdit={() => {}}
                    onCancelEdit={() => {}}
                    compact
                  />
                </motion.div>
              );
            })}
          </AnimatePresence>
        )}
        <div ref={endRef} />
      </div>

      {/* Reply input */}
      <div className='border-t border-border'>
        <div className='px-3 py-1.5 text-[10px] text-muted-foreground'>
          Replying to{' '}
          <span className='font-medium text-foreground'>
            {getUser(parentMsg.authorId)?.displayName}
          </span>
        </div>
        <MessageInput
          placeholder='Reply to thread...'
          onSend={handleReply}
          compact
        />
      </div>
    </motion.div>
  );
};

==============================

import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { mockUsers } from '@/data/mockData';
import { useAuth } from '@/context/AuthContext';

interface TypingIndicatorProps {
  channelId: string | undefined;
}

export const TypingIndicator = ({ channelId }: TypingIndicatorProps) => {
  const { auth } = useAuth();
  const [typingUsers, setTypingUsers] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const intervalRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setInterval>>();

  // Simulate random users typing when channel changes
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!channelId) return;

    const otherUsers = mockUsers.filter(
      (u) => u.id !== auth.user?.id && u.status === 'online',
    );

    const simulateTyping = () => {
      const shouldType = Math.random() > 0.5;
      if (shouldType && otherUsers.length > 0) {
        const count = Math.random() > 0.7 ? 2 : 1;
        const shuffled = [...otherUsers].sort(() => Math.random() - 0.5);
        const selected = shuffled.slice(0, count).map((u) => u.displayName);
        setTypingUsers(selected);

        // Stop typing after 2-4s
        setTimeout(() => setTypingUsers([]), 2000 + Math.random() * 2000);
      }
    };

    // Initial delay then periodic simulation
    const startDelay = setTimeout(() => {
      simulateTyping();
      intervalRef.current = setInterval(
        simulateTyping,
        6000 + Math.random() * 4000,
      );
    }, 3000);

    return () => {
      clearTimeout(startDelay);
      if (intervalRef.current) clearInterval(intervalRef.current);
      setTypingUsers([]);
    };
  }, [channelId, auth.user?.id]);

  const text =
    typingUsers.length === 1
      ? `${typingUsers[0]} is typing`
      : typingUsers.length === 2
        ? `${typingUsers[0]} and ${typingUsers[1]} are typing`
        : null;

  return (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {text && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, height: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, height: 'auto' }}
          exit={{ opacity: 0, height: 0 }}
          transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
          className='px-4 overflow-hidden'
        >
          <div className='flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs text-muted-foreground py-1'>
            <span className='inline-flex gap-0.5'>
              <span className='w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-muted-foreground typing-dot-1' />
              <span className='w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-muted-foreground typing-dot-2' />
              <span className='w-1 h-1 rounded-full bg-muted-foreground typing-dot-3' />
            </span>
            <span className='font-medium'>{text}</span>
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );
};

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import {
  Hash,
  Lock,
  ChevronDown,
  Plus,
  Search,
  Home,
  MessageSquare,
  Bell,
  Settings,
  Volume2,
  VolumeX,
  Megaphone,
  Globe,
  Bookmark,
  FileText,
  Calendar,
  Target,
  BarChart3,
} from 'lucide-react';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { setCurrentChannelId, setCurrentDMId } from '@/features/channelSlice';
import { useGetChannels } from '@/hooks/channel/useGetChannels';
import { useGetWorkspaceUsers } from '@/hooks/users/useGetUsers';
import { useGetWorkspaces } from '@/hooks/workspace/useGetWorkspaces';
import { useAuthUser } from '@/app/selectors';
import { NewDMModal } from '@/components/modals/NewDMModal';
import { NotificationDigest } from '@/components/workspace/NotificationDigest';

// ─── Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
  online: 'bg-online',
  away: 'bg-away',
  dnd: 'bg-dnd',
  offline: 'bg-muted-foreground',
};

/**
 * UI callbacks that still live in your UI context/slice.
 * Once you have a UI slice, these can be replaced with dispatch calls.
 */
interface WorkspaceSidebarProps {
  // Modal openers
  onOpenWorkspaceSwitcher: () => void;
  onOpenCreateChannel: () => void;
  onOpenSearch: () => void;
  onOpenSettings: () => void;
  // Right panel / view navigation
  onSetRightPanel: (panel: string) => void;
  onSetWorkspaceView: (view: string) => void;
  workspaceView: string;
  // Sound
  soundEnabled: boolean;
  onToggleSound: () => void;
  // Mobile
  isMobile: boolean;
  onCloseSidebar: () => void;
  // Profile
  onOpenProfile: (userId: string) => void;
}

// ─── WorkspaceSidebar ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export const WorkspaceSidebar = ({
  onOpenWorkspaceSwitcher,
  onOpenCreateChannel,
  onOpenSearch,
  onOpenSettings,
  onSetRightPanel,
  onSetWorkspaceView,
  workspaceView,
  soundEnabled,
  onToggleSound,
  isMobile,
  onCloseSidebar,
  onOpenProfile,
}: WorkspaceSidebarProps) => {
  // ── Redux ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const currentChannelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);
  const currentDMId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentDMId);
  const unreadCounts = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.unreadCounts);
  const currentWorkspaceId = useAppSelector(
    (s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId,
  );
  const authUser = useAuthUser();

  // ── Server data ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const { data: workspaces } = useGetWorkspaces();
  const { data: channels = [] } = useGetChannels();
  const { data: users = [] } = useGetWorkspaceUsers();

  // ── Local state ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [channelsExpanded, setChannelsExpanded] = useState(true);
  const [dmsExpanded, setDmsExpanded] = useState(true);
  const [newDMOpen, setNewDMOpen] = useState(false);
  const [digestOpen, setDigestOpen] = useState(false);

  // ── Guards ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  // workspaces may be undefined while loading — find only after confirming it's an array
  const currentWorkspace = Array.isArray(workspaces)
    ? (workspaces.find((w) => w.id === currentWorkspaceId) ?? null)
    : null;

  if (!currentWorkspace || !authUser) return null;

  // ── Derived data ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const userId = authUser.id;
  const joinedChannels = channels.filter((ch) => ch.members.includes(userId));

  const getDMPartner = (participantIds: string[]) => {
    const otherId = participantIds.find((id) => id !== userId);
    return otherId ? users.find((u) => u.id === otherId) : null;
  };

  // ── Handlers ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleChannelClick = (channelId: string) => {
    dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(channelId));
    onSetWorkspaceView('chat');
    if (isMobile) onCloseSidebar();
  };

  const handleDMClick = (dmId: string) => {
    dispatch(setCurrentDMId(dmId));
    onSetWorkspaceView('chat');
    if (isMobile) onCloseSidebar();
  };

  const handleHomeClick = () => {
    onSetWorkspaceView('chat');
    const firstChannel = joinedChannels[0];
    if (firstChannel) dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(firstChannel.id));
  };

  const channelIcon = (type: string, isPrivate: boolean) => {
    if (type === 'announcement')
      return <Megaphone className='w-4 h-4 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground' />;
    if (isPrivate)
      return <Lock className='w-4 h-4 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground' />;
    return <Hash className='w-4 h-4 shrink-0 text-muted-foreground' />;
  };

  // ── Render ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  return (
    <>
      <div className='flex flex-col h-full bg-sidebar text-sidebar-foreground'>
        {/* ── Workspace header ──────────────────────────────────────────── */}
        <button
          onClick={onOpenWorkspaceSwitcher}
          className='flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-3 border-b border-sidebar-border hover:bg-sidebar-accent transition-colors'
        >
          <span className='w-8 h-8 rounded-lg bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-secondary flex items-center justify-center text-lg'>
            {currentWorkspace.icon}
          </span>
          <div className='flex-1 text-left min-w-0'>
            <span className='font-heading font-bold text-sidebar-accent-foreground text-sm truncate block'>
              {currentWorkspace.name}
            </span>
            <span className='text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate block'>
              {currentWorkspace.description}
            </span>
          </div>
          <ChevronDown className='w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0' />
        </button>

        {/* ── Search ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
        <div className='px-3 py-2'>
          <button
            onClick={onOpenSearch}
            className='w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-md bg-sidebar-accent text-muted-foreground text-sm hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
          >
            <Search className='w-4 h-4' />
            <span>Search</span>
            <kbd className='ml-auto text-xs bg-muted/50 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded'>
              ⌘K
            </kbd>
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* ── Nav icons ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
        <div className='flex items-center gap-1 px-3 py-1'>
          {[
            { icon: Home, label: 'Home', onClick: handleHomeClick },
            {
              icon: MessageSquare,
              label: 'DMs',
              onClick: () => {
                onSetWorkspaceView('chat');
                setDmsExpanded(true);
              },
            },
            {
              icon: Bookmark,
              label: 'Saved',
              onClick: () => onSetRightPanel('saved'),
            },
          ].map(({ icon: Icon, label, onClick }) => (
            <button
              key={label}
              title={label}
              onClick={onClick}
              className='flex-1 flex items-center justify-center py-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-sidebar-accent transition-colors text-muted-foreground hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground'
            >
              <Icon className='w-4 h-4' />
            </button>
          ))}

          {/* Bell with digest dropdown */}
          <div className='relative flex-1 flex items-center justify-center'>
            <button
              title='Activity'
              onClick={() => setDigestOpen(!digestOpen)}
              className='flex-1 flex items-center justify-center py-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-sidebar-accent transition-colors text-muted-foreground hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground'
            >
              <Bell className='w-4 h-4' />
            </button>
            <AnimatePresence>
              {digestOpen && (
                <NotificationDigest onClose={() => setDigestOpen(false)} />
              )}
            </AnimatePresence>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* ── Scrollable content ────────────────────────────────────────── */}
        <div className='flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-2 py-1 space-y-1'>
          {/* Feature shortcuts */}
          <div className='space-y-0.5 mb-2'>
            {[
              {
                icon: FileText,
                label: 'Docs',
                onClick: () => onSetRightPanel('docs'),
              },
              {
                icon: Calendar,
                label: 'Calendar',
                onClick: () => onSetRightPanel('calendar'),
              },
              {
                icon: Target,
                label: 'Goals',
                onClick: () => onSetWorkspaceView('goals'),
              },
              {
                icon: BarChart3,
                label: 'Analytics',
                onClick: () => onSetWorkspaceView('analytics'),
              },
            ].map(({ icon: Icon, label, onClick }) => (
              <button
                key={label}
                onClick={onClick}
                className='flex items-center gap-2 w-full px-2 py-1 rounded-md text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent transition-colors'
              >
                <Icon className='w-4 h-4 shrink-0' />
                <span>{label}</span>
              </button>
            ))}
          </div>

          {/* ── Channels ──────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div>
            <button
              onClick={() => setChannelsExpanded(!channelsExpanded)}
              className='flex items-center gap-1 w-full px-2 py-1 text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground transition-colors'
            >
              <motion.div
                animate={{ rotate: channelsExpanded ? 0 : -90 }}
                transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
              >
                <ChevronDown className='w-3 h-3' />
              </motion.div>
              <span>Channels</span>
              <button
                onClick={(e) => {
                  e.stopPropagation();
                  onOpenCreateChannel();
                }}
                className='ml-auto p-0.5 rounded hover:bg-sidebar-accent'
              >
                <Plus className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
              </button>
            </button>

            <AnimatePresence>
              {channelsExpanded && (
                <motion.div
                  initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                  animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
                  exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                  transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
                >
                  {joinedChannels.map((ch) => {
                    const unread = unreadCounts[ch.id] ?? 0;
                    const isActive =
                      ch.id === currentChannelId && workspaceView === 'chat';
                    return (
                      <button
                        key={ch.id}
                        onClick={() => handleChannelClick(ch.id)}
                        className={`flex items-center gap-2 w-full px-2 py-1 rounded-md text-sm transition-colors ${
                          isActive
                            ? 'bg-primary/20 text-primary'
                            : 'hover:bg-sidebar-accent text-sidebar-foreground'
                        } ${ch.muted ? 'opacity-50' : ''}`}
                      >
                        {channelIcon(ch.type, ch.isPrivate)}
                        <span
                          className={`truncate ${unread > 0 ? 'font-bold text-foreground' : ''}`}
                        >
                          {ch.name}
                        </span>
                        {unread > 0 && (
                          <motion.span
                            key={unread}
                            initial={{ scale: 1.3 }}
                            animate={{ scale: 1 }}
                            className='ml-auto bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground text-xs px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full min-w-[20px] text-center'
                          >
                            {unread > 99 ? '99+' : unread}
                          </motion.span>
                        )}
                      </button>
                    );
                  })}

                  <button
                    onClick={() =>
                      window.dispatchEvent(
                        new CustomEvent('open-browse-channels'),
                      )
                    }
                    className='flex items-center gap-2 w-full px-2 py-1 rounded-md text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:bg-sidebar-accent transition-colors'
                  >
                    <Globe className='w-4 h-4 shrink-0' />
                    <span>Browse channels</span>
                  </button>
                </motion.div>
              )}
            </AnimatePresence>
          </div>

          {/* ── Direct Messages ───────────────────────────────────────── */}
          <div>
            <button
              onClick={() => setDmsExpanded(!dmsExpanded)}
              className='flex items-center gap-1 w-full px-2 py-1 text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground hover:text-sidebar-accent-foreground transition-colors'
            >
              <motion.div
                animate={{ rotate: dmsExpanded ? 0 : -90 }}
                transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
              >
                <ChevronDown className='w-3 h-3' />
              </motion.div>
              <span>Direct Messages</span>
              <button
                onClick={(e) => {
                  e.stopPropagation();
                  setNewDMOpen(true);
                }}
                className='ml-auto p-0.5 rounded hover:bg-sidebar-accent'
              >
                <Plus className='w-3.5 h-3.5' />
              </button>
            </button>

            <AnimatePresence>
              {dmsExpanded && (
                <motion.div
                  initial={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                  animate={{ height: 'auto', opacity: 1 }}
                  exit={{ height: 0, opacity: 0 }}
                  transition={{ duration: 0.15 }}
                >
                  {currentWorkspace.dms?.map((dm) => {
                    const partner = getDMPartner(dm.participantIds);
                    if (!partner) return null;
                    return (
                      <button
                        key={dm.id}
                        onClick={() => handleDMClick(dm.id)}
                        className={`flex items-center gap-2 w-full px-2 py-1.5 rounded-md text-sm transition-colors ${
                          dm.id === currentDMId
                            ? 'bg-primary/20 text-primary'
                            : 'hover:bg-sidebar-accent text-sidebar-foreground'
                        }`}
                      >
                        <div className='relative shrink-0'>
                          <img
                            src={partner.avatar}
                            alt=''
                            className='w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-muted'
                          />
                          <span
                            className={`absolute -bottom-0.5 -right-0.5 w-2.5 h-2.5 rounded-full border-2 border-sidebar ${statusColors[partner.status]} ${partner.status === 'online' ? 'animate-pulse-dot' : ''}`}
                          />
                        </div>
                        <span className='truncate'>{partner.displayName}</span>
                        {dm.unreadCount > 0 && (
                          <span className='ml-auto bg-destructive text-destructive-foreground text-xs px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full min-w-[20px] text-center'>
                            {dm.unreadCount}
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </button>
                    );
                  })}
                </motion.div>
              )}
            </AnimatePresence>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* ── User footer ───────────────────────────────────────────────── */}
        <div className='border-t border-sidebar-border px-3 py-2'>
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
            <button
              onClick={() => onOpenProfile(authUser.id)}
              className='flex items-center gap-2 flex-1 min-w-0 rounded-md hover:bg-sidebar-accent px-1 py-1 transition-colors'
            >
              <div className='relative shrink-0'>
                <img
                  src={authUser.avatar}
                  alt=''
                  className='w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-muted'
                />
                <span
                  className={`absolute -bottom-0.5 -right-0.5 w-3 h-3 rounded-full border-2 border-sidebar ${statusColors[authUser.status]} ${authUser.status === 'online' ? 'animate-pulse-dot' : ''}`}
                />
              </div>
              <div className='flex-1 min-w-0 text-left'>
                <p className='text-sm font-medium text-sidebar-accent-foreground truncate'>
                  {authUser.displayName}
                </p>
                <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate'>
                  {authUser.statusEmoji} {authUser.statusText}
                </p>
              </div>
            </button>

            <button
              onClick={onToggleSound}
              className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-sidebar-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
              title={soundEnabled ? 'Mute' : 'Unmute'}
            >
              {soundEnabled ? (
                <Volume2 className='w-4 h-4' />
              ) : (
                <VolumeX className='w-4 h-4' />
              )}
            </button>

            <button
              onClick={onOpenSettings}
              className='p-1.5 rounded-md hover:bg-sidebar-accent text-muted-foreground transition-colors'
              title='Settings'
            >
              <Settings className='w-4 h-4' />
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      <NewDMModal open={newDMOpen} onClose={() => setNewDMOpen(false)} />
    </>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\config\axiosInstance.ts
==============================

import axios, { AxiosError } from 'axios';
import type { AxiosResponse, InternalAxiosRequestConfig } from 'axios';

import type { ApiErrorResponse } from '@/types';

const BASE_URL =
  (import.meta.env.VITE_BACKEND_API_URL as string)

/**
 * Axios instance shared across all API modules.
 *
 * Request interceptor  → injects JWT from localStorage into x-access-token header.
 * Response interceptor → unwraps `.data` so callers get the payload directly,
 *                        and normalises errors into a consistent shape.
 */
const axiosInstance = axios.create({
  baseURL: BASE_URL,
  withCredentials: true, // Send/receive httpOnly cookies
  headers: {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  },
  timeout: 15_000,
});

// ─── Request Interceptor ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

axiosInstance.interceptors.request.use(
  (config: InternalAxiosRequestConfig) => {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
    if (token) {
      config.headers['x-access-token'] = token;
    }
    return config;
  },
  (error: AxiosError) => Promise.reject(error),
);

// ─── Response Interceptor ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

axiosInstance.interceptors.response.use(
  (response: AxiosResponse) => response,
  (error: AxiosError<ApiErrorResponse>) => {
    // Token expired / invalid → clear local auth and redirect to login
    if (error.response?.status === 401) {
      localStorage.removeItem('token');
      // Avoid redirect loop on auth pages
      // if (!window.location.pathname.startsWith('/auth')) {
      //   window.location.href = '/auth/signin';
      // }
    }
    return Promise.reject(error);
  },
);

export default axiosInstance;

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\context\AuthContext.tsx
==============================

import  {
  createContext,
  useContext,
  useState,
  useCallback,
  useEffect,
  type ReactNode,

} from 'react';
import { mockApi } from '@/lib/mockApi';
import { type User } from '@/data/mockData';

type AuthStatus = 'loading' | 'authenticated' | 'unauthenticated';

interface AuthState {
  user: User | null;
  token: string | null;
  status: AuthStatus;
}

interface AuthContextType {
  auth: AuthState & { isAuthenticated: boolean };
  login: (email: string, password: string, remember?: boolean) => Promise<void>;
  signup: (
    name: string,
    username: string,
    email: string,
    password: string,
  ) => Promise<void>;
  socialLogin: (provider: 'google' | 'github') => Promise<void>;
  demoLogin: () => void;
  logout: () => void;
  updateProfile: (updates: Partial<User>) => void;
  changePassword: (current: string, newPass: string) => Promise<void>;
  requestPasswordReset: (
    email: string,
  ) => Promise<{ success: boolean; message: string }>;
  checkUsername: (username: string) => Promise<boolean>;
}

const AuthContext = createContext<AuthContextType | null>(null);

export const AuthProvider = ({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) => {
  const [state, setState] = useState<AuthState>({
    user: null,
    token: null,
    status: 'loading',
  });

  // Restore session on mount
  useEffect(() => {
    mockApi.auth.getSession().then((session) => {
      if (session) {
        setState({
          user: session.user,
          token: session.token,
          status: 'authenticated',
        });
      } else {
        setState({ user: null, token: null, status: 'unauthenticated' });
      }
    });
  }, []);

  const login = useCallback(
    async (email: string, password: string, remember = false) => {
      const result = await mockApi.auth.login(email, password);
      if (remember) mockApi.auth.rememberSession();
      setState({
        user: result.user,
        token: result.token,
        status: 'authenticated',
      });
    },
    [],
  );

  const signup = useCallback(
    async (name: string, username: string, email: string, password: string) => {
      const result = await mockApi.auth.signup(email, password, name, username);
      setState({
        user: result.user,
        token: result.token,
        status: 'authenticated',
      });
    },
    [],
  );

  const socialLogin = useCallback(async (provider: 'google' | 'github') => {
    // Simulate social login with delay
    await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 1200));
    const result = await mockApi.auth.login('alex@linkly.com', 'password');
    setState({
      user: { ...result.user, statusText: `Signed in via ${provider}` },
      token: result.token,
      status: 'authenticated',
    });
  }, []);

  const demoLogin = useCallback(() => {
    mockApi.auth.login('alex@linkly.com', 'password').then((result) => {
      setState({
        user: result.user,
        token: result.token,
        status: 'authenticated',
      });
    });
  }, []);

  const logout = useCallback(() => {
    mockApi.auth.logout();
    setState({ user: null, token: null, status: 'unauthenticated' });
  }, []);

  const updateProfile = useCallback((updates: Partial<User>) => {
    setState((prev) => {
      if (!prev.user) return prev;
      const updated = { ...prev.user, ...updates };
      mockApi.auth.updateProfile(prev.user.id, updates);
      return { ...prev, user: updated };
    });
  }, []);

  const changePassword = useCallback(
    async (current: string, newPass: string) => {
      if (!state.user) throw new Error('Not logged in');
      await mockApi.auth.changePassword(state.user.id, current, newPass);
    },
    [state.user],
  );

  const requestPasswordReset = useCallback(async (email: string) => {
    return mockApi.auth.requestPasswordReset(email);
  }, []);

  const checkUsername = useCallback(async (username: string) => {
    return mockApi.auth.checkUsernameAvailable(username);
  }, []);

  const authValue = {
    ...state,
    isAuthenticated: state.status === 'authenticated',
  };

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider
      value={{
        auth: authValue,
        login,
        signup,
        socialLogin,
        demoLogin,
        logout,
        updateProfile,
        changePassword,
        requestPasswordReset,
        checkUsername,
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
};

export const useAuth = () => {
  const ctx = useContext(AuthContext);
  // if (!ctx) throw new Error('useAuth must be used within AuthProvider');
  return ctx;
};

import { createContext } from 'react';

import type { UIContextType } from '@/types/uiContext.types';







export const UIContext = createContext<UIContextType | null>(null);

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\context\UIProvider.tsx

import type { RightPanel, WorkspaceView } from "@/types/uiContext.types";
import { useCallback, useEffect, useState, type ReactNode } from "react";
import type { Locale } from '@/lib/i18n';
import { UIContext } from "./UIContext";

export const UIProvider = ({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) => {
  const [sidebarOpen, setSidebarOpen] = useState(true);
  const [rightPanel, setRightPanel] = useState<RightPanel>(null);
  const [threadParentId, setThreadParentId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [profileUserId, setProfileUserId] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [searchOpen, setSearchOpen] = useState(false);
  const [settingsOpen, setSettingsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [createChannelOpen, setCreateChannelOpen] = useState(false);
  const [createWorkspaceOpen, setCreateWorkspaceOpen] = useState(false);
  const [workspaceSwitcherOpen, setWorkspaceSwitcherOpen] = useState(false);
  const [shortcutsOpen, setShortcutsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [soundEnabled, setSoundEnabled] = useState(true);
  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = useState(false);
  const [showConfetti, setShowConfetti] = useState(false);
  const [workspaceView, setWorkspaceView] = useState<WorkspaceView>('chat');
  const [locale, setLocaleState] = useState<Locale>(
    () => (localStorage.getItem('linkly_locale') as Locale) || 'en',
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    const check = () => setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < 768);
    check();
    window.addEventListener('resize', check);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', check);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
      if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key === 'k') {
        e.preventDefault();
        setSearchOpen(true);
      }
      if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key === '/') {
        e.preventDefault();
        setShortcutsOpen(true);
      }
      if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        setSearchOpen(false);
        setShortcutsOpen(false);
        setSettingsOpen(false);
        setCreateChannelOpen(false);
        setCreateWorkspaceOpen(false);
        setWorkspaceSwitcherOpen(false);
      }
    };
    window.addEventListener('keydown', handler);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('keydown', handler);
  }, []);

  const toggleSidebar = useCallback(() => setSidebarOpen((p) => !p), []);

  const toggleSound = useCallback(() => setSoundEnabled((p) => !p), []);
  const setLocale = useCallback((l: Locale) => {
    setLocaleState(l);
    localStorage.setItem('linkly_locale', l);
  }, []);

  const triggerConfetti = useCallback(() => {
    setShowConfetti(true);
    setTimeout(() => setShowConfetti(false), 3000);
  }, []);

  const openThread = useCallback((messageId: string) => {
    setThreadParentId(messageId);
    setRightPanel('thread');
    setProfileUserId(null);
  }, []);
  const closeThread = useCallback(() => {
    setThreadParentId(null);
    if (rightPanel === 'thread') setRightPanel(null);
  }, [rightPanel]);
  const openProfile = useCallback((userId: string) => {
    setProfileUserId(userId);
    setRightPanel('profile');
    setThreadParentId(null);
  }, []);
  const closeProfile = useCallback(() => {
    setProfileUserId(null);
    if (rightPanel === 'profile') setRightPanel(null);
  }, [rightPanel]);

  return (
    <UIContext.Provider
      value={{
        sidebarOpen,
        setSidebarOpen,
        toggleSidebar,
        rightPanel,
        setRightPanel,
        threadParentId,
        openThread,
        closeThread,
        profileUserId,
        openProfile,
        closeProfile,
        searchOpen,
        setSearchOpen,
        settingsOpen,
        setSettingsOpen,
        createChannelOpen,
        setCreateChannelOpen,
        createWorkspaceOpen,
        setCreateWorkspaceOpen,
        workspaceSwitcherOpen,
        setWorkspaceSwitcherOpen,
        shortcutsOpen,
        setShortcutsOpen,
        soundEnabled,
        toggleSound,
        isMobile,
        showConfetti,
        triggerConfetti,
        workspaceView,
        setWorkspaceView,
        locale,
        setLocale,
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </UIContext.Provider>
  );
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\context\WorkspaceContext.tsx
