import React, {
  createContext,
  useContext,
  useState,
  useCallback,
  useEffect,
  useRef,
  ReactNode,
} from 'react';
import { mockApi } from '@/lib/mockApi';
import {
  type Workspace,
  type Channel,
  type Message,
  type DM,
  type User,
  type Notification,
  type Reaction,
} from '@/data/mockData';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

interface WorkspaceContextType {
  workspaces: Workspace[];
  currentWorkspace: Workspace | null;
  setCurrentWorkspaceId: (id: string) => void;
  currentChannel: Channel | null;
  setCurrentChannelId: (id: string | null) => void;
  currentDM: DM | null;
  setCurrentDMId: (id: string | null) => void;
  messages: Message[];
  sendMessage: (content: string, attachments?: Message['attachments']) => void;
  editMessage: (messageId: string, newContent: string) => void;
  deleteMessage: (messageId: string) => void;
  toggleReaction: (messageId: string, emoji: string, userId: string) => void;
  togglePin: (messageId: string) => void;
  addThreadReply: (parentId: string, content: string, userId: string) => void;
  createChannel: (
    channel: Omit<Channel, 'id' | 'pinnedMessages' | 'unreadCount' | 'muted'>,
  ) => void;
  createWorkspace: (
    name: string,
    icon: string,
    description: string,
    firstChannel: string,
  ) => void;
  joinWorkspace: (code: string) => Workspace | null;
  getUser: (id: string) => User | undefined;
  notifications: Notification[];
  markNotificationRead: (id: string) => void;
  markAllNotificationsRead: () => void;
  dmMessages: Message[];
  sendDMMessage: (content: string) => void;
  loadingMessages: boolean;
  loadEarlierMessages: () => void;
  hasEarlierMessages: boolean;
  unreadCounts: Record<string, number>;
  allChannels: Channel[];
  joinChannel: (channelId: string) => void;
  leaveChannel: (channelId: string) => void;
}

const WorkspaceContext = createContext<WorkspaceContextType | null>(null);

export const WorkspaceProvider = ({
  children,
  userId,
}: {
  children: ReactNode;
  userId: string;
}) => {
  const [workspaces, setWorkspaces] = useState<Workspace[]>([]);
  const [currentWorkspaceId, setCurrentWorkspaceId] = useState<string>('w1');
  const [currentChannelId, setCurrentChannelIdRaw] = useState<string | null>(
    'c1',
  );
  const [currentDMId, setCurrentDMIdRaw] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [allMessages, setAllMessages] = useState<Record<string, Message[]>>({});
  const [notifications, setNotifications] = useState<Notification[]>([]);
  const [loadingMessages, setLoadingMessages] = useState(false);
  const [hasEarlierMessages, setHasEarlierMessages] = useState(false);
  const [unreadCounts, setUnreadCounts] = useState<Record<string, number>>({});
  const [usersCache, setUsersCache] = useState<Map<string, User>>(new Map());
  const initRef = useRef(false);

  // Load initial data from mockApi
  useEffect(() => {
    if (initRef.current) return;
    initRef.current = true;

    Promise.all([
      mockApi.workspaces.list(userId),
      mockApi.users.getAll(),
      mockApi.notifications.list(userId),
    ]).then(([wsList, usersList, notifs]) => {
      setWorkspaces(wsList);
      setUsersCache(new Map(usersList.map((u) => [u.id, u])));
      setNotifications(notifs);
    });
  }, [userId]);

  const currentWorkspace =
    workspaces.find((w) => w.id === currentWorkspaceId) || null;
  const currentChannel = currentChannelId
    ? currentWorkspace?.channels.find((c) => c.id === currentChannelId) || null
    : null;
  const currentDM = currentDMId
    ? currentWorkspace?.dms.find((d) => d.id === currentDMId) || null
    : null;
  const messages = currentChannelId ? allMessages[currentChannelId] || [] : [];
  const dmMessages = currentDM?.messages || [];
  const allChannels = currentWorkspace?.channels || [];

  // Load messages when channel changes
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!currentChannelId) return;
    if (allMessages[currentChannelId]) return; // already loaded
    setLoadingMessages(true);
    mockApi.messages.getAll(currentChannelId).then((msgs) => {
      setAllMessages((prev) => ({ ...prev, [currentChannelId]: msgs }));
      setHasEarlierMessages(false); // getAll returns everything
      setLoadingMessages(false);
    });
  }, [currentChannelId]);

  // Mark channel as read when entering
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!currentChannelId) return;
    const msgs = allMessages[currentChannelId];
    if (!msgs || msgs.length === 0) return;
    const lastMsg = msgs[msgs.length - 1];
    mockApi.readStates.markRead(userId, currentChannelId, lastMsg.id);
    setUnreadCounts((prev) => ({ ...prev, [currentChannelId]: 0 }));
  }, [currentChannelId, allMessages, userId]);

  // Compute unread counts for all channels in current workspace
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!currentWorkspace) return;
    const computeUnreads = async () => {
      const counts: Record<string, number> = {};
      for (const ch of currentWorkspace.channels) {
        if (ch.id === currentChannelId) {
          counts[ch.id] = 0;
          continue;
        }
        const count = await mockApi.readStates.getUnreadCount(userId, ch.id);
        counts[ch.id] = count;
      }
      setUnreadCounts(counts);
    };
    computeUnreads();
  }, [
    currentWorkspace?.id,
    currentWorkspace?.channels.length,
    userId,
    currentChannelId,
  ]);

  const getUser = useCallback((id: string) => usersCache.get(id), [usersCache]);

  // Refresh user cache helper
  const refreshUser = useCallback((id: string) => {
    mockApi.users.getUser(id).then((u) => {
      if (u) setUsersCache((prev) => new Map(prev).set(id, u));
    });
  }, []);

  const setCurrentChannelId = useCallback((id: string | null) => {
    setCurrentChannelIdRaw(id);
    if (id) setCurrentDMIdRaw(null);
  }, []);

  const setCurrentDMId = useCallback((id: string | null) => {
    setCurrentDMIdRaw(id);
    if (id) setCurrentChannelIdRaw(null);
  }, []);

  // ── AI Bot responses ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const botResponses = [
    "I've analyzed the thread — here's a quick summary: the team agreed to move forward with the proposed approach and assigned action items.",
    "Here's a draft meeting agenda:\n1. Sprint review\n2. Blockers discussion\n3. Next sprint planning\n4. Open floor",
    "Based on channel activity, I'd suggest these topics: **Release planning**, **Code review standards**, **Team retrospective**",
    "Here's a draft message for you:\n> Hi team, just wanted to share an update on our progress. We're on track for the deadline and have resolved the key blockers. Let me know if you need anything!",
    '📊 Channel insights: This channel has been most active between 9-11am. Top contributors this week are the usual suspects!',
    'I can help with that! Here are some suggestions:\n- Break the task into smaller subtasks\n- Set a deadline for each\n- Assign owners and track in /goals',
  ];

  const triggerBotReply = useCallback((channelId: string) => {
    setTimeout(
      () => {
        const botMsg: Message = {
          id: `bot_${Date.now()}`,
          channelId,
          authorId: 'bot_linkly',
          content:
            botResponses[Math.floor(Math.random() * botResponses.length)],
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
          edited: false,
          reactions: [],
          thread: [],
          attachments: [],
        };
        setAllMessages((prev) => ({
          ...prev,
          [channelId]: [...(prev[channelId] || []), botMsg],
        }));
        mockApi.messages.send(channelId, 'bot_linkly', botMsg.content);
      },
      1500 + Math.random() * 1000,
    );
  }, []);

  // ── Optimistic message send ─────────────────────────────────────────────
  const sendMessage = useCallback(
    (content: string, attachments: Message['attachments'] = []) => {
      if (!currentChannelId) return;
      const tempId = `temp_${Date.now()}`;
      const tempMsg: Message = {
        id: tempId,
        channelId: currentChannelId,
        authorId: userId,
        content,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        edited: false,
        reactions: [],
        thread: [],
        attachments,
      };
      setAllMessages((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        [currentChannelId]: [...(prev[currentChannelId] || []), tempMsg],
      }));

      mockApi.messages
        .send(currentChannelId, userId, content, attachments)
        .then((real) => {
          setAllMessages((prev) => ({
            ...prev,
            [currentChannelId]: (prev[currentChannelId] || []).map((m) =>
              m.id === tempId ? real : m,
            ),
          }));
        })
        .catch(() => {
          setAllMessages((prev) => ({
            ...prev,
            [currentChannelId]: (prev[currentChannelId] || []).filter(
              (m) => m.id !== tempId,
            ),
          }));
          toast.error('Failed to send message');
        });

      // Trigger bot reply if @Linkly is mentioned
      if (content.toLowerCase().includes('@linkly')) {
        triggerBotReply(currentChannelId);
      }
    },
    [currentChannelId, userId, triggerBotReply],
  );

  const sendDMMessage = useCallback(
    (content: string) => {
      if (!currentDMId || !currentWorkspaceId) return;
      const tempId = `dm_temp_${Date.now()}`;
      const tempMsg: Message = {
        id: tempId,
        dmId: currentDMId,
        authorId: userId,
        content,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        edited: false,
        reactions: [],
        thread: [],
        attachments: [],
      };
      // Optimistic update
      setWorkspaces((prev) =>
        prev.map((w) =>
          w.id === currentWorkspaceId
            ? {
                ...w,
                dms: w.dms.map((d) =>
                  d.id === currentDMId
                    ? { ...d, messages: [...d.messages, tempMsg] }
                    : d,
                ),
              }
            : w,
        ),
      );

      mockApi.dms
        .sendMessage(currentWorkspaceId, currentDMId, userId, content)
        .then((real) => {
          setWorkspaces((prev) =>
            prev.map((w) =>
              w.id === currentWorkspaceId
                ? {
                    ...w,
                    dms: w.dms.map((d) =>
                      d.id === currentDMId
                        ? {
                            ...d,
                            messages: d.messages.map((m) =>
                              m.id === tempId ? real : m,
                            ),
                          }
                        : d,
                    ),
                  }
                : w,
            ),
          );
        })
        .catch(() => {
          setWorkspaces((prev) =>
            prev.map((w) =>
              w.id === currentWorkspaceId
                ? {
                    ...w,
                    dms: w.dms.map((d) =>
                      d.id === currentDMId
                        ? {
                            ...d,
                            messages: d.messages.filter((m) => m.id !== tempId),
                          }
                        : d,
                    ),
                  }
                : w,
            ),
          );
          toast.error('Failed to send message');
        });
    },
    [currentDMId, currentWorkspaceId, userId],
  );

  const editMessage = useCallback(
    (messageId: string, newContent: string) => {
      if (!currentChannelId) return;
      // Optimistic
      setAllMessages((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        [currentChannelId]: (prev[currentChannelId] || []).map((m) =>
          m.id === messageId
            ? {
                ...m,
                content: newContent,
                edited: true,
                editedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
              }
            : m,
        ),
      }));
      mockApi.messages
        .edit(currentChannelId, messageId, newContent)
        .catch(() => {
          toast.error('Failed to edit message');
        });
    },
    [currentChannelId],
  );

  const deleteMessage = useCallback(
    (messageId: string) => {
      if (!currentChannelId) return;
      const backup = allMessages[currentChannelId] || [];
      setAllMessages((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        [currentChannelId]: (prev[currentChannelId] || []).filter(
          (m) => m.id !== messageId,
        ),
      }));
      mockApi.messages.delete(currentChannelId, messageId).catch(() => {
        setAllMessages((prev) => ({ ...prev, [currentChannelId]: backup }));
        toast.error('Failed to delete message');
      });
    },
    [currentChannelId, allMessages],
  );

  const toggleReaction = useCallback(
    (messageId: string, emoji: string, uid: string) => {
      if (!currentChannelId) return;
      // Optimistic update locally
      const updateReactions = (msgs: Message[]): Message[] =>
        msgs.map((m) => {
          if (m.id === messageId) {
            const existing = m.reactions.find((r) => r.emoji === emoji);
            let newReactions: Reaction[];
            if (existing) {
              if (existing.userIds.includes(uid)) {
                const filtered = existing.userIds.filter((u) => u !== uid);
                newReactions =
                  filtered.length > 0
                    ? m.reactions.map((r) =>
                        r.emoji === emoji ? { ...r, userIds: filtered } : r,
                      )
                    : m.reactions.filter((r) => r.emoji !== emoji);
              } else {
                newReactions = m.reactions.map((r) =>
                  r.emoji === emoji
                    ? { ...r, userIds: [...r.userIds, uid] }
                    : r,
                );
              }
            } else {
              newReactions = [...m.reactions, { emoji, userIds: [uid] }];
            }
            return { ...m, reactions: newReactions };
          }
          return { ...m, thread: updateReactions(m.thread) };
        });

      setAllMessages((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        [currentChannelId]: updateReactions(prev[currentChannelId] || []),
      }));
      mockApi.messages
        .toggleReaction(currentChannelId, messageId, emoji, uid)
        .catch(() => {
          toast.error('Failed to update reaction');
        });
    },
    [currentChannelId],
  );

  const togglePin = useCallback(
    (messageId: string) => {
      if (!currentChannelId || !currentWorkspaceId) return;
      // Optimistic
      setWorkspaces((prev) =>
        prev.map((w) =>
          w.id === currentWorkspaceId
            ? {
                ...w,
                channels: w.channels.map((ch) => {
                  if (ch.id !== currentChannelId) return ch;
                  const isPinned = ch.pinnedMessages.includes(messageId);
                  return {
                    ...ch,
                    pinnedMessages: isPinned
                      ? ch.pinnedMessages.filter((id) => id !== messageId)
                      : [...ch.pinnedMessages, messageId],
                  };
                }),
              }
            : w,
        ),
      );
      mockApi.messages
        .pin(currentChannelId, messageId, currentWorkspaceId)
        .catch(() => {
          toast.error('Failed to toggle pin');
        });
    },
    [currentChannelId, currentWorkspaceId],
  );

  const addThreadReply = useCallback(
    (parentId: string, content: string, uid: string) => {
      if (!currentChannelId) return;
      const tempId = `thread_temp_${Date.now()}`;
      const reply: Message = {
        id: tempId,
        channelId: currentChannelId,
        authorId: uid,
        content,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        edited: false,
        reactions: [],
        thread: [],
        attachments: [],
      };
      // Optimistic
      setAllMessages((prev) => ({
        ...prev,
        [currentChannelId]: (prev[currentChannelId] || []).map((m) =>
          m.id === parentId ? { ...m, thread: [...m.thread, reply] } : m,
        ),
      }));
      mockApi.threads
        .addReply(currentChannelId, parentId, content, uid)
        .then((real) => {
          setAllMessages((prev) => ({
            ...prev,
            [currentChannelId]: (prev[currentChannelId] || []).map((m) =>
              m.id === parentId
                ? {
                    ...m,
                    thread: m.thread.map((t) => (t.id === tempId ? real : t)),
                  }
                : m,
            ),
          }));
        })
        .catch(() => {
          toast.error('Failed to add reply');
        });
    },
    [currentChannelId],
  );

  const createChannel = useCallback(
    (
      channelData: Omit<
        Channel,
        'id' | 'pinnedMessages' | 'unreadCount' | 'muted'
      >,
    ) => {
      if (!currentWorkspaceId) return;
      const tempId = `ch_temp_${Date.now()}`;
      const tempChannel: Channel = {
        ...channelData,
        id: tempId,
        pinnedMessages: [],
        unreadCount: 0,
        muted: false,
      };
      // Optimistic
      setWorkspaces((prev) =>
        prev.map((w) =>
          w.id === currentWorkspaceId
            ? { ...w, channels: [...w.channels, tempChannel] }
            : w,
        ),
      );
      setCurrentChannelId(tempId);

      mockApi.channels
        .create(currentWorkspaceId, channelData)
        .then((real) => {
          setWorkspaces((prev) =>
            prev.map((w) =>
              w.id === currentWorkspaceId
                ? {
                    ...w,
                    channels: w.channels.map((ch) =>
                      ch.id === tempId ? real : ch,
                    ),
                  }
                : w,
            ),
          );
          setCurrentChannelIdRaw(real.id);
          toast.success(`Channel #${real.name} created`);
        })
        .catch(() => {
          setWorkspaces((prev) =>
            prev.map((w) =>
              w.id === currentWorkspaceId
                ? {
                    ...w,
                    channels: w.channels.filter((ch) => ch.id !== tempId),
                  }
                : w,
            ),
          );
          toast.error('Failed to create channel');
        });
    },
    [currentWorkspaceId, setCurrentChannelId],
  );

  const createWorkspace = useCallback(
    (name: string, icon: string, description: string, firstChannel: string) => {
      mockApi.workspaces
        .create(name, icon, description, firstChannel, userId)
        .then((ws) => {
          setWorkspaces((prev) => [...prev, ws]);
          setCurrentWorkspaceId(ws.id);
          setCurrentChannelId(ws.channels[0]?.id || null);
          toast.success(`Workspace "${name}" created`);
        })
        .catch(() => {
          toast.error('Failed to create workspace');
        });
    },
    [userId, setCurrentChannelId],
  );

  const joinWorkspace = useCallback(
    (code: string) => {
      // Synchronous-looking but we update state from mockApi result
      let result: Workspace | null = null;
      mockApi.workspaces.join(code, userId).then((ws) => {
        if (ws) {
          result = ws;
          setWorkspaces((prev) => {
            const existing = prev.find((w) => w.id === ws.id);
            if (existing) return prev.map((w) => (w.id === ws.id ? ws : w));
            return [...prev, ws];
          });
          setCurrentWorkspaceId(ws.id);
          setCurrentChannelId(ws.channels[0]?.id || null);
          toast.success(`Joined workspace "${ws.name}"`);
        }
      });
      // Return synchronously for backward compat (the callers check null)
      const ws = workspaces.find(
        (w) => w.joinCode.toLowerCase() === code.toLowerCase(),
      );
      return ws || null;
    },
    [workspaces, userId, setCurrentChannelId],
  );

  const joinChannel = useCallback(
    (channelId: string) => {
      if (!currentWorkspaceId) return;
      // Optimistic: add user to channel members
      setWorkspaces((prev) =>
        prev.map((w) =>
          w.id === currentWorkspaceId
            ? {
                ...w,
                channels: w.channels.map((ch) =>
                  ch.id === channelId && !ch.members.includes(userId)
                    ? { ...ch, members: [...ch.members, userId] }
                    : ch,
                ),
              }
            : w,
        ),
      );
      mockApi.channels
        .join(currentWorkspaceId, channelId, userId)
        .then(() => {
          toast.success('Joined channel');
        })
        .catch(() => {
          toast.error('Failed to join channel');
        });
    },
    [currentWorkspaceId, userId],
  );

  const leaveChannel = useCallback(
    (channelId: string) => {
      if (!currentWorkspaceId) return;
      setWorkspaces((prev) =>
        prev.map((w) =>
          w.id === currentWorkspaceId
            ? {
                ...w,
                channels: w.channels.map((ch) =>
                  ch.id === channelId
                    ? { ...ch, members: ch.members.filter((m) => m !== userId) }
                    : ch,
                ),
              }
            : w,
        ),
      );
      if (currentChannelId === channelId) {
        const firstOther = currentWorkspace?.channels.find(
          (c) => c.id !== channelId && c.members.includes(userId),
        );
        setCurrentChannelId(firstOther?.id || null);
      }
      mockApi.channels
        .leave(currentWorkspaceId, channelId, userId)
        .catch(() => {
          toast.error('Failed to leave channel');
        });
    },
    [
      currentWorkspaceId,
      userId,
      currentChannelId,
      currentWorkspace,
      setCurrentChannelId,
    ],
  );

  const loadEarlierMessages = useCallback(() => {
    if (!currentChannelId || loadingMessages) return;
    const msgs = allMessages[currentChannelId] || [];
    if (msgs.length === 0) return;
    setLoadingMessages(true);
    mockApi.messages
      .list(currentChannelId, { before: msgs[0].id, limit: 30 })
      .then((earlier) => {
        if (earlier.length === 0) {
          setHasEarlierMessages(false);
        } else {
          setAllMessages((prev) => ({
            ...prev,
            [currentChannelId]: [...earlier, ...(prev[currentChannelId] || [])],
          }));
          setHasEarlierMessages(earlier.length >= 30);
        }
        setLoadingMessages(false);
      });
  }, [currentChannelId, loadingMessages, allMessages]);

  const markNotificationRead = useCallback((id: string) => {
    setNotifications((prev) =>
      prev.map((n) => (n.id === id ? { ...n, read: true } : n)),
    );
    mockApi.notifications.markRead(id);
  }, []);

  const markAllNotificationsRead = useCallback(() => {
    setNotifications((prev) => prev.map((n) => ({ ...n, read: true })));
    mockApi.notifications.markAllRead();
  }, []);

  return (
    <WorkspaceContext.Provider
      value={{
        workspaces,
        currentWorkspace,
        setCurrentWorkspaceId,
        currentChannel,
        setCurrentChannelId,
        currentDM,
        setCurrentDMId,
        messages,
        sendMessage,
        editMessage,
        deleteMessage,
        toggleReaction,
        togglePin,
        addThreadReply,
        createChannel,
        createWorkspace,
        joinWorkspace,
        getUser,
        notifications,
        markNotificationRead,
        markAllNotificationsRead,
        dmMessages,
        sendDMMessage,
        loadingMessages,
        loadEarlierMessages,
        hasEarlierMessages,
        unreadCounts,
        allChannels,
        joinChannel,
        leaveChannel,
      }}
    >
      {children}
    </WorkspaceContext.Provider>
  );
};

export const useWorkspace = () => {
  const ctx = useContext(WorkspaceContext);
  if (!ctx)
    throw new Error('useWorkspace must be used within WorkspaceProvider');
  return ctx;
};

// ── Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export type UserStatus = 'online' | 'away' | 'dnd' | 'offline';

export interface User {
  id: string;
  username: string;
  displayName: string;
  email: string;
  avatar: string;
  status: UserStatus;
  statusEmoji: string;
  statusText: string;
  bio: string;
  title: string;
  timezone: string;
  memberSince: string;
}

export interface Reaction {
  emoji: string;
  userIds: string[];
}

export interface Attachment {
  id: string;
  type: 'image' | 'file';
  name: string;
  url: string;
  size: string;
}

export interface Message {
  id: string;
  channelId?: string;
  dmId?: string;
  authorId: string;
  content: string;
  timestamp: string;
  edited: boolean;
  editedAt?: string;
  reactions: Reaction[];
  thread: Message[];
  attachments: Attachment[];
  isSystem?: boolean;
}

export type ChannelType = 'text' | 'voice' | 'announcement';

export interface Channel {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: ChannelType;
  description: string;
  isPrivate: boolean;
  pinnedMessages: string[];
  members: string[];
  unreadCount: number;
  muted: boolean;
}

export interface DM {
  id: string;
  participantIds: string[];
  messages: Message[];
  unreadCount: number;
}

export interface Workspace {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  icon: string;
  description: string;
  ownerId: string;
  members: string[];
  channels: Channel[];
  dms: DM[];
  joinCode: string;
}

export interface Notification {
  id: string;
  type: 'mention' | 'reaction' | 'thread_reply' | 'dm';
  fromUserId: string;
  channelId?: string;
  dmId?: string;
  messagePreview: string;
  timestamp: string;
  read: boolean;
}

export interface PollOption {
  id: string;
  text: string;
  votes: string[];
}

export interface Poll {
  id: string;
  question: string;
  options: PollOption[];
  creatorId: string;
  anonymous: boolean;
  endDate?: string;
  channelId: string;
  messageId: string;
  createdAt: string;
}

import { createSlice } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import type { PayloadAction } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';

import type { AuthState, AuthUser } from '@/types/auth.types';

/**
 * Auth slice — state storage only.
 *
 * There are NO async thunks here. All API calls are handled by TanStack Query
 * hooks. Once a query/mutation succeeds, the hook dispatches these plain
 * actions to sync the result into Redux (and redux-persist takes care of
 * persisting user + token to localStorage).
 */

const initialState: AuthState = {
  user: null,
  token: null,
};

const authSlice = createSlice({
  name: 'auth',
  initialState,
  reducers: {
    /**
     * Called by useSignIn hook on successful sign-in.
     * Stores the authenticated user and token.
     */
    setCredentials(state, action: PayloadAction<AuthUser>) {
      state.user = action.payload;
      state.token = action.payload.token;
    },

    /**
     * Called by useSignOut hook (or the axios 401 interceptor).
     * Wipes all auth state — redux-persist will sync the cleared
     * state back to localStorage automatically.
     */
    clearCredentials(state) {
      state.user = null;
      state.token = null;
    },
  },
});

export const { setCredentials, clearCredentials } = authSlice.actions;
export default authSlice.reducer;

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\features\channelSlice.ts
==============================

// src/features/channelSlice.ts
// Owns: currentChannelId, currentDMId, unreadCounts
// Mutual exclusion: selecting a channel clears DM and vice versa
// unreadCounts incremented by socket events, cleared on channel enter

import { createSlice } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import type { PayloadAction } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';

interface ChannelState {
  currentChannelId: string | null;
  currentDMId: string | null;
  unreadCounts: Record<string, number>; // channelId → unread count
}

const initialState: ChannelState = {
  currentChannelId: null,
  currentDMId: null,
  unreadCounts: {},
};

const channelSlice = createSlice({
  name: 'channel',
  initialState,
  reducers: {
    setCurrentChannelId(state, action: PayloadAction<string | null>) {
      state.currentChannelId = action.payload;
      // Switching to a channel clears active DM
      if (action.payload) {
        state.currentDMId = null;
        // Mark as read immediately on enter
        state.unreadCounts[action.payload] = 0;
      }
    },

    setCurrentDMId(state, action: PayloadAction<string | null>) {
      state.currentDMId = action.payload;
      // Switching to a DM clears active channel
      if (action.payload) {
        state.currentChannelId = null;
      }
    },

    // Called after TanStack Query fetches unread counts on workspace load
    setUnreadCounts(state, action: PayloadAction<Record<string, number>>) {
      state.unreadCounts = action.payload;
    },

    // Called when user enters a channel — marks it as fully read
    markChannelRead(state, action: PayloadAction<string>) {
      state.unreadCounts[action.payload] = 0;
    },

    // Called by socket event when a new message arrives in a channel
    // the user is NOT currently viewing
    incrementUnread(state, action: PayloadAction<string>) {
      const channelId = action.payload;
      if (channelId !== state.currentChannelId) {
        state.unreadCounts[channelId] =
          (state.unreadCounts[channelId] ?? 0) + 1;
      }
    },

    // Reset everything on workspace switch
    resetChannelState(state) {
      state.currentChannelId = null;
      state.currentDMId = null;
      state.unreadCounts = {};
    },
  },
});

export const {
  setCurrentChannelId,
  setCurrentDMId,
  setUnreadCounts,
  markChannelRead,
  incrementUnread,
  resetChannelState,
} = channelSlice.actions;
export default channelSlice.reducer;

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\features\messageSlice.ts
==============================

import { createAsyncThunk, createSlice, PayloadAction } from '@reduxjs/toolkit';
import { AxiosError } from 'axios';

import { messageApi } from '@/api/messageApi';
import { ApiErrorResponse, Message, MessageState } from '@/types';

// ─── Thunks ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export const fetchMessages = createAsyncThunk<
  Message[],
  { channelId: string; page?: number; limit?: number },
  { rejectValue: string }
>('messages/fetchByChannel', async ({ channelId, page = 1, limit = 20 }, { rejectWithValue }) => {
  try {
    const res = await messageApi.getByChannel(channelId, page, limit);
    return res.data;
  } catch (err) {
    const error = err as AxiosError<ApiErrorResponse>;
    return rejectWithValue(error.response?.data?.message ?? 'Failed to fetch messages');
  }
});

// ─── Initial State ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const initialState: MessageState = {
  messages: [],
  loading: 'idle',
  error: null,
  sendingMessage: false
};

// ─── Slice ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const messageSlice = createSlice({
  name: 'messages',
  initialState,
  reducers: {
    /** Real-time: socket delivered a new message — prepend to list */
    receiveMessage(state, action: PayloadAction<Message>) {
      const exists = state.messages.some((m) => m._id === action.payload._id);
      if (!exists) {
        state.messages.unshift(action.payload);
      }
    },
    setSendingMessage(state, action: PayloadAction<boolean>) {
      state.sendingMessage = action.payload;
    },
    clearMessages(state) {
      state.messages = [];
      state.loading = 'idle';
      state.error = null;
    },
    clearMessageError(state) {
      state.error = null;
    }
  },
  extraReducers: (builder) => {
    builder
      .addCase(fetchMessages.pending, (state) => {
        state.loading = 'loading';
        state.error = null;
      })
      .addCase(fetchMessages.fulfilled, (state, action) => {
        state.loading = 'succeeded';
        state.messages = action.payload;
      })
      .addCase(fetchMessages.rejected, (state, action) => {
        state.loading = 'failed';
        state.error = action.payload ?? 'Failed to fetch messages';
      });
  }
});

export const { receiveMessage, setSendingMessage, clearMessages, clearMessageError } =
  messageSlice.actions;
export default messageSlice.reducer;

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\auth\useSignIn.ts
==============================

import type { ApiErrorResponse, AuthUser, SignInPayload } from "@/types";
import useAppDispatch from "../useAppDispatch";
import { signInRequest } from "@/services/auth.service";
import { setCredentials } from "@/features/authSlice";
import type { AxiosError } from "axios";
import { useMutation } from "@tanstack/react-query";


/**
 * Mutation hook for sign-in.
 *
 * On success:
 *  1. Persists the JWT to localStorage (picked up by the axios interceptor).
 *  2. Dispatches `setCredentials` → Redux + redux-persist stores user + token.
 *
 * Usage:
 * ```tsx
 * const { mutate: signIn, isPending, error } = useSignIn();
 * signIn({ email, password });
 * ```
 */
export const useSignIn = () => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();

  return useMutation({
    mutationFn: (payload: SignInPayload) => signInRequest(payload),

    onSuccess: (authUser: AuthUser) => {
      // 1. Persist token for axios request interceptor
      localStorage.setItem('token', authUser.token);
      // 2. Sync into Redux — redux-persist will write user + token to localStorage
      dispatch(setCredentials(authUser));
    },

    onError: (err: AxiosError<ApiErrorResponse>) => {
      console.error('[useSignIn] error:', err.response?.data?.message);
    },
  });
};


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\auth\useSignOut.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import useAppDispatch from "../useAppDispatch";
import { clearCredentials } from "@/features/authSlice";
import { signOutRequest } from "@/services/auth.service";

/**
 * Mutation hook for sign-out.
 *
 * On success (and on error — best-effort):
 *  1. Clears JWT from localStorage.
 *  2. Dispatches `clearCredentials` → Redux + redux-persist wipes persisted auth.
 *  3. Invalidates all cached TanStack Query data so stale user-specific
 *     data is not shown after a different user signs in.
 *
 * Usage:
 * ```tsx
 * const { mutate: signOut, isPending } = useSignOut();
 * signOut();
 * ```
 */
export const useSignOut = () => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  const clearLocal = () => {
    localStorage.removeItem('token');
    dispatch(clearCredentials());
    // Nuke all cached query data — prevents data leaking between sessions
    queryClient.clear();
  };

  return useMutation({
    mutationFn: () => signOutRequest(),
    onSuccess: clearLocal,
    // Clear locally even if the server call fails
    onError: clearLocal,
  });
};

import { signUpRequest } from "@/services/auth.service";
import type { ApiErrorResponse, SignUpPayload } from "@/types";
import { useMutation } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import type { AxiosError } from "axios";

/**
 * Mutation hook for user registration.
 *
 * On success: the user is created on the server but NOT signed in.
 * The caller should navigate to sign-in or show a "check your email" message.
 *
 * Usage:
 * ```tsx
 * const { mutate: signUp, isPending, error } = useSignUp();
 * signUp({ email, username, password });
 * ```
 */
export const useSignUp = () => {
  return useMutation({
    mutationFn: (payload: SignUpPayload) => signUpRequest(payload),

    onError: (err: AxiosError<ApiErrorResponse>) => {
      // Error is surfaced via mutation.error — handle toasts in the component
      console.error('[useSignUp] error:', err.response?.data?.message);
    },
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\channel\useCreateChannel.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { setCurrentChannelId } from '@/features/channelSlice';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

import type { Channel } from '@/data/mockData';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

type CreateChannelPayload = Omit<
  Channel,
  'id' | 'pinnedMessages' | 'unreadCount' | 'muted'
>;

export const useCreateChannel = () => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const workspaceId = useAppSelector((s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId);

  return useMutation<Channel, Error, CreateChannelPayload>({
    mutationFn: (payload) =>
      axiosInstance
        .post(`/workspaces/${workspaceId}/channels`, payload)
        .then((r) => r.data),

    onMutate: async (payload) => {
      await queryClient.cancelQueries({ queryKey: ['channels', workspaceId] });
      const previous = queryClient.getQueryData<Channel[]>([
        'channels',
        workspaceId,
      ]);

      // Optimistic: add temp channel to list immediately
      const tempChannel: Channel = {
        ...payload,
        id: `temp_${Date.now()}`,
        pinnedMessages: [],
        unreadCount: 0,
        muted: false,
      };
      queryClient.setQueryData<Channel[]>(['channels', workspaceId], (old) => [
        ...(old ?? []),
        tempChannel,
      ]);
      dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(tempChannel.id));

      return { previous, tempId: tempChannel.id };
    },

    onSuccess: (real, _, ctx) => {
      // Replace temp channel with real one from server
      queryClient.setQueryData<Channel[]>(['channels', workspaceId], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((ch) => (ch.id === ctx?.tempId ? real : ch)),
      );
      dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(real.id));
      toast.success(`Channel #${real.name} created`);
    },

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      // Rollback optimistic update
      queryClient.setQueryData(['channels', workspaceId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to create channel');
    },
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\channel\useJoinChannel.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import type { Channel } from '@/data/mockData';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

export const useJoinChannel = () => {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const workspaceId = useAppSelector((s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId);
  const userId = useAppSelector((s) => s.auth.user?.id);

  return useMutation<void, Error, string>({
    mutationFn: (channelId) =>
      axiosInstance
        .post(`/workspaces/${workspaceId}/channels/${channelId}/join`)
        .then((r) => r.data),

    onMutate: async (channelId) => {
      await queryClient.cancelQueries({ queryKey: ['channels', workspaceId] });
      const previous = queryClient.getQueryData<Channel[]>([
        'channels',
        workspaceId,
      ]);

      // Optimistic: add userId to channel members
      queryClient.setQueryData<Channel[]>(['channels', workspaceId], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((ch) =>
          ch.id === channelId && !ch.members.includes(userId!)
            ? { ...ch, members: [...ch.members, userId!] }
            : ch,
        ),
      );
      return { previous };
    },

    onSuccess: () => toast.success('Joined channel'),

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(['channels', workspaceId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to join channel');
    },
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\channel\useLeaveChannel.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { setCurrentChannelId } from '@/features/channelSlice';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

import type { Channel } from '@/data/mockData';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

export const useLeaveChannel = () => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const workspaceId = useAppSelector((s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId);
  const currentChannelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);
  const userId = useAppSelector((s) => s.auth.user?.id);

  return useMutation<void, Error, string>({
    mutationFn: (channelId) =>
      axiosInstance
        .post(`/workspaces/${workspaceId}/channels/${channelId}/leave`)
        .then((r) => r.data),

    onMutate: async (channelId) => {
      await queryClient.cancelQueries({ queryKey: ['channels', workspaceId] });
      const previous = queryClient.getQueryData<Channel[]>([
        'channels',
        workspaceId,
      ]);

      // Optimistic: remove userId from members
      queryClient.setQueryData<Channel[]>(['channels', workspaceId], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((ch) =>
          ch.id === channelId
            ? { ...ch, members: ch.members.filter((m) => m !== userId) }
            : ch,
        ),
      );

      // If leaving current channel, switch to first available other channel
      if (currentChannelId === channelId) {
        const channels =
          queryClient.getQueryData<Channel[]>(['channels', workspaceId]) ?? [];
        const next = channels.find(
          (c) => c.id !== channelId && c.members.includes(userId!),
        );
        dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(next?.id ?? null));
      }

      return { previous };
    },

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(['channels', workspaceId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to leave channel');
    },
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\messages\useAddThreadReply.ts

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';
import type { Message } from '@/data/mockData';

interface ThreadReplyPayload {
  parentId: string;
  content: string;
}

export const useAddThreadReply = () => {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const channelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);
  const userId = useAppSelector((s) => s.auth.user?.id);

  return useMutation<Message, Error, ThreadReplyPayload>({
    mutationFn: ({ parentId, content }) =>
      axiosInstance
        .post(`/channels/${channelId}/messages/${parentId}/replies`, {
          content,
        })
        .then((r) => r.data),

    onMutate: async ({ parentId, content }) => {
      await queryClient.cancelQueries({ queryKey: ['messages', channelId] });
      const previous = queryClient.getQueryData<Message[]>([
        'messages',
        channelId,
      ]);

      const tempId = `thread_temp_${Date.now()}`;
      const tempReply: Message = {
        id: tempId,
        channelId: channelId!,
        authorId: userId!,
        content,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        edited: false,
        reactions: [],
        thread: [],
        attachments: [],
      };

      queryClient.setQueryData<Message[]>(['messages', channelId], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((m) =>
          m.id === parentId ? { ...m, thread: [...m.thread, tempReply] } : m,
        ),
      );

      return { previous, tempId };
    },

    onSuccess: (real, { parentId }, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData<Message[]>(['messages', channelId], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((m) =>
          m.id === parentId
            ? {
                ...m,
                thread: m.thread.map((t) => (t.id === ctx?.tempId ? real : t)),
              }
            : m,
        ),
      );
    },

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(['messages', channelId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to add reply');
    },
  });
};

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';
import type { Message } from '@/data/mockData';

export const useDeleteMessage = () => {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const channelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);

  return useMutation<void, Error, string>({
    mutationFn: (messageId) =>
      axiosInstance
        .delete(`/channels/${channelId}/messages/${messageId}`)
        .then((r) => r.data),

    onMutate: async (messageId) => {
      await queryClient.cancelQueries({ queryKey: ['messages', channelId] });
      const previous = queryClient.getQueryData<Message[]>([
        'messages',
        channelId,
      ]);

      queryClient.setQueryData<Message[]>(['messages', channelId], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).filter((m) => m.id !== messageId),
      );

      return { previous };
    },

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(['messages', channelId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to delete message');
    },
  });
};

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(['messages', channelId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to edit message');

import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

import type { Message } from '@/data/mockData';

export const useGetMessages = () => {
  const channelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);

  return useQuery<Message[]>({
    queryKey: ['messages', channelId],
    queryFn: () =>
      axiosInstance.get(`/channels/${channelId}/messages`).then((r) => r.data),
    enabled: !!channelId,
    staleTime: 1000 * 30, // 30s — messages go stale quickly
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\messages\useSendMessage.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

import type { Message } from '@/data/mockData';

interface SendMessagePayload {
  content: string;
  attachments?: Message['attachments'];
}

export const useSendMessage = () => {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const channelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);
  const userId = useAppSelector((s) => s.auth.user?.id);

  return useMutation<Message, Error, SendMessagePayload>({
    mutationFn: ({ content, attachments }) =>
      axiosInstance
        .post(`/channels/${channelId}/messages`, { content, attachments })
        .then((r) => r.data),

    onMutate: async ({ content, attachments = [] }) => {
      await queryClient.cancelQueries({ queryKey: ['messages', channelId] });
      const previous = queryClient.getQueryData<Message[]>([
        'messages',
        channelId,
      ]);

      const tempId = `temp_${Date.now()}`;
      const tempMsg: Message = {
        id: tempId,
        channelId: channelId!,
        authorId: userId!,
        content,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        edited: false,
        reactions: [],
        thread: [],
        attachments,
      };

      queryClient.setQueryData<Message[]>(['messages', channelId], (old) => [
        ...(old ?? []),
        tempMsg,
      ]);

      return { previous, tempId };
    },

    onSuccess: (real, _, ctx) => {
      // Replace optimistic message with real one from server
      queryClient.setQueryData<Message[]>(['messages', channelId], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((m) => (m.id === ctx?.tempId ? real : m)),
      );
    },

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(['messages', channelId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to send message');
    },
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\messages\useTogglePin.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

import type { Channel } from '@/data/mockData';

export const useTogglePin = () => {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const channelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);
  const workspaceId = useAppSelector((s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId);

  return useMutation<void, Error, string>({
    mutationFn: (messageId) =>
      axiosInstance
        .post(`/channels/${channelId}/messages/${messageId}/pin`)
        .then((r) => r.data),

    onMutate: async (messageId) => {
      await queryClient.cancelQueries({ queryKey: ['channels', workspaceId] });
      const previous = queryClient.getQueryData<Channel[]>([
        'channels',
        workspaceId,
      ]);

      queryClient.setQueryData<Channel[]>(['channels', workspaceId], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((ch) => {
          if (ch.id !== channelId) return ch;
          const isPinned = ch.pinnedMessages.includes(messageId);
          return {
            ...ch,
            pinnedMessages: isPinned
              ? ch.pinnedMessages.filter((id) => id !== messageId)
              : [...ch.pinnedMessages, messageId],
          };
        }),
      );

      return { previous };
    },

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(['channels', workspaceId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to toggle pin');
    },
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\messages\useToggleReaction.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';
import type { Message, Reaction } from '@/data/mockData';

interface ToggleReactionPayload {
  messageId: string;
  emoji: string;
}

const applyReactionToggle = (
  messages: Message[],
  messageId: string,
  emoji: string,
  userId: string,
): Message[] =>
  messages.map((m) => {
    if (m.id === messageId) {
      const existing = m.reactions.find((r) => r.emoji === emoji);
      let newReactions: Reaction[];
      if (existing) {
        const filtered = existing.userIds.filter((u) => u !== userId);
        if (existing.userIds.includes(userId)) {
          newReactions =
            filtered.length > 0
              ? m.reactions.map((r) =>
                  r.emoji === emoji ? { ...r, userIds: filtered } : r,
                )
              : m.reactions.filter((r) => r.emoji !== emoji);
        } else {
          newReactions = m.reactions.map((r) =>
            r.emoji === emoji ? { ...r, userIds: [...r.userIds, userId] } : r,
          );
        }
      } else {
        newReactions = [...m.reactions, { emoji, userIds: [userId] }];
      }
      return { ...m, reactions: newReactions };
    }
    // Also apply to thread replies
    return {
      ...m,
      thread: applyReactionToggle(m.thread, messageId, emoji, userId),
    };
  });

export const useToggleReaction = () => {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();
  const channelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);
  const userId = useAppSelector((s) => s.auth.user?.id);

  return useMutation<void, Error, ToggleReactionPayload>({
    mutationFn: ({ messageId, emoji }) =>
      axiosInstance
        .post(`/channels/${channelId}/messages/${messageId}/reactions`, {
          emoji,
        })
        .then((r) => r.data),

    onMutate: async ({ messageId, emoji }) => {
      await queryClient.cancelQueries({ queryKey: ['messages', channelId] });
      const previous = queryClient.getQueryData<Message[]>([
        'messages',
        channelId,
      ]);

      queryClient.setQueryData<Message[]>(['messages', channelId], (old) =>
        applyReactionToggle(old ?? [], messageId, emoji, userId!),
      );

      return { previous };
    },

    onError: (_, __, ctx) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData(['messages', channelId], ctx?.previous);
      toast.error('Failed to update reaction');
    },
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\notifications\useGetNotifications.ts

import { useQuery, useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

import type { Notification } from '@/data/mockData';

export const useGetNotifications = () =>
  useQuery<Notification[]>({
    queryKey: ['notifications'],
    queryFn: () => axiosInstance.get('/notifications').then((r) => r.data),
    refetchInterval: 1000 * 30, // poll every 30s until you have sockets
  });

export const useMarkNotificationRead = () => {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  return useMutation<void, Error, string>({
    mutationFn: (id) =>
      axiosInstance.patch(`/notifications/${id}/read`).then((r) => r.data),
    onMutate: (id) => {
      queryClient.setQueryData<Notification[]>(['notifications'], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((n) => (n.id === id ? { ...n, read: true } : n)),
      );
    },
    onError: () => toast.error('Failed to mark notification read'),
  });
};

export const useMarkAllNotificationsRead = () => {
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  return useMutation<void, Error, void>({
    mutationFn: () =>
      axiosInstance.patch('/notifications/read-all').then((r) => r.data),
    onMutate: () => {
      queryClient.setQueryData<Notification[]>(['notifications'], (old) =>
        (old ?? []).map((n) => ({ ...n, read: true })),
      );
    },
    onError: () => toast.error('Failed to mark all notifications read'),
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\use-mobile.ts

import * as React from "react"

const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768

export function useIsMobile() {
  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(undefined)

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`)
    const onChange = () => {
      setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
    }
    mql.addEventListener("change", onChange)
    setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT)
    return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange)
  }, [])

  return !!isMobile
}

import type { AppDispatch } from '@/app/store';
import { useDispatch } from 'react-redux';


/**
 * Typed dispatch hook — always use this instead of plain `useDispatch`.
 * Gives correct types for async thunks.
 */
const useAppDispatch = () => useDispatch<AppDispatch>();
export default useAppDispatch;

import { TypedUseSelectorHook, useSelector } from 'react-redux';

import { RootState } from '@/store';

/**
 * Typed selector hook — always use this instead of plain `useSelector`.
 */
const useAppSelector: TypedUseSelectorHook<RootState> = useSelector;
export default useAppSelector;

import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

import type { User } from '@/data/mockData';

// Fetch all users in the workspace — cached indefinitely (users rarely change)
export const useGetWorkspaceUsers = () => {
  const workspaceId = useAppSelector((s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId);

  return useQuery<User[]>({
    queryKey: ['users', workspaceId],
    queryFn: () =>
      axiosInstance
        .get(`/workspaces/${workspaceId}/members`)
        .then((r) => r.data),
    enabled: !!workspaceId,
    staleTime: Infinity,
  });
};

// Replaces: getUser(id) — returns a single user from the cached list
export const useGetUser = (userId: string) => {
  const workspaceId = useAppSelector((s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId);

  return useQuery<User[], Error, User | undefined>({
    queryKey: ['users', workspaceId],
    queryFn: () =>
      axiosInstance
        .get(`/workspaces/${workspaceId}/members`)
        .then((r) => r.data),
    enabled: !!workspaceId,
    staleTime: Infinity,
    select: (users) => users.find((u) => u.id === userId),
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\workspace\useCreateWorkspace.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppDispatch } from '@/app/hooks';
import { setCurrentWorkspaceId } from '@/features/workspaceSlice';
import { setCurrentChannelId } from '@/features/channelSlice';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

import type { Workspace } from '@/data/mockData';

interface CreateWorkspacePayload {
  name: string;
  icon: string;
  description: string;
  firstChannel: string;
}

export const useCreateWorkspace = () => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  return useMutation<Workspace, Error, CreateWorkspacePayload>({
    mutationFn: (payload) =>
      axiosInstance.post('/workspaces', payload).then((r) => r.data),
    onSuccess: (ws) => {
      // Invalidate workspace list so useGetWorkspaces refetches
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['workspaces'] });
      dispatch(setCurrentWorkspaceId(ws.id));
      dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(ws.channels[0]?.id ?? null));
      toast.success(`Workspace "${ws.name}" created`);
    },
    onError: () => toast.error('Failed to create workspace'),
  });
};


==============================
FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\workspace\useGetWorkspaces.ts
==============================

import { useQuery } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppDispatch, useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';
import { setCurrentWorkspaceId } from '@/features/workspaceSlice';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

import type { Workspace } from '@/data/mockData';

export const useGetWorkspaces = () => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const currentWorkspaceId = useAppSelector(
    (s) => s.workspace.currentWorkspaceId,
  );

  return useQuery<Workspace[]>({
    queryKey: ['workspaces'],
    queryFn: async () => {
      const { data } = await axiosInstance.get('/workspaces');
      // Auto-select first workspace if none selected yet
      if (!currentWorkspaceId && data.length > 0) {
        dispatch(setCurrentWorkspaceId(data[0].id));
      }
      return data;
    },
  });
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\hooks\workspace\useJoinWorkspace.ts
==============================

import { useMutation, useQueryClient } from '@tanstack/react-query';
import { useAppDispatch } from '@/app/hooks';
import { setCurrentWorkspaceId } from '@/features/workspaceSlice';
import { setCurrentChannelId } from '@/features/channelSlice';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';
import type { Workspace } from '@/data/mockData';

export const useJoinWorkspace = () => {
  const dispatch = useAppDispatch();
  const queryClient = useQueryClient();

  return useMutation<Workspace, Error, string>({
    mutationFn: (code) =>
      axiosInstance.post('/workspaces/join', { code }).then((r) => r.data),
    onSuccess: (ws) => {
      queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['workspaces'] });
      dispatch(setCurrentWorkspaceId(ws.id));
      dispatch(setCurrentChannelId(ws.channels[0]?.id ?? null));
      toast.success(`Joined workspace "${ws.name}"`);
    },
    onError: () => toast.error('Invalid invite code'),
  });
};

export const LOCALE_LABELS: Record<Locale, string> = {
  en: 'English',
  es: 'Español',
  fr: 'Français',
  ja: '日本語',
  ar: 'العربية',
};

export const RTL_LOCALES: Locale[] = ['ar'];

export function t(key: string, locale: Locale = 'en'): string {
  return dictionaries[locale]?.[key] || dictionaries.en[key] || key;
}

// ── Dummy Backend Layer ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
import {
  mockUsers,
  mockWorkspaces,
  seedMessages,
  seedNotifications,
  type User,
  type Workspace,
  type Channel,
  type Message,
  type DM,
  type Notification,
  type Reaction,
  type Attachment,
  type Poll,
  type PollOption,
} from '@/data/mockData';

// ── Helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const delay = (ms = 80) => new Promise<void>((r) => setTimeout(r, ms));
export const generateId = () =>
  `${Date.now()}_${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 8)}`;

const fail = (code: string, message: string): never => {
  throw { code, message };
};

// ── In-Memory Stores ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

let usersStore = new Map<string, User>(mockUsers.map((u) => [u.id, { ...u }]));
let workspacesStore = new Map<string, Workspace>(
  mockWorkspaces.map((w) => [w.id, JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(w))]),
);
let messagesStore = new Map<string, Message[]>(
  Object.entries(seedMessages).map(([k, v]) => [
    k,
    JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(v)),
  ]),
);
let notificationsStore: Notification[] = JSON.parse(
  JSON.stringify(seedNotifications),
);
let sessionStore: { token: string; userId: string } | null = null;
let readStates = new Map<string, Map<string, string>>(); // userId -> channelId -> lastReadMessageId
let searchHistory = new Map<string, string[]>(); // userId -> recent queries
let userPrefs = new Map<
  string,
  { theme: string; notifications: Record<string, boolean> }
>();

// Init read states for all users
mockUsers.forEach((u) => readStates.set(u.id, new Map()));

// Password store (email -> password) — seeded users have "password"
const passwords = new Map<string, string>(
  mockUsers.map((u) => [u.email, 'password']),
);

// Polls store (pollId -> Poll)
let pollsStore = new Map<string, Poll>();

// Bookmarks store (userId -> { messageId, channelId, channelName, savedAt, tags }[])
let bookmarksStore = new Map<
  string,
  {
    messageId: string;
    channelId: string;
    channelName: string;
    savedAt: string;
    tags: string[];
  }[]
>();

// ── Auth ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const auth = {
  async login(
    email: string,
    password: string,
  ): Promise<{ user: User; token: string }> {
    await delay(600);
    const user = Array.from(usersStore.values()).find((u) => u.email === email);
    if (!user) fail('INVALID_CREDENTIALS', 'No account found with that email');
    if (passwords.get(email) !== password)
      fail('INVALID_CREDENTIALS', 'Incorrect password');
    const token = `mock-jwt-${user!.id}-${Date.now()}`;
    sessionStore = { token, userId: user!.id };
    sessionStorage.setItem('linkly_session', JSON.stringify(sessionStore));
    return { user: { ...user! }, token };
  },

  async signup(
    email: string,
    password: string,
    fullName: string,
    username: string,
  ): Promise<{ user: User; token: string }> {
    await delay(800);
    if (Array.from(usersStore.values()).some((u) => u.email === email))
      fail('EMAIL_TAKEN', 'Email already registered');
    if (Array.from(usersStore.values()).some((u) => u.username === username))
      fail('USERNAME_TAKEN', 'Username already taken');
    const id = `u_${generateId()}`;
    const user: User = {
      id,
      username,
      displayName: fullName,
      email,
      avatar: `https://api.dicebear.com/7.x/avataaars/svg?seed=${encodeURIComponent(fullName)}`,
      status: 'online',
      statusEmoji: '',
      statusText: '',
      bio: '',
      title: '',
      timezone: Intl.DateTimeFormat().resolvedOptions().timeZone,
      memberSince: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],
    };
    usersStore.set(id, user);
    passwords.set(email, password);
    readStates.set(id, new Map());
    // Add to first workspace
    const w1 = workspacesStore.get('w1');
    if (w1) {
      w1.members.push(id);
      w1.channels.forEach((ch) => {
        if (!ch.isPrivate) ch.members.push(id);
      });
    }
    const token = `mock-jwt-${id}-${Date.now()}`;
    sessionStore = { token, userId: id };
    sessionStorage.setItem('linkly_session', JSON.stringify(sessionStore));
    return { user: { ...user }, token };
  },

  async logout(): Promise<void> {
    await delay(50);
    sessionStore = null;
    sessionStorage.removeItem('linkly_session');
  },

  async getSession(): Promise<{ user: User; token: string } | null> {
    await delay(100);
    const stored = sessionStorage.getItem('linkly_session');
    if (stored) {
      const s = JSON.parse(stored);
      const user = usersStore.get(s.userId);
      if (user) {
        sessionStore = s;
        return { user: { ...user }, token: s.token };
      }
    }
    // Check localStorage for "remember me"
    const remembered = localStorage.getItem('linkly_remember');
    if (remembered) {
      const s = JSON.parse(remembered);
      const user = usersStore.get(s.userId);
      if (user) {
        sessionStore = s;
        sessionStorage.setItem('linkly_session', remembered);
        return { user: { ...user }, token: s.token };
      }
    }
    return null;
  },

  async updateProfile(userId: string, fields: Partial<User>): Promise<User> {
    await delay(100);
    const user = usersStore.get(userId);
    if (!user) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'User not found');
    const updated = { ...user!, ...fields, id: user!.id };
    usersStore.set(userId, updated);
    return { ...updated };
  },

  async changePassword(
    userId: string,
    currentPass: string,
    newPass: string,
  ): Promise<void> {
    await delay(200);
    const user = usersStore.get(userId);
    if (!user) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'User not found');
    if (passwords.get(user.email) !== currentPass)
      fail('INVALID_PASSWORD', 'Current password is incorrect');
    passwords.set(user.email, newPass);
  },

  async requestPasswordReset(
    email: string,
  ): Promise<{ success: boolean; message: string }> {
    await delay(500);
    return {
      success: true,
      message:
        'If an account exists with that email, a reset link has been sent.',
    };
  },

  async checkUsernameAvailable(username: string): Promise<boolean> {
    await delay(300);
    return !Array.from(usersStore.values()).some(
      (u) => u.username === username,
    );
  },

  rememberSession() {
    if (sessionStore)
      localStorage.setItem('linkly_remember', JSON.stringify(sessionStore));
  },
};

// ── Users ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const users = {
  async getUser(id: string): Promise<User | null> {
    await delay();
    return usersStore.get(id) ? { ...usersStore.get(id)! } : null;
  },
  async searchUsers(query: string): Promise<User[]> {
    await delay();
    const q = query.toLowerCase();
    return Array.from(usersStore.values())
      .filter(
        (u) =>
          u.displayName.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          u.username.toLowerCase().includes(q),
      )
      .map((u) => ({ ...u }));
  },
  async updateStatus(
    userId: string,
    status: { emoji: string; text: string; duration?: number },
  ): Promise<User> {
    await delay();
    const user = usersStore.get(userId);
    if (!user) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'User not found');
    user!.statusEmoji = status.emoji;
    user!.statusText = status.text;
    return { ...user! };
  },
  async getAll(): Promise<User[]> {
    await delay();
    return Array.from(usersStore.values()).map((u) => ({ ...u }));
  },
  async getPrefs(
    userId: string,
  ): Promise<{ theme: string; notifications: Record<string, boolean> } | null> {
    await delay();
    return userPrefs.get(userId) || null;
  },
  async savePrefs(
    userId: string,
    prefs: Partial<{ theme: string; notifications: Record<string, boolean> }>,
  ): Promise<void> {
    await delay();
    const existing = userPrefs.get(userId) || {
      theme: 'dark',
      notifications: { desktop: true, mobile: true, email: false, sound: true },
    };
    userPrefs.set(userId, { ...existing, ...prefs });
  },
};

// ── Workspaces ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const workspaces = {
  async list(userId: string): Promise<Workspace[]> {
    await delay();
    return Array.from(workspacesStore.values())
      .filter((w) => w.members.includes(userId))
      .map((w) => ({ ...w }));
  },
  async get(id: string): Promise<Workspace | null> {
    await delay();
    const w = workspacesStore.get(id);
    return w ? { ...w } : null;
  },
  async create(
    name: string,
    icon: string,
    description: string,
    firstChannel: string,
    ownerId: string,
  ): Promise<Workspace> {
    await delay(150);
    const id = `ws_${generateId()}`;
    const chId = `ch_${generateId()}`;
    const ws: Workspace = {
      id,
      name,
      icon,
      description,
      ownerId,
      members: [ownerId],
      joinCode: Math.random().toString(36).substring(2, 8).toUpperCase(),
      channels: [
        {
          id: chId,
          name: firstChannel || 'general',
          type: 'text',
          description: 'Default channel',
          isPrivate: false,
          pinnedMessages: [],
          members: [ownerId],
          unreadCount: 0,
          muted: false,
        },
      ],
      dms: [],
    };
    workspacesStore.set(id, ws);
    messagesStore.set(chId, [
      {
        id: `sys_${generateId()}`,
        channelId: chId,
        authorId: 'system',
        content: `Channel #${firstChannel || 'general'} was created`,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        edited: false,
        reactions: [],
        thread: [],
        attachments: [],
        isSystem: true,
      },
    ]);
    return { ...ws };
  },
  async join(code: string, userId: string): Promise<Workspace | null> {
    await delay();
    const ws = Array.from(workspacesStore.values()).find(
      (w) => w.joinCode.toLowerCase() === code.toLowerCase(),
    );
    if (!ws) return null;
    if (!ws.members.includes(userId)) {
      ws.members.push(userId);
      ws.channels.forEach((ch) => {
        if (!ch.isPrivate) ch.members.push(userId);
      });
    }
    return { ...ws };
  },
  async update(
    id: string,
    fields: Partial<Pick<Workspace, 'name' | 'icon' | 'description'>>,
  ): Promise<Workspace> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(id);
    if (!ws) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'Workspace not found');
    Object.assign(ws!, fields);
    return { ...ws! };
  },
  async leave(id: string, userId: string): Promise<void> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(id);
    if (!ws) return;
    ws.members = ws.members.filter((m) => m !== userId);
    ws.channels.forEach((ch) => {
      ch.members = ch.members.filter((m) => m !== userId);
    });
  },
};

// ── Channels ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const channels = {
  async list(workspaceId: string): Promise<Channel[]> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    return ws ? [...ws.channels] : [];
  },
  async get(workspaceId: string, channelId: string): Promise<Channel | null> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    return ws?.channels.find((c) => c.id === channelId) || null;
  },
  async create(
    workspaceId: string,
    data: Omit<Channel, 'id' | 'pinnedMessages' | 'unreadCount' | 'muted'>,
  ): Promise<Channel> {
    await delay(120);
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    if (!ws) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'Workspace not found');
    const ch: Channel = {
      ...data,
      id: `ch_${generateId()}`,
      pinnedMessages: [],
      unreadCount: 0,
      muted: false,
    };
    ws!.channels.push(ch);
    messagesStore.set(ch.id, [
      {
        id: `sys_${generateId()}`,
        channelId: ch.id,
        authorId: 'system',
        content: `Channel #${ch.name} was created`,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        edited: false,
        reactions: [],
        thread: [],
        attachments: [],
        isSystem: true,
      },
    ]);
    return { ...ch };
  },
  async join(
    workspaceId: string,
    channelId: string,
    userId: string,
  ): Promise<void> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    const ch = ws?.channels.find((c) => c.id === channelId);
    if (ch && !ch.members.includes(userId)) ch.members.push(userId);
  },
  async leave(
    workspaceId: string,
    channelId: string,
    userId: string,
  ): Promise<void> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    const ch = ws?.channels.find((c) => c.id === channelId);
    if (ch) ch.members = ch.members.filter((m) => m !== userId);
  },
  async getMembers(workspaceId: string, channelId: string): Promise<User[]> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    const ch = ws?.channels.find((c) => c.id === channelId);
    if (!ch) return [];
    return ch.members.map((id) => usersStore.get(id)).filter(Boolean) as User[];
  },
};

// ── Messages ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const messages = {
  async list(
    channelId: string,
    opts?: { before?: string; limit?: number },
  ): Promise<Message[]> {
    await delay();
    const msgs = messagesStore.get(channelId) || [];
    const limit = opts?.limit || 30;
    if (opts?.before) {
      const idx = msgs.findIndex((m) => m.id === opts.before);
      if (idx <= 0) return [];
      return msgs.slice(Math.max(0, idx - limit), idx);
    }
    return msgs.slice(-limit);
  },
  async send(
    channelId: string,
    authorId: string,
    content: string,
    attachments: Attachment[] = [],
  ): Promise<Message> {
    await delay(100);
    const msg: Message = {
      id: `msg_${generateId()}`,
      channelId,
      authorId,
      content,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      edited: false,
      reactions: [],
      thread: [],
      attachments,
    };
    const msgs = messagesStore.get(channelId) || [];
    msgs.push(msg);
    messagesStore.set(channelId, msgs);
    return { ...msg };
  },
  async edit(
    channelId: string,
    messageId: string,
    newContent: string,
  ): Promise<Message> {
    await delay();
    const msgs = messagesStore.get(channelId) || [];
    const msg = msgs.find((m) => m.id === messageId);
    if (!msg) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'Message not found');
    msg!.content = newContent;
    msg!.edited = true;
    msg!.editedAt = new Date().toISOString();
    return { ...msg! };
  },
  async delete(channelId: string, messageId: string): Promise<void> {
    await delay();
    const msgs = messagesStore.get(channelId) || [];
    messagesStore.set(
      channelId,
      msgs.filter((m) => m.id !== messageId),
    );
  },
  async toggleReaction(
    channelId: string,
    messageId: string,
    emoji: string,
    userId: string,
  ): Promise<Message | null> {
    await delay(50);
    const msgs = messagesStore.get(channelId) || [];
    const updateReactions = (list: Message[]): Message | null => {
      for (const m of list) {
        if (m.id === messageId) {
          const existing = m.reactions.find((r) => r.emoji === emoji);
          if (existing) {
            if (existing.userIds.includes(userId)) {
              existing.userIds = existing.userIds.filter((u) => u !== userId);
              if (existing.userIds.length === 0)
                m.reactions = m.reactions.filter((r) => r.emoji !== emoji);
            } else {
              existing.userIds.push(userId);
            }
          } else {
            m.reactions.push({ emoji, userIds: [userId] });
          }
          return { ...m };
        }
        const found = updateReactions(m.thread);
        if (found) return found;
      }
      return null;
    };
    return updateReactions(msgs);
  },
  async pin(
    channelId: string,
    messageId: string,
    workspaceId: string,
  ): Promise<void> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    const ch = ws?.channels.find((c) => c.id === channelId);
    if (ch) {
      if (ch.pinnedMessages.includes(messageId)) {
        ch.pinnedMessages = ch.pinnedMessages.filter((id) => id !== messageId);
      } else {
        ch.pinnedMessages.push(messageId);
      }
    }
  },
  async getAll(channelId: string): Promise<Message[]> {
    await delay();
    return [...(messagesStore.get(channelId) || [])];
  },
  async search(
    query: string,
    opts?: {
      channelId?: string;
      authorId?: string;
      hasAttachments?: boolean;
      dateFrom?: string;
      dateTo?: string;
    },
  ): Promise<Message[]> {
    await delay(100);
    const q = query.toLowerCase();
    const results: Message[] = [];
    messagesStore.forEach((msgs, chId) => {
      if (opts?.channelId && chId !== opts.channelId) return;
      msgs.forEach((msg) => {
        if (msg.isSystem) return;
        if (opts?.authorId && msg.authorId !== opts.authorId) return;
        if (opts?.hasAttachments && msg.attachments.length === 0) return;
        if (opts?.dateFrom && msg.timestamp < opts.dateFrom) return;
        if (opts?.dateTo && msg.timestamp > opts.dateTo) return;
        if (msg.content.toLowerCase().includes(q))
          results.push({ ...msg, channelId: chId });
      });
    });
    return results.sort(
      (a, b) =>
        new Date(b.timestamp).getTime() - new Date(a.timestamp).getTime(),
    );
  },
};
