const threads = {
  async getReplies(channelId: string, parentId: string): Promise<Message[]> {
    await delay();
    const msgs = messagesStore.get(channelId) || [];
    const parent = msgs.find((m) => m.id === parentId);
    return parent ? [...parent.thread] : [];
  },
  async addReply(
    channelId: string,
    parentId: string,
    content: string,
    userId: string,
  ): Promise<Message> {
    await delay(80);
    const reply: Message = {
      id: `thread_${generateId()}`,
      channelId,
      authorId: userId,
      content,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      edited: false,
      reactions: [],
      thread: [],
      attachments: [],
    };
    const msgs = messagesStore.get(channelId) || [];
    const parent = msgs.find((m) => m.id === parentId);
    if (!parent) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'Parent message not found');
    parent!.thread.push(reply);
    return { ...reply };
  },
};

// ── DMs ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const dms = {
  async list(workspaceId: string, userId: string): Promise<DM[]> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    return ws?.dms.filter((d) => d.participantIds.includes(userId)) || [];
  },
  async getOrCreate(
    workspaceId: string,
    userId1: string,
    userId2: string,
  ): Promise<DM> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    if (!ws) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'Workspace not found');
    let dm = ws!.dms.find(
      (d) =>
        d.participantIds.includes(userId1) &&
        d.participantIds.includes(userId2),
    );
    if (!dm) {
      dm = {
        id: `dm_${generateId()}`,
        participantIds: [userId1, userId2],
        messages: [],
        unreadCount: 0,
      };
      ws!.dms.push(dm);
    }
    return { ...dm };
  },
  async getMessages(workspaceId: string, dmId: string): Promise<Message[]> {
    await delay();
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    const dm = ws?.dms.find((d) => d.id === dmId);
    return dm ? [...dm.messages] : [];
  },
  async sendMessage(
    workspaceId: string,
    dmId: string,
    authorId: string,
    content: string,
  ): Promise<Message> {
    await delay(80);
    const ws = workspacesStore.get(workspaceId);
    const dm = ws?.dms.find((d) => d.id === dmId);
    if (!dm) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'DM not found');
    const msg: Message = {
      id: `dm_msg_${generateId()}`,
      dmId,
      authorId,
      content,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      edited: false,
      reactions: [],
      thread: [],
      attachments: [],
    };
    dm!.messages.push(msg);
    return { ...msg };
  },
};

// ── Search ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const search = {
  async global(
    query: string,
    filters?: {
      type?: string;
      channelId?: string;
      authorId?: string;
      dateFrom?: string;
      dateTo?: string;
      hasFiles?: boolean;
      hasLinks?: boolean;
      hasReactions?: boolean;
    },
  ): Promise<{
    messages: (Message & { channelName?: string })[];
    channels: Channel[];
    people: User[];
    files: { message: Message; attachment: Attachment; channelName?: string }[];
    total: number;
  }> {
    await delay(100);
    const q = query.toLowerCase();
    const msgResults: (Message & { channelName?: string })[] = [];
    const fileResults: {
      message: Message;
      attachment: Attachment;
      channelName?: string;
    }[] = [];
    const channelResults: Channel[] = [];
    const peopleResults: User[] = [];

    // Search messages and files
    if (
      !filters?.type ||
      filters.type === 'all' ||
      filters.type === 'messages' ||
      filters.type === 'files'
    ) {
      messagesStore.forEach((msgs, chId) => {
        if (filters?.channelId && chId !== filters.channelId) return;
        const ws = Array.from(workspacesStore.values()).find((w) =>
          w.channels.some((c) => c.id === chId),
        );
        const ch = ws?.channels.find((c) => c.id === chId);
        msgs.forEach((msg) => {
          if (msg.isSystem) return;
          if (filters?.authorId && msg.authorId !== filters.authorId) return;
          if (filters?.dateFrom && msg.timestamp < filters.dateFrom) return;
          if (filters?.dateTo && msg.timestamp > filters.dateTo) return;
          if (filters?.hasReactions && msg.reactions.length === 0) return;
          if (filters?.hasFiles && msg.attachments.length === 0) return;
          if (filters?.hasLinks && !msg.content.includes('http')) return;

          if (
            (!filters?.type ||
              filters.type === 'all' ||
              filters.type === 'messages') &&
            msg.content.toLowerCase().includes(q)
          ) {
            msgResults.push({ ...msg, channelId: chId, channelName: ch?.name });
          }
          if (
            !filters?.type ||
            filters.type === 'all' ||
            filters.type === 'files'
          ) {
            msg.attachments.forEach((att) => {
              if (att.name.toLowerCase().includes(q)) {
                fileResults.push({
                  message: { ...msg, channelId: chId },
                  attachment: att,
                  channelName: ch?.name,
                });
              }
            });
          }
        });
      });
    }

    // Search channels
    if (
      !filters?.type ||
      filters.type === 'all' ||
      filters.type === 'channels'
    ) {
      workspacesStore.forEach((ws) => {
        ws.channels.forEach((ch) => {
          if (
            ch.name.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
            ch.description.toLowerCase().includes(q)
          ) {
            channelResults.push({ ...ch });
          }
        });
      });
    }

    // Search people
    if (!filters?.type || filters.type === 'all' || filters.type === 'people') {
      usersStore.forEach((u) => {
        if (
          u.displayName.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          u.username.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
          u.title.toLowerCase().includes(q)
        ) {
          peopleResults.push({ ...u });
        }
      });
    }

    msgResults.sort(
      (a, b) =>
        new Date(b.timestamp).getTime() - new Date(a.timestamp).getTime(),
    );
    return {
      messages: msgResults.slice(0, 20),
      channels: channelResults,
      people: peopleResults,
      files: fileResults,
      total:
        msgResults.length +
        channelResults.length +
        peopleResults.length +
        fileResults.length,
    };
  },

  async addToHistory(userId: string, query: string): Promise<void> {
    const history = searchHistory.get(userId) || [];
    searchHistory.set(
      userId,
      [query, ...history.filter((s) => s !== query)].slice(0, 10),
    );
  },
  async getHistory(userId: string): Promise<string[]> {
    await delay(50);
    return searchHistory.get(userId) || [];
  },
  async clearHistoryItem(userId: string, query: string): Promise<void> {
    const history = searchHistory.get(userId) || [];
    searchHistory.set(
      userId,
      history.filter((s) => s !== query),
    );
  },
};

const notifications = {

// ── Read States ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const readStatesApi = {
  async markRead(
    userId: string,
    channelId: string,
    lastMessageId: string,
  ): Promise<void> {
    await delay(30);
    let userStates = readStates.get(userId);
    if (!userStates) {
      userStates = new Map();
      readStates.set(userId, userStates);
    }
    userStates.set(channelId, lastMessageId);
  },
  async getUnreadCount(userId: string, channelId: string): Promise<number> {
    const userStates = readStates.get(userId);
    const lastRead = userStates?.get(channelId);
    const msgs = messagesStore.get(channelId) || [];
    if (!lastRead)
      return msgs.filter((m) => !m.isSystem).length > 0
        ? msgs.filter((m) => !m.isSystem && m.authorId !== userId).length
        : 0;
    const idx = msgs.findIndex((m) => m.id === lastRead);
    if (idx === -1) return 0;
    return msgs
      .slice(idx + 1)
      .filter((m) => !m.isSystem && m.authorId !== userId).length;
  },
};

// ── Files ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const files = {
  async upload(
    file: File,
  ): Promise<{ url: string; name: string; size: string }> {
    await delay(300);
    const url = URL.createObjectURL(file);
    return {
      url,
      name: file.name,
      size: `${(file.size / 1024).toFixed(0)} KB`,
    };
  },
  async getUserFiles(
    userId: string,
  ): Promise<{ attachment: Attachment; channelName: string; date: string }[]> {
    await delay();
    const results: {
      attachment: Attachment;
      channelName: string;
      date: string;
    }[] = [];
    messagesStore.forEach((msgs, chId) => {
      const ws = Array.from(workspacesStore.values()).find((w) =>
        w.channels.some((c) => c.id === chId),
      );
      const ch = ws?.channels.find((c) => c.id === chId);
      msgs.forEach((msg) => {
        if (msg.authorId === userId && msg.attachments.length > 0) {
          msg.attachments.forEach((att) => {
            results.push({
              attachment: att,
              channelName: ch?.name || 'Unknown',
              date: msg.timestamp,
            });
          });
        }
      });
    });
    return results;
  },
};

const polls = {
  async create(data: {
    question: string;
    options: string[];
    creatorId: string;
    anonymous: boolean;
    endDate?: string;
    channelId: string;
    messageId: string;
  }): Promise<Poll> {
    await delay(100);
    const poll: Poll = {
      id: `poll_${generateId()}`,
      question: data.question,
      options: data.options.map((text, i) => ({
        id: `opt_${i}`,
        text,
        votes: [],
      })),
      creatorId: data.creatorId,
      anonymous: data.anonymous,
      endDate: data.endDate,
      channelId: data.channelId,
      messageId: data.messageId,
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };
    pollsStore.set(poll.id, poll);
    return { ...poll };
  },
  async get(pollId: string): Promise<Poll | null> {
    await delay(50);
    const p = pollsStore.get(pollId);
    return p
      ? { ...p, options: p.options.map((o) => ({ ...o, votes: [...o.votes] })) }
      : null;
  },
  async vote(pollId: string, optionId: string, userId: string): Promise<Poll> {
    await delay(80);
    const p = pollsStore.get(pollId);
    if (!p) fail('NOT_FOUND', 'Poll not found');
    // Remove previous vote
    p!.options.forEach((o) => {
      o.votes = o.votes.filter((v) => v !== userId);
    });
    // Add new vote
    const opt = p!.options.find((o) => o.id === optionId);
    if (opt) opt.votes.push(userId);
    return {
      ...p!,
      options: p!.options.map((o) => ({ ...o, votes: [...o.votes] })),
    };
  },
};

// ── Bookmarks ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const bookmarks = {
  async list(
    userId: string,
  ): Promise<
    {
      messageId: string;
      channelId: string;
      channelName: string;
      savedAt: string;
      tags: string[];
    }[]
  > {
    await delay(80);
    return [...(bookmarksStore.get(userId) || [])];
  },
  async toggle(
    userId: string,
    messageId: string,
    channelId: string,
    channelName: string,
  ): Promise<boolean> {
    await delay(50);
    let items = bookmarksStore.get(userId) || [];
    const existing = items.find((b) => b.messageId === messageId);
    if (existing) {
      items = items.filter((b) => b.messageId !== messageId);
      bookmarksStore.set(userId, items);
      return false; // removed
    } else {
      items.push({
        messageId,
        channelId,
        channelName,
        savedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        tags: [],
      });
      bookmarksStore.set(userId, items);
      return true; // added
    }
  },
  async isBookmarked(userId: string, messageId: string): Promise<boolean> {
    const items = bookmarksStore.get(userId) || [];
    return items.some((b) => b.messageId === messageId);
  },
};

import {
  createContext,
  useContext,
  useEffect,
  useState,
  ReactNode,
} from 'react';

// ─── Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

type Theme = 'dark' | 'light' | 'system';

interface ThemeContextType {
  theme: Theme;
  setTheme: (t: Theme) => void;
  toggleTheme: () => void;
  resolvedTheme: 'dark' | 'light'; // actual applied theme (resolves 'system')
}

// ─── Context ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | null>(null);

const STORAGE_KEY = 'app_theme';

// ─── Provider ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export const ThemeProvider = ({ children }: { children: ReactNode }) => {
  const [theme, setThemeState] = useState<Theme>(
    () => (localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY) as Theme) ?? 'dark',
  );

  // Derive the actual applied theme when 'system' is selected
  const resolvedTheme: 'dark' | 'light' =
    theme === 'system'
      ? window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches
        ? 'dark'
        : 'light'
      : theme;

  // Apply / remove .dark on <html> whenever theme changes
  useEffect(() => {
    const root = document.documentElement;

    const applyTheme = (resolved: 'dark' | 'light') => {
      root.classList.toggle('dark', resolved === 'dark');
    };

    applyTheme(resolvedTheme);

    // If 'system', also listen for OS-level changes
    if (theme === 'system') {
      const mq = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
      const handler = (e: MediaQueryListEvent) =>
        applyTheme(e.matches ? 'dark' : 'light');
      mq.addEventListener('change', handler);
      return () => mq.removeEventListener('change', handler);
    }
  }, [theme, resolvedTheme]);

  const setTheme = (t: Theme) => {
    setThemeState(t);
    localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, t);
  };

  const toggleTheme = () =>
    setTheme(resolvedTheme === 'dark' ? 'light' : 'dark');

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider
      value={{ theme, setTheme, toggleTheme, resolvedTheme }}
    >
      {children}
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
};

// ─── Hook ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export const useTheme = () => {
  const ctx = useContext(ThemeContext);
  if (!ctx) throw new Error('useTheme must be used within ThemeProvider');
  return ctx;
};

import { useState, useEffect, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';

// ── useAsync: for read operations ────────────────────────────────────────

interface AsyncState<T> {
  data: T | null;
  loading: boolean;
  error: Error | null;
  refetch: () => void;
}

export function useAsync<T>(fn: () => Promise<T>, deps: any[]): AsyncState<T> {
  const [data, setData] = useState<T | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<Error | null>(null);
  const mountedRef = useRef(true);
  const counterRef = useRef(0);

  const execute = useCallback(() => {
    const current = ++counterRef.current;
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    fn()
      .then((result) => {
        if (mountedRef.current && current === counterRef.current) {
          setData(result);
          setLoading(false);
        }
      })
      .catch((err) => {
        if (mountedRef.current && current === counterRef.current) {
          setError(
            err instanceof Error
              ? err
              : new Error(err?.message || 'Unknown error'),
          );
          setLoading(false);
        }
      });
  }, deps);

  useEffect(() => {
    mountedRef.current = true;
    execute();
    return () => {
      mountedRef.current = false;
    };
  }, [execute]);

  return { data, loading, error, refetch: execute };
}

// ── useMutation: for write operations ────────────────────────────────────

interface MutationState<T> {
  data: T | null;
  loading: boolean;
  error: Error | null;
}

interface UseMutationReturn<TArgs extends any[], TResult> {
  mutate: (...args: TArgs) => Promise<TResult>;
  state: MutationState<TResult>;
  reset: () => void;
}

export function useMutation<TArgs extends any[], TResult>(
  fn: (...args: TArgs) => Promise<TResult>,
): UseMutationReturn<TArgs, TResult> {
  const [state, setState] = useState<MutationState<TResult>>({
    data: null,
    loading: false,
    error: null,
  });

  const mutate = useCallback(
    async (...args: TArgs): Promise<TResult> => {
      setState({ data: null, loading: true, error: null });
      try {
        const result = await fn(...args);
        setState({ data: result, loading: false, error: null });
        return result;
      } catch (err: any) {
        const error =
          err instanceof Error
            ? err
            : new Error(err?.message || 'Operation failed');
        setState({ data: null, loading: false, error });
        throw error;
      }
    },
    [fn],
  );

  const reset = useCallback(() => {
    setState({ data: null, loading: false, error: null });
  }, []);

  return { mutate, state, reset };
}

import { clsx, type ClassValue } from "clsx"
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge"

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs))
}

// Animated count-up hook
const useCountUp = (end: number, duration = 2000) => {
  const [count, setCount] = useState(0);
  const ref = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  const isInView = useInView(ref, { once: true });

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isInView) return;
    let start = 0;
    const step = end / (duration / 16);
    const timer = setInterval(() => {
      start += step;
      if (start >= end) {
        setCount(end);
        clearInterval(timer);
      } else {
        setCount(Math.floor(start));
      }
    }, 16);
    return () => clearInterval(timer);
  }, [isInView, end, duration]);

  return { count, ref };
};

const StatItem = ({
  value,
  suffix,
  label,
}: {
  value: number;
  suffix: string;
  label: string;
}) => {
  const { count, ref } = useCountUp(value);
  return (
    <div ref={ref}>
      <p className='font-heading font-bold text-2xl md:text-3xl bg-gradient-to-r from-primary to-secondary bg-clip-text text-transparent'>
        {count.toLocaleString()}
        {suffix}
      </p>
      <p className='text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-1'>{label}</p>
    </div>
  );
};

import { useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useEffect } from 'react';

const NotFound = () => {
  const location = useLocation();

  useEffect(() => {
    console.error(
      '404 Error: User attempted to access non-existent route:',
      location.pathname,
    );
  }, [location.pathname]);

  return (
    <div className='flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-muted'>
      <div className='text-center'>
        <h1 className='mb-4 text-4xl font-bold'>404</h1>
        <p className='mb-4 text-xl text-muted-foreground'>
          Oops! Page not found
        </p>
        <a href='/' className='text-primary underline hover:text-primary/90'>
          Return to Home
        </a>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default NotFound;

import { useState } from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { Link, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { Zap, Loader2, Eye, EyeOff, Github } from 'lucide-react';
import { toast } from 'sonner';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { Card, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Checkbox } from '@/components/ui/checkbox';
import { ForgotPasswordModal } from '@/components/auth/ForgotPasswordModal';

import type { SignInPayload } from '@/types/auth.types';
import { useSignIn } from '@/hooks/auth/useSignIn';

// ─── Field-level validation ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

type FormErrors = Partial<Record<keyof SignInPayload, string>>;

const validateField = (
  field: keyof SignInPayload,
  value: string,
): string | undefined => {
  if (field === 'email') {
    if (!value) return 'Email is required';
    if (!/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(value)) return 'Enter a valid email';
  }
  if (field === 'password' && !value) return 'Password is required';
  return undefined;
};

// ─── Component ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const SignIn = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { mutate: signIn, isPending } = useSignIn();

  const [form, setForm] = useState<SignInPayload>({ email: '', password: '' });
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState<FormErrors>({});
  const [remember, setRemember] = useState(false);
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);
  const [shake, setShake] = useState(false);
  const [forgotOpen, setForgotOpen] = useState(false);

  const triggerShake = () => {
    setShake(true);
    setTimeout(() => setShake(false), 600);
  };

  const handleBlur = (field: keyof SignInPayload) => {
    const err = validateField(field, form[field]);
    setErrors((prev) => ({ ...prev, [field]: err }));
  };

  const handleChange = (field: keyof SignInPayload, value: string) => {
    setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, [field]: value }));
    // Clear inline error as the user types
    setErrors((prev) => ({ ...prev, [field]: undefined }));
  };

  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    // Validate all fields before submitting
    const emailErr = validateField('email', form.email);
    const passErr = validateField('password', form.password);

    if (emailErr || passErr) {
      setErrors({ email: emailErr, password: passErr });
      triggerShake();
      return;
    }

    signIn(form, {
      onSuccess: () => {
        if (remember) {
          // Token is already in localStorage via the hook's onSuccess.
          // Flag the preference so the axios interceptor can reuse it on next load.
          localStorage.setItem('rememberMe', 'true');
        }
        toast.success('Welcome back!');
        navigate('/workspaces/w1');
      },
      onError: (err) => {
        triggerShake();
        // Axios error message surfaced from the backend
        const message =
          (err as { response?: { data?: { message?: string } } }).response?.data
            ?.message ?? 'Invalid email or password';
        toast.error(message);
      },
    });
  };

  return (
    <div className='min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background px-4'>
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 24 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.4 }}
        className='w-full max-w-md'
      >
        {/* Logo */}
        <div className='text-center mb-8'>
          <button
            onClick={() => navigate('/')}
            className='inline-flex items-center gap-2.5 mb-4'
          >
            <div className='w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-secondary flex items-center justify-center shadow-md'>
              <Zap className='w-5 h-5 text-primary-foreground' />
            </div>
            <span className='font-bold text-xl tracking-tight'>Linkly</span>
          </button>
          <h1 className='text-2xl font-bold mb-1'>Welcome back</h1>
          <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
            Sign in to your account to continue
          </p>
        </div>

        <Card className='shadow-lg border-border/50'>
          <CardContent className='pt-6'>
            {/* Sign-in form */}
            <motion.form
              onSubmit={handleSubmit}
              className='space-y-4'
              animate={shake ? { x: [0, -8, 8, -8, 8, 0] } : {}}
              transition={{ duration: 0.4 }}
              noValidate
            >
              {/* Email */}
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                <Label htmlFor='email'>Email</Label>
                <Input
                  id='email'
                  type='email'
                  placeholder='you@company.com'
                  value={form.email}
                  onChange={(e) => handleChange('email', e.target.value)}
                  onBlur={() => handleBlur('email')}
                  disabled={isPending}
                  className={
                    errors.email
                      ? 'border-destructive focus-visible:ring-destructive'
                      : ''
                  }
                  autoComplete='email'
                />
                {errors.email && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>{errors.email}</p>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Password */}
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                <Label htmlFor='password'>Password</Label>
                <div className='relative'>
                  <Input
                    id='password'
                    type={showPassword ? 'text' : 'password'}
                    placeholder='••••••••'
                    value={form.password}
                    onChange={(e) => handleChange('password', e.target.value)}
                    onBlur={() => handleBlur('password')}
                    disabled={isPending}
                    className={`pr-10 ${errors.password ? 'border-destructive focus-visible:ring-destructive' : ''}`}
                    autoComplete='current-password'
                  />
                  <button
                    type='button'
                    onClick={() => setShowPassword((v) => !v)}
                    className='absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors'
                    tabIndex={-1}
                    aria-label={
                      showPassword ? 'Hide password' : 'Show password'
                    }
                  >
                    {showPassword ? (
                      <EyeOff className='w-4 h-4' />
                    ) : (
                      <Eye className='w-4 h-4' />
                    )}
                  </button>
                </div>
                {errors.password && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>{errors.password}</p>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Remember me + Forgot password */}
              <div className='flex items-center justify-between'>
                <div className='flex items-center gap-2'>
                  <Checkbox
                    id='remember'
                    checked={remember}
                    onCheckedChange={(checked) => setRemember(checked === true)}
                  />
                  <Label
                    htmlFor='remember'
                    className='text-sm font-normal text-muted-foreground cursor-pointer'
                  >
                    Remember me
                  </Label>
                </div>
                <button
                  type='button'
                  onClick={() => setForgotOpen(true)}
                  className='text-sm text-primary hover:underline'
                >
                  Forgot password?
                </button>
              </div>

              <Button className='w-full' type='submit' disabled={isPending}>
                {isPending && <Loader2 className='w-4 h-4 animate-spin mr-2' />}
                {isPending ? 'Signing in…' : 'Sign In'}
              </Button>
            </motion.form>

            {/* Divider */}
            <div className='relative my-5'>
              <div className='absolute inset-0 flex items-center'>
                <div className='w-full border-t border-border' />
              </div>
              <div className='relative flex justify-center text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                <span className='bg-card px-3'>or continue with</span>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Social buttons (UI only — wire up OAuth when ready) */}
            <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-3'>
              <Button variant='outline' className='w-full' disabled>
                <svg className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' viewBox='0 0 24 24'>
                  <path
                    d='M22.56 12.25c0-.78-.07-1.53-.2-2.25H12v4.26h5.92a5.06 5.06 0 0 1-2.2 3.32v2.77h3.57c2.08-1.92 3.28-4.74 3.28-8.1z'
                    fill='#4285F4'
                  />
                  <path
                    d='M12 23c2.97 0 5.46-.98 7.28-2.66l-3.57-2.77c-.98.66-2.23 1.06-3.71 1.06-2.86 0-5.29-1.93-6.16-4.53H2.18v2.84C3.99 20.53 7.7 23 12 23z'
                    fill='#34A853'
                  />
                  <path
                    d='M5.84 14.09c-.22-.66-.35-1.36-.35-2.09s.13-1.43.35-2.09V7.07H2.18C1.43 8.55 1 10.22 1 12s.43 3.45 1.18 4.93l2.85-2.22.81-.62z'
                    fill='#FBBC05'
                  />
                  <path
                    d='M12 5.38c1.62 0 3.06.56 4.21 1.64l3.15-3.15C17.45 2.09 14.97 1 12 1 7.7 1 3.99 3.47 2.18 7.07l3.66 2.84c.87-2.6 3.3-4.53 6.16-4.53z'
                    fill='#EA4335'
                  />
                </svg>
                Google
              </Button>
              <Button variant='outline' className='w-full' disabled>
                <Github className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
                GitHub
              </Button>
            </div>

            <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-6 text-center'>
              Don't have an account?{' '}
              <Link
                to='/signup'
                className='text-primary font-medium hover:underline'
              >
                Sign Up
              </Link>
            </p>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      </motion.div>

      <ForgotPasswordModal
        open={forgotOpen}
        onClose={() => setForgotOpen(false)}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

export default SignIn;

import { useCallback, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { motion } from 'framer-motion';
import { Check, Eye, EyeOff, Github, Loader2, X, Zap } from 'lucide-react';
import { Link, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { toast } from 'sonner';

import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { Card, CardContent } from '@/components/ui/card';
import { Checkbox } from '@/components/ui/checkbox';
import { Input } from '@/components/ui/input';
import { Label } from '@/components/ui/label';
import { PasswordStrengthMeter } from '@/components/auth/PasswordStrengthMeter';

import type { ApiErrorResponse, SignUpPayload } from '@/types/auth.types';
import { useSignUp } from '@/hooks/auth/useSignUp';

// ─── Types ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

interface FormState extends SignUpPayload {
  name: string;
  confirmPassword: string;
}

type FormErrors = Partial<Record<keyof FormState | 'agreed', string>>;
type UsernameStatus = 'idle' | 'checking' | 'available' | 'taken';

// ─── Validation ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const validateField = (
  field: keyof FormState | 'agreed',
  value: string | boolean,
  form: FormState,
): string | undefined => {
  switch (field) {
    case 'name':
      if (!String(value).trim()) return 'Name is required';
      break;
    case 'username':
      if (!String(value).trim()) return 'Username is required';
      if (String(value).length < 3) return 'At least 3 characters';
      break;
    case 'email':
      if (!value) return 'Email is required';
      if (!/^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(String(value)))
        return 'Enter a valid email';
      break;
    case 'password':
      if (!value) return 'Password is required';
      if (String(value).length < 6) return 'At least 6 characters';
      break;
    case 'confirmPassword':
      if (String(value) !== form.password) return "Passwords don't match";
      break;
    case 'agreed':
      if (!value) return 'You must agree to the terms';
      break;
  }
  return undefined;
};

const validateAll = (form: FormState, agreed: boolean): FormErrors => {
  const errors: FormErrors = {};
  (
    [
      'name',
      'username',
      'email',
      'password',
      'confirmPassword',
    ] as (keyof FormState)[]
  ).forEach((field) => {
    const err = validateField(field, form[field], form);
    if (err) errors[field] = err;
  });
  const agreedErr = validateField('agreed', agreed, form);
  if (agreedErr) errors.agreed = agreedErr;
  return errors;
};

// ─── Username suggestions ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const buildSuggestions = (name: string): string[] => {
  const parts = name.toLowerCase().trim().split(/\s+/);
  const suggestions =
    parts.length >= 2
      ? [
          `${parts[0][0]}${parts[parts.length - 1]}`,
          `${parts[0]}.${parts[parts.length - 1]}`,
          `${parts[0][0]}${parts[parts.length - 1]}${Math.floor(Math.random() * 99)}`,
        ]
      : [parts[0], `${parts[0]}${Math.floor(Math.random() * 99)}`];
  return suggestions.map((s) => s.replace(/[^a-z0-9._]/g, ''));
};

// ─── Component ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const SignUp = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { mutate: signUp, isPending } = useSignUp();

  const [form, setForm] = useState<FormState>({
    name: '',
    username: '',
    email: '',
    password: '',
    confirmPassword: '',
  });
  const [agreed, setAgreed] = useState(false);
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState<FormErrors>({});
  const [showPassword, setShowPassword] = useState(false);
  const [usernameStatus, setUsernameStatus] = useState<UsernameStatus>('idle');
  const [suggestions, setSuggestions] = useState<string[]>([]);

  // ── Username suggestions from full name ──────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (form.name.trim().length > 1) {
      setSuggestions(buildSuggestions(form.name));
    } else {
      setSuggestions([]);
    }
  }, [form.name]);

  // ── Debounced username availability check ────────────────────────────────
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!form.username || form.username.length < 2) {
      setUsernameStatus('idle');
      return;
    }
    setUsernameStatus('checking');
    const timer = setTimeout(async () => {
      // TODO: replace with real API call — e.g. checkUsernameRequest(form.username)
      setUsernameStatus('available');
    }, 400);
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, [form.username]);

  // ── Field helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const setField = useCallback(
    <K extends keyof FormState>(key: K, value: FormState[K]) => {
      setForm((prev) => ({ ...prev, [key]: value }));
      setErrors((prev) => ({ ...prev, [key]: undefined }));
    },
    [],
  );

  const handleBlur = useCallback(
    (field: keyof FormState) => {
      const err = validateField(field, form[field], form);
      setErrors((prev) => ({ ...prev, [field]: err }));
    },
    [form],
  );

  // ── Submit ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    const validationErrors = validateAll(form, agreed);
    if (Object.keys(validationErrors).length > 0) {
      setErrors(validationErrors);
      return;
    }

    // Strip UI-only fields before sending to the API
    const { name: _name, confirmPassword: _confirm, ...payload } = form;

    signUp(payload, {
      onSuccess: () => {
        toast.success('Account created! Please sign in. 🎉');
        navigate('/signin');
      },
      onError: (err) => {
        const apiError = err as unknown as ApiErrorResponse;
        toast.error(apiError?.message ?? 'Sign up failed. Please try again.');
      },
    });
  };

  // ─── Render ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  return (
    <div className='min-h-screen flex items-center justify-center bg-background px-4 py-8'>
      <motion.div
        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 24 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        transition={{ duration: 0.4 }}
        className='w-full max-w-md'
      >
        {/* Logo */}
        <div className='text-center mb-8'>
          <button
            onClick={() => navigate('/')}
            className='inline-flex items-center gap-2.5 mb-4'
          >
            <div className='w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-gradient-to-br from-primary to-secondary flex items-center justify-center shadow-md'>
              <Zap className='w-5 h-5 text-primary-foreground' />
            </div>
            <span className='font-bold text-xl tracking-tight'>Linkly</span>
          </button>
          <h1 className='text-2xl font-bold mb-1'>Create your account</h1>
          <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground'>
            Get started with Linkly for free
          </p>
        </div>

        <Card className='shadow-lg border-border/50'>
          <CardContent className='pt-6'>
            <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className='space-y-4' noValidate>
              {/* Full Name */}
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                <Label htmlFor='name'>Full name</Label>
                <Input
                  id='name'
                  type='text'
                  placeholder='Alex Chen'
                  value={form.name}
                  onChange={(e) => setField('name', e.target.value)}
                  onBlur={() => handleBlur('name')}
                  disabled={isPending}
                  autoComplete='name'
                  className={
                    errors.name
                      ? 'border-destructive focus-visible:ring-destructive'
                      : ''
                  }
                />
                {errors.name && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>{errors.name}</p>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Username */}
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                <Label htmlFor='username'>Username</Label>
                <div className='relative'>
                  <Input
                    id='username'
                    type='text'
                    placeholder='alexchen'
                    value={form.username}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setField(
                        'username',
                        e.target.value
                          .toLowerCase()
                          .replace(/[^a-z0-9._]/g, ''),
                      )
                    }
                    onBlur={() => handleBlur('username')}
                    disabled={isPending}
                    autoComplete='username'
                    className={`pr-10 ${
                      errors.username
                        ? 'border-destructive focus-visible:ring-destructive'
                        : usernameStatus === 'taken'
                          ? 'border-destructive'
                          : usernameStatus === 'available'
                            ? 'border-green-500'
                            : ''
                    }`}
                  />
                  <div className='absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2'>
                    {usernameStatus === 'checking' && (
                      <Loader2 className='w-4 h-4 animate-spin text-muted-foreground' />
                    )}
                    {usernameStatus === 'available' && (
                      <Check className='w-4 h-4 text-green-500' />
                    )}
                    {usernameStatus === 'taken' && (
                      <X className='w-4 h-4 text-destructive' />
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>

                {usernameStatus === 'available' && !errors.username && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-green-500'>✓ Available</p>
                )}
                {usernameStatus === 'taken' && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>✗ Username taken</p>
                )}
                {errors.username && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>{errors.username}</p>
                )}

                {/* Suggestions shown only when field is empty */}
                {suggestions.length > 0 && !form.username && (
                  <div className='flex gap-1.5 flex-wrap'>
                    {suggestions.map((s) => (
                      <button
                        key={s}
                        type='button'
                        onClick={() => setField('username', s)}
                        className='text-xs px-2.5 py-1 rounded-full bg-muted text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground hover:bg-accent transition-colors'
                      >
                        {s}
                      </button>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Email */}
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                <Label htmlFor='email'>Email</Label>
                <Input
                  id='email'
                  type='email'
                  placeholder='you@company.com'
                  value={form.email}
                  onChange={(e) => setField('email', e.target.value)}
                  onBlur={() => handleBlur('email')}
                  disabled={isPending}
                  autoComplete='email'
                  className={
                    errors.email
                      ? 'border-destructive focus-visible:ring-destructive'
                      : ''
                  }
                />
                {errors.email && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>{errors.email}</p>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Password */}
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                <Label htmlFor='password'>Password</Label>
                <div className='relative'>
                  <Input
                    id='password'
                    type={showPassword ? 'text' : 'password'}
                    placeholder='••••••••'
                    value={form.password}
                    onChange={(e) => setField('password', e.target.value)}
                    onBlur={() => handleBlur('password')}
                    disabled={isPending}
                    autoComplete='new-password'
                    className={`pr-10 ${errors.password ? 'border-destructive focus-visible:ring-destructive' : ''}`}
                  />
                  <button
                    type='button'
                    onClick={() => setShowPassword((v) => !v)}
                    className='absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground transition-colors'
                    tabIndex={-1}
                    aria-label={
                      showPassword ? 'Hide password' : 'Show password'
                    }
                  >
                    {showPassword ? (
                      <EyeOff className='w-4 h-4' />
                    ) : (
                      <Eye className='w-4 h-4' />
                    )}
                  </button>
                </div>
                <PasswordStrengthMeter password={form.password} />
                {errors.password && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>{errors.password}</p>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Confirm Password */}
              <div className='space-y-2'>
                <Label htmlFor='confirmPassword'>Confirm password</Label>
                <div className='relative'>
                  <Input
                    id='confirmPassword'
                    type='password'
                    placeholder='••••••••'
                    value={form.confirmPassword}
                    onChange={(e) =>
                      setField('confirmPassword', e.target.value)
                    }
                    onBlur={() => handleBlur('confirmPassword')}
                    disabled={isPending}
                    autoComplete='new-password'
                    className={`pr-10 ${
                      errors.confirmPassword
                        ? 'border-destructive focus-visible:ring-destructive'
                        : form.confirmPassword &&
                            form.password === form.confirmPassword
                          ? 'border-green-500'
                          : ''
                    }`}
                  />
                  {form.confirmPassword &&
                    form.password === form.confirmPassword && (
                      <Check className='absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-green-500' />
                    )}
                </div>
                {errors.confirmPassword && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive'>
                    {errors.confirmPassword}
                  </p>
                )}
              </div>

              {/* Terms */}
              <div className='space-y-1'>
                <div className='flex items-start gap-2'>
                  <Checkbox
                    id='terms'
                    checked={agreed}
                    onCheckedChange={(checked) => {
                      setAgreed(checked === true);
                      setErrors((p) => ({ ...p, agreed: undefined }));
                    }}
                    className='mt-0.5'
                  />
                  <Label
                    htmlFor='terms'
                    className='text-sm font-normal text-muted-foreground leading-snug cursor-pointer'
                  >
                    I agree to the Terms of Service and Privacy Policy
                  </Label>
                </div>
                {errors.agreed && (
                  <p className='text-xs text-destructive pl-6'>
                    {errors.agreed}
                  </p>
                )}
              </div>

              <Button
                type='submit'
                className='w-full'
                disabled={
                  isPending || !form.name || !form.email || !form.password
                }
              >
                {isPending && <Loader2 className='w-4 h-4 animate-spin mr-2' />}
                {isPending ? 'Creating account…' : 'Create Account'}
              </Button>
            </form>

            {/* Divider */}
            <div className='relative my-5'>
              <div className='absolute inset-0 flex items-center'>
                <div className='w-full border-t border-border' />
              </div>
              <div className='relative flex justify-center text-xs text-muted-foreground'>
                <span className='bg-card px-3'>or continue with</span>
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* Social — UI only until OAuth is wired up */}
            <div className='grid grid-cols-2 gap-3'>
              <Button variant='outline' className='w-full' disabled>
                <svg className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' viewBox='0 0 24 24'>
                  <path
                    d='M22.56 12.25c0-.78-.07-1.53-.2-2.25H12v4.26h5.92a5.06 5.06 0 0 1-2.2 3.32v2.77h3.57c2.08-1.92 3.28-4.74 3.28-8.1z'
                    fill='#4285F4'
                  />
                  <path
                    d='M12 23c2.97 0 5.46-.98 7.28-2.66l-3.57-2.77c-.98.66-2.23 1.06-3.71 1.06-2.86 0-5.29-1.93-6.16-4.53H2.18v2.84C3.99 20.53 7.7 23 12 23z'
                    fill='#34A853'
                  />
                  <path
                    d='M5.84 14.09c-.22-.66-.35-1.36-.35-2.09s.13-1.43.35-2.09V7.07H2.18C1.43 8.55 1 10.22 1 12s.43 3.45 1.18 4.93l2.85-2.22.81-.62z'
                    fill='#FBBC05'
                  />
                  <path
                    d='M12 5.38c1.62 0 3.06.56 4.21 1.64l3.15-3.15C17.45 2.09 14.97 1 12 1 7.7 1 3.99 3.47 2.18 7.07l3.66 2.84c.87-2.6 3.3-4.53 6.16-4.53z'
                    fill='#EA4335'
                  />
                </svg>
                Google
              </Button>
              <Button variant='outline' className='w-full' disabled>
                <Github className='w-4 h-4 mr-2' />
                GitHub
              </Button>
            </div>

            <p className='text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-6 text-center'>
              Already have an account?{' '}
              <Link
                to='/signin'
                className='text-primary font-medium hover:underline'
              >
                Sign in
              </Link>
            </p>
          </CardContent>
        </Card>
      </motion.div>
    </div>
  );
};

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { Menu } from 'lucide-react';
import { useUI } from '@/context/useUI';
import { useAppSelector } from '@/app/hooks';

import { useSendMessage } from '@/hooks/messages/useSendMessage';

import { WorkspaceSidebar } from '@/components/workspace/WorkspaceSidebar';
import { ChannelView } from '@/components/workspace/ChannelView';
import { DMView } from '@/components/workspace/DMView';
import { ThreadPanel } from '@/components/workspace/ThreadPanel';
import { ProfilePanel } from '@/components/workspace/ProfilePanel';
import { PinnedMessagesPanel } from '@/components/workspace/PinnedMessagesPanel';
import { MembersPanel } from '@/components/workspace/MembersPanel';
import { SavedItemsPanel } from '@/components/workspace/SavedItemsPanel';
import { DocsPanel } from '@/components/workspace/DocsPanel';
import { CalendarPanel } from '@/components/workspace/CalendarPanel';
import { AnalyticsDashboard } from '@/components/workspace/AnalyticsDashboard';
import { GoalsPanel } from '@/components/workspace/GoalsPanel';
import { CanvasPanel } from '@/components/workspace/CanvasPanel';
import { MoodCheckIn } from '@/components/workspace/MoodCheckIn';
import { SearchModal } from '@/components/modals/SearchModal';
import { CreateChannelModal } from '@/components/modals/CreateChannelModal';
import { CreateWorkspaceModal } from '@/components/modals/CreateWorkspaceModal';
import { WorkspaceSwitcher } from '@/components/modals/WorkspaceSwitcher';
import { SettingsModal } from '@/components/modals/SettingsModal';
import { ConfettiOverlay } from '@/components/ConfettiOverlay';
import { ProfilePage } from '@/components/profile/ProfilePage';
import { BrowseChannelsModal } from '@/components/modals/BrowseChannelsModal';

import { ActivityPanel } from '@/components/workspace/ActivityPanel';

// ─── Skeleton ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const SkeletonLoader = () => (
  <div className='flex h-screen bg-background'>
    <div className='w-[260px] bg-sidebar border-r border-sidebar-border p-4 space-y-4 hidden md:block'>
      <div className='h-10 bg-muted rounded-lg animate-shimmer' />
      <div className='h-8 bg-muted rounded-md animate-shimmer' />
      <div className='space-y-2 mt-4'>
        {Array.from({ length: 6 }).map((_, i) => (
          <div
            key={i}
            className='h-7 bg-muted rounded-md animate-shimmer'
            style={{ animationDelay: `${i * 0.1}s` }}
          />
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
    <div className='flex-1 p-4 space-y-4'>
      <div className='h-12 bg-muted rounded-lg animate-shimmer' />
      <div className='space-y-4 mt-8'>
        {Array.from({ length: 5 }).map((_, i) => (
          <div key={i} className='flex gap-3'>
            <div className='w-9 h-9 rounded-full bg-muted animate-shimmer shrink-0' />
            <div className='flex-1 space-y-2'>
              <div className='h-4 bg-muted rounded w-32 animate-shimmer' />
              <div className='h-4 bg-muted rounded w-3/4 animate-shimmer' />
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
);

// ─── Modals (extracted to avoid repetition in two render paths) ───────────────

const SharedModals = ({
  browseChannelsOpen,
  onCloseBrowseChannels,
}: {
  browseChannelsOpen: boolean;
  onCloseBrowseChannels: () => void;
}) => (
  <>
    <SearchModal />
    <CreateChannelModal />
    <CreateWorkspaceModal />
    <WorkspaceSwitcher />
    <SettingsModal />
    <BrowseChannelsModal
      open={browseChannelsOpen}
      onClose={onCloseBrowseChannels}
    />
  </>
);

// ─── WorkspacePage ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

const WorkspacePage = () => {
  // ── UI state from UIContext ──────────────────────────────────────────────
  const {
    sidebarOpen,
    setSidebarOpen,
    rightPanel,
    setRightPanel,
    isMobile,
    workspaceView,
    setWorkspaceView,
  } = useUI();

  // ── Navigation state from Redux ──────────────────────────────────────────
  const currentChannelId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentChannelId);
  const currentDMId = useAppSelector((s) => s.channel.currentDMId);

  // ── Server data from TanStack Query ─────────────────────────────────────
  // currentChannel object — comes from the channels query cache
  // We only need the name here for the mobile header; ChannelView fetches its own data
  const { data: channels = [] } = useGetChannels();
  const currentChannel =
    channels.find((c) => c.id === currentChannelId) ?? null;

  // sendMessage — used only for canvas share and docs share
  const { mutate: sendMessage } = useSendMessage();

  // ── Local state ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [fullProfileUserId, setFullProfileUserId] = useState<string | null>(
    null,
  );
  const [browseChannelsOpen, setBrowseChannelsOpen] = useState(false);
  const [canvasOpen, setCanvasOpen] = useState(false);

  // ── Effects ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  useEffect(() => {
    const timer = setTimeout(() => setLoading(false), 800);
    return () => clearTimeout(timer);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handler = () => setBrowseChannelsOpen(true);
    window.addEventListener('open-browse-channels', handler);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('open-browse-channels', handler);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    const canvasHandler = () => setCanvasOpen(true);
    const docsHandler = () => setRightPanel('docs');
    const calendarHandler = () => setRightPanel('calendar');
    const goalsHandler = () => setWorkspaceView('goals');

    window.addEventListener('open-canvas', canvasHandler);
    window.addEventListener('open-docs', docsHandler);
    window.addEventListener('open-calendar', calendarHandler);
    window.addEventListener('open-goals', goalsHandler);

    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('open-canvas', canvasHandler);
      window.removeEventListener('open-docs', docsHandler);
      window.removeEventListener('open-calendar', calendarHandler);
      window.removeEventListener('open-goals', goalsHandler);
    };
  }, [setRightPanel, setWorkspaceView]);

  // ── Handlers ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  const handleCanvasShare = () => {
    sendMessage({
      content: '🎨 *Shared a canvas drawing*\n📎 canvas-snapshot.png',
    });
    setCanvasOpen(false);
  };

  const handleDocsShare = (text: string) => {
    sendMessage({ content: text });
    setRightPanel(null);
  };

  // ── Mobile header label ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

  const mobileHeaderLabel = () => {
    if (workspaceView === 'analytics') return 'Analytics';
    if (workspaceView === 'goals') return 'Goals';
    if (currentChannel) return `#${currentChannel.name}`;
    if (currentDMId) return 'Direct Message';
    return 'Linkly';
  };

  // ── Main content ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  const renderMainContent = () => {
    switch (workspaceView) {
      case 'analytics':
        return <AnalyticsDashboard onBack={() => setWorkspaceView('chat')} />;
      case 'goals':
        return <GoalsPanel onBack={() => setWorkspaceView('chat')} />;
      default:
        return (
          <>
            <MoodCheckIn />
            {currentDMId ? <DMView /> : <ChannelView />}
          </>
        );
    }
  };

  // ── Sidebar (shared between both render paths) ────────────────────────────

  const renderSidebar = () => (
    <AnimatePresence>
      {(sidebarOpen || !isMobile) && (
        <motion.div
          initial={isMobile ? { x: -260 } : false}
          animate={{ x: 0 }}
          exit={{ x: -260 }}
          className={`${isMobile ? 'fixed left-0 top-0 z-40 h-full' : 'relative'} w-[260px] shrink-0`}
        >
          <WorkspaceSidebar />
        </motion.div>
      )}
    </AnimatePresence>
  );

  // ── Loading ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  if (loading) return <SkeletonLoader />;

  // ── Full profile page view ────────────────────────────────────────────────

  if (fullProfileUserId) {
    return (
      <div className='flex h-screen bg-background overflow-hidden'>
        <ConfettiOverlay />
        {renderSidebar()}
        <div className='flex-1 flex flex-col min-w-0'>
          <ProfilePage
            userId={fullProfileUserId}
            onBack={() => setFullProfileUserId(null)}
          />
        </div>
        <SharedModals
          browseChannelsOpen={browseChannelsOpen}
          onCloseBrowseChannels={() => setBrowseChannelsOpen(false)}
        />
      </div>
    );
  }

  // ── Main workspace view ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

  return (
    <div
      className={`flex h-screen bg-background overflow-hidden ${isMobile ? 'pb-14' : ''}`}
    >
      <ConfettiOverlay />

      {/* Canvas overlay */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {canvasOpen && (
          <CanvasPanel
            onClose={() => setCanvasOpen(false)}
            onShareToChannel={handleCanvasShare}
          />
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>

      {/* Mobile sidebar backdrop */}
      {isMobile && sidebarOpen && (
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
          exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
          className='fixed inset-0 bg-background/60 z-30'
          onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(false)}
        />
      )}

      {renderSidebar()}

      {/* Main content area */}
      <div className='flex-1 flex flex-col min-w-0'>
        {/* Mobile top bar */}
        {isMobile && (
          <div className='flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 border-b border-border bg-background'>
            <button
              onClick={() => setSidebarOpen(true)}
              className='p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-accent'
            >
              <Menu className='w-5 h-5' />
            </button>
            <span className='font-heading font-bold text-sm truncate'>
              {mobileHeaderLabel()}
            </span>
          </div>
        )}
        {renderMainContent()}
      </div>

      {/* Right panels */}
      <AnimatePresence>
        {rightPanel && (
          <div
            className={`${isMobile ? 'fixed right-0 top-0 z-40 h-full' : 'relative'} w-[320px] shrink-0`}
          >
            {rightPanel === 'thread' && <ThreadPanel />}
            {rightPanel === 'profile' && (
              <ProfilePanel
                onViewFullProfile={(id) => setFullProfileUserId(id)}
              />
            )}
            {rightPanel === 'activity' && <ActivityPanel />}
            {rightPanel === 'pinned' && <PinnedMessagesPanel />}
            {rightPanel === 'members' && (
              <MembersPanel onViewProfile={(id) => setFullProfileUserId(id)} />
            )}
            {rightPanel === 'saved' && <SavedItemsPanel />}
            {rightPanel === 'docs' && (
              <DocsPanel
                onClose={() => setRightPanel(null)}
                onShareToChannel={handleDocsShare}
              />
            )}
            {rightPanel === 'calendar' && (
              <CalendarPanel onClose={() => setRightPanel(null)} />
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </AnimatePresence>

      <SharedModals
        browseChannelsOpen={browseChannelsOpen}
        onCloseBrowseChannels={() => setBrowseChannelsOpen(false)}
      />

      {isMobile && <MobileBottomNav />}
    </div>
  );
};

export default WorkspacePage;

import type { AxiosError } from 'axios';


import type {
  ApiErrorResponse,
  ApiSuccessResponse,
  AuthUser,
  SignInPayload,
  SignUpPayload,
  User,
} from '@/types/auth.types';
import axiosInstance from '@/config/axiosInstance';

// ─── Error Helper ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/**
 * Extracts a normalised error from an Axios error and re-throws it.
 * Throws the server's error body if present, otherwise a generic fallback.
 * The `never` return type lets TypeScript know this always throws,
 * so callers don't need a dummy return after calling it.
 */
const extractError = (error: unknown): never => {
  const err = error as AxiosError<ApiErrorResponse>;
  throw (
    err.response?.data ?? { success: false, message: 'Something went wrong' }
  );
};

// ─── Auth Service ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/**
 * POST /users/signup
 * Registers a new user. Does NOT sign them in automatically.
 * Returns the created user (no token).
 */
export const signUpRequest = async (payload: SignUpPayload): Promise<User> => {
  try {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.post<ApiSuccessResponse<User>>(
      '/users/signup',
      payload,
    );
    return data.data;
  } catch (error) {
    return extractError(error);
  }
};

/**
 * POST /users/signin
 * Authenticates the user and returns user data + JWT token.
 */
export const signInRequest = async (
  payload: SignInPayload,
): Promise<AuthUser> => {
  try {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.post<ApiSuccessResponse<AuthUser>>(
      '/users/signin',
      payload,
    );
    return data.data;
  } catch (error) {
    return extractError(error);
  }
};

/**
 * POST /users/signout
 * Clears the httpOnly cookie on the server side.
 */
export const signOutRequest = async (): Promise<void> => {
  try {
    await axiosInstance.post('/users/signout');
  } catch (error) {
    return extractError(error);
  }
};

import { ApiSuccessResponse, ImageKitAuthParams, Message } from '@/types';
import axiosInstance from './axiosInstance';

export const messageApi = {
  /** GET /messages/:channelId?page=1&limit=20 */
  getByChannel: async (
    channelId: string,
    page = 1,
    limit = 20
  ): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Message[]>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.get<ApiSuccessResponse<Message[]>>(
      `/messages/${channelId}`,
      { params: { page, limit } }
    );
    return data;
  },

  /**
   * GET /messages/imagekit-auth
   * Returns signed auth params for direct client-side uploads to ImageKit.
   */
  getImageKitAuthParams: async (): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<ImageKitAuthParams>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.get<ApiSuccessResponse<ImageKitAuthParams>>(
      '/messages/imagekit-auth'
    );
    return data;
  }
};

import {
  AddChannelPayload,
  AddMemberPayload,
  ApiSuccessResponse,
  CreateWorkspacePayload,
  JoinWorkspacePayload,
  UpdateWorkspacePayload,
  Workspace
} from '@/types';
import axiosInstance from './axiosInstance';

export const workspaceApi = {
  /** GET /workspaces — all workspaces the user is a member of */
  getAll: async (): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace[]>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.get<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace[]>>('/workspaces');
    return data;
  },

  /** GET /workspaces/:id */
  getById: async (workspaceId: string): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.get<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>>(
      `/workspaces/${workspaceId}`
    );
    return data;
  },

  /** GET /workspaces/join/:joinCode */
  getByJoinCode: async (joinCode: string): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.get<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>>(
      `/workspaces/join/${joinCode}`
    );
    return data;
  },

  /** POST /workspaces */
  create: async (payload: CreateWorkspacePayload): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.post<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>>(
      '/workspaces',
      payload
    );
    return data;
  },

  /** PUT /workspaces/:id */
  update: async (
    workspaceId: string,
    payload: UpdateWorkspacePayload
  ): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.put<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>>(
      `/workspaces/${workspaceId}`,
      payload
    );
    return data;
  },

  /** DELETE /workspaces/:id */
  remove: async (workspaceId: string): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<null>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.delete<ApiSuccessResponse<null>>(
      `/workspaces/${workspaceId}`
    );
    return data;
  },

  /** PUT /workspaces/:id/members */
  addMember: async (
    workspaceId: string,
    payload: AddMemberPayload
  ): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.put<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>>(
      `/workspaces/${workspaceId}/members`,
      payload
    );
    return data;
  },

  /** PUT /workspaces/:id/channels */
  addChannel: async (
    workspaceId: string,
    payload: AddChannelPayload
  ): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.put<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>>(
      `/workspaces/${workspaceId}/channels`,
      payload
    );
    return data;
  },

  /** PUT /workspaces/:id/joinCode/reset */
  resetJoinCode: async (workspaceId: string): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.put<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>>(
      `/workspaces/${workspaceId}/joinCode/reset`
    );
    return data;
  },

  /** PUT /workspaces/:id/join */
  join: async (
    workspaceId: string,
    payload: JoinWorkspacePayload
  ): Promise<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>> => {
    const { data } = await axiosInstance.put<ApiSuccessResponse<Workspace>>(
      `/workspaces/${workspaceId}/join`,
      payload
    );
    return data;
  }
};

FILE: E:\My Projects\Slack Clone\Slack-Frontend-New\src\socket\socketManager.ts
==============================

import { io, Socket } from 'socket.io-client';

const SOCKET_URL =
  (import.meta.env.VITE_SOCKET_URL as string | undefined) ?? 'http://localhost:3000';

/**
 * Singleton Socket.IO manager.
 *
 * Keeps a single socket instance alive for the app's lifetime.
 * Components interact with sockets exclusively via this manager + useSocket hook
 * — never instantiate `io()` directly in components.
 */
class SocketManager {
  private socket: Socket | null = null;

  connect(token: string): Socket {
    if (this.socket?.connected) return this.socket;

    this.socket = io(SOCKET_URL, {
      auth: { token },
      transports: ['websocket'],
      reconnectionAttempts: 5,
      reconnectionDelay: 2000,
      withCredentials: true
    });

    this.socket.on('connect_error', (err) => {
      console.error('[Socket] Connection error:', err.message);
    });

    return this.socket;
  }

  disconnect(): void {
    if (this.socket) {
      this.socket.disconnect();
      this.socket = null;
    }
  }

  getSocket(): Socket | null {
    return this.socket;
  }

  joinChannel(channelId: string): void {
    this.socket?.emit('JoinChannel', { channelId }, (res: { success: boolean; message: string }) => {
      if (res.success) {
        console.info(`[Socket] Joined channel: ${channelId}`);
      }
    });
  }

  leaveChannel(channelId: string): void {
    this.socket?.emit('LeaveChannel', { channelId });
  }

  sendMessage(data: {
    body: string;
    image?: string;
    channelId: string;
    senderId: string;
    workspaceId: string;
  }): void {
    this.socket?.emit('NewMessage', data, (res: { success: boolean; message: string }) => {
      if (!res.success) {
        console.error('[Socket] Failed to send message:', res.message);
      }
    });
  }
}

// Export singleton
export const socketManager = new SocketManager();

// ─── Request Payloads ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface SignUpPayload {
  email: string;
  username: string;
  password: string;
}

export interface SignInPayload {
  email: string;
  password: string;
}

// ─── Response Shapes ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/** Returned from POST /users/signup (no token yet — user must verify email) */
export interface User {
  _id: string;
  username: string;
  email: string;
  avatar?: string;
  isVerified: boolean;
}

/** Returned from POST /users/signin (includes JWT) */
export interface AuthUser {
  _id: string;
  username: string;
  email: string;
  avatar?: string;
  token: string;
}

// ─── Redux Auth State ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface AuthState {
  user: AuthUser | null;
  token: string | null;
}

// ─── API Response wrapper ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface ApiSuccessResponse<T> {
  success: true;
  message: string;
  data: T;
  err: Record<string, unknown>;
}

export interface ApiErrorResponse {
  success: false;
  message: string;
  data: Record<string, unknown>;
  err: unknown;
}

// ─── API Response Shape ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface ApiSuccessResponse<T = unknown> {
  success: true;
  statusCode: number;
  message: string;
  data: T;
}

export interface ApiErrorResponse {
  success: false;
  statusCode: number;
  message: string;
  errors: string[];
  data: null;
}

export type ApiResponse<T = unknown> = ApiSuccessResponse<T> | ApiErrorResponse;

// ─── User ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface User {
  _id: string;
  email: string;
  username: string;
  avatar?: string;
  isVerified: boolean;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
}

export interface AuthUser extends User {
  token: string;
}

export interface SignUpPayload {
  email: string;
  username: string;
  password: string;
}

export interface SignInPayload {
  email: string;
  password: string;
}

// ─── Workspace ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface WorkspaceMember {
  memberId: User;
  role: 'admin' | 'member';
}

export interface Channel {
  _id: string;
  name: string;
  workspaceId: string;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
}

export interface Workspace {
  _id: string;
  name: string;
  description?: string;
  members: WorkspaceMember[];
  joinCode: string;
  channels: Channel[];
  createdAt?: string;
  updatedAt?: string;
}

export interface CreateWorkspacePayload {
  name: string;
  description?: string;
}

export interface UpdateWorkspacePayload {
  name?: string;
  description?: string;
}

export interface AddMemberPayload {
  memberId: string;
  role?: 'admin' | 'member';
}

export interface AddChannelPayload {
  channelName: string;
}

export interface JoinWorkspacePayload {
  joinCode: string;
}

// ─── Channel ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface ChannelWithMessages extends Channel {
  workspaceId: string | Workspace;
  messages: Message[];
}

// ─── Message ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface MessageSender {
  _id: string;
  username: string;
  email: string;
  avatar?: string;
}

export interface Message {
  _id: string;
  body: string;
  image?: string;
  channelId: string;
  senderId: MessageSender;
  workspaceId: string;
  createdAt: string;
  updatedAt: string;
}

export interface CreateMessagePayload {
  body: string;
  image?: string;
  channelId: string;
  senderId: string;
  workspaceId: string;
}

// ─── ImageKit ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export interface ImageKitAuthParams {
  token: string;
  expire: number;
  signature: string;
}

// ─── Redux State Slices ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

export type LoadingState = 'idle' | 'loading' | 'succeeded' | 'failed';

export interface AuthState {
  user: AuthUser | null;
  token: string | null;
  loading: LoadingState;
  error: string | null;
}

export interface WorkspaceState {
  workspaces: Workspace[];
  currentWorkspace: Workspace | null;
  loading: LoadingState;
  error: string | null;
}

export interface ChannelState {
  currentChannel: ChannelWithMessages | null;
  loading: LoadingState;
  error: string | null;
}

export interface MessageState {
  messages: Message[];
  loading: LoadingState;
  error: string | null;
  sendingMessage: boolean;
}

export interface SocketState {
  connected: boolean;
  currentChannelId: string | null;
}

import type { Locale } from "@/lib/i18n";

export type RightPanel =
  | 'thread'
  | 'profile'
  | 'activity'
  | 'pinned'
  | 'members'
  | 'saved'
  | 'docs'
  | 'calendar'
  | null;

export type WorkspaceView = 'chat' | 'analytics' | 'goals' | 'canvas';

export interface UIContextType {
  sidebarOpen: boolean;
  setSidebarOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
  toggleSidebar: () => void;
  rightPanel: RightPanel;
  setRightPanel: (p: RightPanel) => void;
  threadParentId: string | null;
  openThread: (messageId: string) => void;
  closeThread: () => void;
  profileUserId: string | null;
  openProfile: (userId: string) => void;
  closeProfile: () => void;
  searchOpen: boolean;
  setSearchOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
  settingsOpen: boolean;
  setSettingsOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
  createChannelOpen: boolean;
  setCreateChannelOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
  createWorkspaceOpen: boolean;
  setCreateWorkspaceOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
  workspaceSwitcherOpen: boolean;
  setWorkspaceSwitcherOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
  shortcutsOpen: boolean;
  setShortcutsOpen: (open: boolean) => void;
  soundEnabled: boolean;
  toggleSound: () => void;
  isMobile: boolean;
  showConfetti: boolean;
  triggerConfetti: () => void;
  workspaceView: WorkspaceView;
  setWorkspaceView: (v: WorkspaceView) => void;
  locale: Locale;
  setLocale: (l: Locale) => void;
}
